CREATE OR REPLACE PACKAGE BODY SETTLESUP Is
  currentdate      Date;
  currentmkt       Varchar2(20);
  currentmkttype   Char(1);
  ChargeDeductMode Varchar2(20);
  AdjQsChargeId    Varchar2(20);
  b_sb             supplierbase%Rowtype;
  b_cont           contmain%Rowtype;
  b_hd             supsettlehead%Rowtype;
  b_detrow         supsettledet%Rowtype;
  b_dettemp        supsettledet%Rowtype;
  b_dettot         supsettledet%Rowtype;
  b_dettemptot     supsettledet%Rowtype;
  b_scds           salecostday_set%Rowtype;
  --b_cscharge contsupcharge%ROWTYPE;
  b_rowno     Integer := 0;
  b_firstset  Char(1) := 'N';
  b_ce        tcelist := tcelist(); --超额基数
  b_celist    CeRecList := CeRecList();
  b_isqs      Char(1) := '0'; -- 0 结算 / 1 清算
  b_ispop     Char(1) := '0';
  b_popbillno Varchar2(20);
  b_bdtype    Char(1);
  --保底日期段
  b_bd bdlist := bdlist();
  --清算日期段
  b_qs qslist := qslist();
  --联合合同保底
  b_unioncontno Varchar2(15);
  --清算目标指标
  b_qsvalue    qsvalue;
  b_CreditMode Char(1) := fgetprivatepara('S1');
  b_NullBill   Char(1) := fgetPrivatePara('S2');
  b_DateType   Char(1) := fGetPrivatePara('S3');
  b_AllowNeg   Char(1) := fGetPrivatePara('S4');
  Function fround(pnum In Number, p_point In Number Default 0.01)
    Return Number Is
    l_point Integer;
    l_ret   Number;
  Begin
    If p_point Is Null Then
      l_point := 0.01;
    End If;
    Select decode(p_point,
                  0.01,
                  2,
                  --分
                  0.1,
                  1,
                  --角
                  1,
                  0,
                  --元
                  10,
                  -1,
                  --十元
                  100,
                  -2) --百元
      Into l_point
      From dual;
    l_ret := round(pnum, l_point);
    /*
    SELECT round(1234.58, 2) a1, round(1234.58, 1) a2,
       round(1234.58, 0) a3, round(1234.58, -1) a4, round(1234.58, -2) a4 FROM dual
    result
    A1      A2      A3    A4    A4
    1234.58  1234.6  1235  1230  1200
    */
    Return l_ret;
  End;
  --
  Function getchargetype(vid In Char) Return Char Is
    ltype Char(1);
  Begin
    Begin
      Select ccdeftype Into ltype From codecharge Where cccode = vid;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        ltype := '1';
    End;
    Return ltype;
  End;

  Function getmoney(i_money In number, i_min In number, i_max In number)
    Return number Is
    lmoney number;
  Begin
    if nvl(i_min, 0) = 0 and nvl(i_max, 0) = 0 then
      lmoney := i_money;
    elsif nvl(i_min, 0) = 0 and nvl(i_max, 0) <> 0 then
      if i_money >= i_max then
        lmoney := i_max;
      else
        lmoney := i_money;
      end if;
    elsif nvl(i_min, 0) <> 0 and nvl(i_max, 0) <> 0 then
      if i_money <= i_min then
        lmoney := i_min;
      elsif i_money >= i_max then
        lmoney := i_max;
      else
        lmoney := i_money;
      end if;
    elsif nvl(i_min, 0) <> 0 and nvl(i_max, 0) = 0 then
      if i_money <= i_min then
        lmoney := i_min;
      else
        lmoney := i_money;
      end if;
    end if;
    Return lmoney;
  End;

  Function getxykrate(vid In Char) Return Number Is
    lrate Number;
  Begin
    If b_CreditMode = 'B' Then
      Return 1;
    Else
      Begin
        Select xtrate
          Into lrate
          From xyktype
         Where ctid = vid
           And xtflag = 'Y';
      Exception
        When Others Then
          lrate := 0;
      End;
      Return lrate;
    End If;
  End;
  Function getxykchargeexp(i_contno     In Varchar2,
                           i_supid      In Varchar2,
                           i_wmid       In Char,
                           i_mkt        In Varchar2,
                           i_mfid       In Varchar2,
                           i_startdate  In Date,
                           i_enddate    In Date,
                           i_xyktype    In Varchar2,
                           i_chargecode In Varchar2,
                           i_contrate   In Number) Return Number Is
    lbrand contmanaframe.cmfbrand%Type;
    l_ret  Number;
  Begin
    -- 取得品牌
    Begin
      Select cmfbrand
        Into lbrand
        From contmanaframe
       Where cmfcontno = i_contno
         And cmfmfid = i_mfid
         And cmfmarket = i_mkt
         And cmfbrand = '0';
      --全部品牌
      Select nvl(Sum(decode(i_xyktype,
                            chargetypexyk1,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy1, ssdxyksr1),
                            chargetypexyk2,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy2, ssdxyksr2),
                            chargetypexyk3,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy3, ssdxyksr3),
                            chargetypexyk4,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy4, ssdxyksr4),
                            chargetypexyk5,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy5, ssdxyksr5),
                            chargetypexyk6,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy6, ssdxyksr6),
                            chargetypexyk7,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy7, ssdxyksr7),
                            chargetypexyk8,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy8, ssdxyksr8),
                            chargetypexyk9,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy9, ssdxyksr9),
                            chargetypexyk10,
                            Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy10, ssdxyksr10)) *
                     (cesrate - getxykrate(i_xyktype)) * i_contrate),
                 0)
        Into l_ret
        From salesupday, chargeexpset
       Where ssdmkt = i_mkt
         And ssdmfid = i_mfid
         And ssdsupid = i_supid
         And ssdwmid = i_wmid
         And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) >=
             i_startdate
         And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) <= i_enddate
         And SSdgdid = cesgdid
         And cesmkt = i_mkt
         And cescttype = i_xyktype
         And cesctid = i_chargecode
         And Not Exists (Select *
                From salecostday_supset
               Where scdsdate = ssddate
                 And scdsmkt = ssdmkt
                 And scdsmfid = ssdmfid
                 And scdscatid = ssdcatid
                 And scdssupid = ssdsupid
                 And scdswmid = ssdwmid
                 And scdstaxtype = ssdtaxtype
                 And scdsxstax = ssdxstax
                 And scdshsrq = ssdhsrq
                 And scdsmd = ssdmd
                 And scdsbrand = ssdbrand
                 And scdstmtype = ssdtmtype
                 --And scdsjsflag = 'Y'
                 And SCDSJSBILLNO <> b_hd.sshbillno);
    Exception
      When Others Then
        --部分品牌
        Select nvl(Sum(decode(i_xyktype,
                              chargetypexyk1,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy1, ssdxyksr1),
                              chargetypexyk2,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy2, ssdxyksr2),
                              chargetypexyk3,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy3, ssdxyksr3),
                              chargetypexyk4,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy4, ssdxyksr4),
                              chargetypexyk5,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy5, ssdxyksr5),
                              chargetypexyk6,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy6, ssdxyksr6),
                              chargetypexyk7,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy7, ssdxyksr7),
                              chargetypexyk8,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy8, ssdxyksr8),
                              chargetypexyk9,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy9, ssdxyksr9),
                              chargetypexyk10,
                              Decode(b_CreditMode,
                                     'B',
                                     ssdxykfy10,
                                     ssdxyksr10)) *
                       (cesrate - getxykrate(i_xyktype)) * i_contrate),
                   0)
          Into l_ret
          From salesupday, chargeexpset
         Where ssdmkt = i_mkt
           And ssdmfid = i_mfid
           And ssdsupid = i_supid
           And ssdwmid = i_wmid
           And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) >=
               i_startdate
           And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) <=
               i_enddate
           And SSdgdid = cesgdid
           And cescttype = i_xyktype
           And cesmkt = i_mkt
           And cesctid = i_chargecode
           And Not Exists
         (Select *
                  From salecostday_supset
                 Where scdsdate = ssddate
                   And scdsmkt = ssdmkt
                   And scdsmfid = ssdmfid
                   And scdscatid = ssdcatid
                   And scdssupid = ssdsupid
                   And scdswmid = ssdwmid
                   And scdstaxtype = ssdtaxtype
                   And scdsxstax = ssdxstax
                   And scdshsrq = ssdhsrq
                   And scdsmd = ssdmd
                   And scdsbrand = ssdbrand
                   And scdstmtype = ssdtmtype
                   --And scdsjsflag = 'Y'
                   And SCDSJSBILLNO <> b_hd.sshbillno)
           And ssdbrand In (Select cmfbrand
                              From contmanaframe
                             Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                               And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                               And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                               And cmfbrand <> '0');
    End;
    Return l_ret;
  End;
  Function getchargeexp(i_contno     In Varchar2,
                        i_supid      In Varchar2,
                        i_wmid       In Char,
                        i_mkt        In Varchar2,
                        i_mfid       In Varchar2,
                        i_startdate  In Date,
                        i_enddate    In Date,
                        i_chargetype In Varchar2,
                        i_chargecode In Varchar2,
                        i_contrate   In Number) Return Number Is
    lbrand contmanaframe.cmfbrand%Type;
    l_ret  Number;
  Begin
    -- 取得品牌
    Begin
      Select cmfbrand
        Into lbrand
        From contmanaframe
       Where cmfcontno = i_contno
         And cmfmfid = i_mfid
         And cmfmarket = i_mkt
         And cmfbrand = '0';
      --全部品牌
      Select decode(i_chargetype,
                    chargetypexssr,
                    round(nvl(Sum((xssr + pfsr) * (cesrate - i_contrate)), 0),
                          2),
                    chargetypexsje,
                    round(nvl(Sum((xssjje + pfsjje) * (cesrate - i_contrate)),
                              0),
                          2),
                    chargetypexscb,
                    round(nvl(Sum((xshsjjje + pfhsjjje) *
                                  (cesrate - i_contrate)),
                              0),
                          2) + round(nvl(Sum((xshsjjad + pfhsjjad) *
                                             (cesrate - i_contrate)),
                                         0),
                                     2) -
                    round(nvl(Sum((xssupzk + pfsupzk) *
                                  (cesrate - i_contrate)),
                              0),
                          2),
                    0)
      
        Into l_ret
        From SALEGOODSDAY, chargeexpset
       Where sgdmkt = i_mkt
         And sgdmfid = i_mfid
         And sgdsupid = i_supid
         And sgdwmid = i_wmid
         And sgdhsrq >= i_startdate
         And sgdhsrq <= i_enddate
         And cescttype = i_chargetype
         And cesmkt = i_mkt
         And cesgdid = sgdgdid
         And cesctid = i_chargecode
         And (b_isqs = '1' Or
             (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
              (Select *
                  From salecostday_supset
                 Where b_isqs = '0'
                   And scdsdate = sgddate
                   And scdsmkt = sgdmkt
                   And scdsmfid = sgdmfid
                   And scdscatid = sgdcatid
                   And scdssupid = sgdsupid
                   And scdswmid = sgdwmid
                   And scdstaxtype = sgdtaxtype
                   And scdsxstax = sgdxstax
                   And scdshsrq = sgdhsrq
                   And scdsmd = sgdmd
                   And scdsbrand = sgdbrand
                   And scdstmtype = sgdtmtype
                   --And scdsjsflag = 'Y'
                   And scdsjsbillno <> b_hd.sshbillno)));
    Exception
      When Others Then
        --部分品牌
        Select decode(i_chargetype,
                      chargetypexssr,
                      round(nvl(Sum((xssr + pfsr) * (cesrate - i_contrate)),
                                0),
                            2),
                      chargetypexsje,
                      round(nvl(Sum((xssjje + pfsjje) *
                                    (cesrate - i_contrate)),
                                0),
                            2),
                      chargetypexscb,
                      round(nvl(Sum((xshsjjje + pfhsjjje) *
                                    (cesrate - i_contrate)),
                                0),
                            2) + round(nvl(Sum((xshsjjad + pfhsjjad) *
                                               (cesrate - i_contrate)),
                                           0),
                                       2) -
                      round(nvl(Sum((xssupzk + pfsupzk) *
                                    (cesrate - i_contrate)),
                                0),
                            2),
                      0)
        
          Into l_ret
          From SALEGOODSDAY, chargeexpset
         Where sgdmkt = i_mkt
           And sgdmfid = i_mfid
           And sgdsupid = i_supid
           And sgdwmid = i_wmid
           And sgdhsrq >= i_startdate
           And sgdhsrq <= i_enddate
           And cescttype = i_chargetype
           And cesmkt = i_mkt
           And cesgdid = sgdgdid
           And cesctid = i_chargecode
           And (b_isqs = '1' Or
               (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                (Select *
                    From salecostday_supset
                   Where b_isqs = '0'
                     And scdsdate = sgddate
                     And scdsmkt = sgdmkt
                     And scdsmfid = sgdmfid
                     And scdscatid = sgdcatid
                     And scdssupid = sgdsupid
                     And scdswmid = sgdwmid
                     And scdstaxtype = sgdtaxtype
                     And scdsxstax = sgdxstax
                     And scdshsrq = sgdhsrq
                     And scdsmd = sgdmd
                     And scdsbrand = sgdbrand
                     And scdstmtype = sgdtmtype
                     --And scdsjsflag = 'Y'
                     And scdsjsbillno <> b_hd.sshbillno)))
           And sgdbrand In (Select cmfbrand
                              From contmanaframe
                             Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                               And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                               And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                               And cmfbrand <> '0');
    End;
    Return l_ret;
  End;
  Function getjxtaxhsje(vjsdh In Varchar2, vtaxrate In Number) Return Number As
    lje Number;
  Begin
    Select nvl(Sum(ssdn15), 0)
      Into lje
      From supsettledet
     Where ssdbillno = vjsdh
       And ssdn35 = vtaxrate;
    Return lje;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Return 0;
  End getjxtaxhsje;
  Function getjxtaxbhsje(vjsdh In Varchar2, vtaxrate In Number) Return Number As
    lje Number;
  Begin
    Select nvl(Sum(ssdn16), 0)
      Into lje
      From supsettledet
     Where ssdbillno = vjsdh
       And ssdn35 = vtaxrate;
    Return lje;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Return 0;
  End getjxtaxbhsje;
  --获取分税率结算信息
  Function Getjxtaxdesc(Vjsdh In Varchar2) Return Varchar2 As
    v_Desc Varchar2(2000);
  Begin
    For Rr In (Select Ssdn35,
                      '税率' || To_Char(Ssdn35 * 100) || '%: ' || '含税金额 ￥' ||
                      Trim(To_Char(Sum(Ssdn15), '9,999,999,999.99')) ||
                      ',  不含税金额 ￥' ||
                      Trim(To_Char(Sum(Ssdn16), '9,999,999,999.99')) Tt
                 From Supsettledet
                Where Ssdbillno = Vjsdh
                Group By Ssdn35
                Order By Ssdn35) Loop
      If v_Desc Is Null Then
        v_Desc := Rr.Tt;
      Else
        v_Desc := v_Desc || chr(13) || chr(10) || Rr.Tt;
      End If;
    End Loop;
    Return v_Desc;
  End;

  --获得合同定义的非票减的扣款方式
  Function fGetContChargeMode(i_contno        In Varchar2,
                              i_defchargetype In Char) Return Char As
    lmode Char(1);
  Begin
    Select Nvl(Trim(cmchar3), i_defchargetype)
      Into lmode
      From contmain
     Where cmcontno = i_contno;
    Return lmode;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Return i_defchargetype;
  End fGetContChargeMode;

  --判断日期是否属于该合同保底期
  Function fChkIsBdPeriod(i_contno In Varchar2, i_chkdate In Date)
    Return Char As
    l_startdate Date;
    l_enddate   Date;
    l_flag      Char(1);
  Begin
    Select Min(cbeffdate), Max(cblapdate)
      Into l_startdate, l_enddate
      From contbd
     Where cbcontno = i_contno;
    If i_chkdate >= l_startdate And i_chkdate <= l_enddate Then
      l_flag := 'Y';
    Else
      l_flag := 'N';
    End If;
    Return l_flag;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Return 'Y';
  End fChkIsBdPeriod;

  Procedure initce Is
  Begin
    If b_ce Is Not Null Then
      b_ce := tcelist();
    End If;
  End initce;
  Procedure addce(i_sum In Number, i_rate In Number) Is
  Begin
    If i_sum Is Null Or i_sum <= 0 Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If i_rate Is Null Or i_rate < 0 Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If b_ce Is Null Then
      b_ce := tcelist();
    End If;
    b_ce.EXTEND;
    b_ce(b_ce.LAST).cesum := i_sum;
    b_ce(b_ce.LAST).cerate := i_rate;
  End addce;
  Procedure sortce Is
    i   Number;
    j   Number;
    lce tce;
  Begin
    --按基数从低到高排序
    For i In 1 .. b_ce.COUNT Loop
      If i < b_ce.COUNT Then
        For j In (i + 1) .. b_ce.COUNT Loop
          If b_ce(i).cesum > b_ce(j).cesum Then
            lce := b_ce(i);
            b_ce(i) := b_ce(j);
            b_ce(j) := lce;
          End If;
        End Loop;
      End If;
    End Loop;
  End sortce;

  Procedure InitCeList Is
  Begin
    If b_celist Is Not Null Then
      b_celist := CeRecList();
    End If;
  End InitCeList;

  Procedure AddCeRec(i_mode In Char, i_sum In Number, i_rate In Number) Is
  Begin
    If i_mode Is Null Or i_mode Not In (CeModeQe, CeModeCe) Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If i_sum Is Null Or i_sum <= 0 Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If i_rate Is Null Or i_rate <= 0 Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If b_celist Is Null Then
      b_celist := CeRecList();
    End If;
    b_celist.EXTEND;
    b_celist(b_celist.LAST).cemode := i_mode;
    b_celist(b_celist.LAST).cesum := i_sum;
    b_celist(b_celist.LAST).cerate := i_rate;
  End AddCeRec;

  Procedure SortCeList Is
    i      Number;
    j      Number;
    lcerec CeRec;
  Begin
    --按基数从低到高排序
    For i In 1 .. b_celist.COUNT Loop
      If i < b_celist.COUNT Then
        For j In (i + 1) .. b_celist.COUNT Loop
          If b_celist(i).cesum > b_celist(j).cesum Then
            lcerec := b_celist(i);
            b_celist(i) := b_celist(j);
            b_celist(j) := lcerec;
          End If;
        End Loop;
      End If;
    End Loop;
  End SortCeList;

  Procedure initbd Is
  Begin
    If b_bd Is Not Null Then
      b_bd := bdlist();
    End If;
  End initbd;

  Procedure addbd(i_seq In Number, i_startdate In Date, i_enddate In Date) Is
  Begin
    If i_seq Is Null Or i_seq <= 0 Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If i_startdate Is Null Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If i_enddate Is Null Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If b_bd Is Null Then
      b_bd := bdlist();
    End If;
    b_bd.EXTEND;
    b_bd(b_bd.LAST).seq := i_seq;
    b_bd(b_bd.LAST).startdate := i_startdate;
    b_bd(b_bd.LAST).enddate := i_enddate;
  End addbd;

  Procedure sortbd Is
    i   Number;
    j   Number;
    lbd bddata;
  Begin
    --按日期从后往前排,即按seq从小到大排序
    For i In 1 .. b_bd.COUNT Loop
      If i < b_bd.COUNT Then
        For j In (i + 1) .. b_bd.COUNT Loop
          If b_bd(i).seq > b_bd(j).seq Then
            lbd := b_bd(i);
            b_bd(i) := b_bd(j);
            b_bd(j) := lbd;
          End If;
        End Loop;
      End If;
    End Loop;
  End sortbd;

  Procedure initqs Is
  Begin
    If b_qs Is Not Null Then
      b_qs := qslist();
    End If;
  End initqs;

  Procedure addqs(i_seq       In Number,
                  i_startdate In Date,
                  i_enddate   In Date,
                  i_unionflag In Char) Is
  Begin
    If i_seq Is Null Or i_seq <= 0 Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If i_startdate Is Null Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If i_enddate Is Null Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If i_unionflag Is Null Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If b_qs Is Null Then
      b_qs := qslist();
    End If;
    b_qs.EXTEND;
    b_qs(b_qs.LAST).seq := i_seq;
    b_qs(b_qs.LAST).startdate := i_startdate;
    b_qs(b_qs.LAST).enddate := i_enddate;
    b_qs(b_qs.LAST).unionflag := i_unionflag;
  End addqs;

  Procedure sortqs Is
    i   Number;
    j   Number;
    lqs qsdata;
  Begin
    --按日期从后往前排,即按seq从小到大排序
    For i In 1 .. b_qs.COUNT Loop
      If i < b_qs.COUNT Then
        For j In (i + 1) .. b_qs.COUNT Loop
          If b_qs(i).seq > b_qs(j).seq Then
            lqs := b_qs(i);
            b_qs(i) := b_qs(j);
            b_qs(j) := lqs;
          End If;
        End Loop;
      End If;
    End Loop;
  End sortqs;
  --统计商品销售数量
  Procedure SaleQtyStatis(p_BillNo In Varchar2) Is
    l_Xssl Number;
  Begin
    If b_isqs = '0' Then
      For vr In (Select *
                   From SupSettleDet
                  Where SsdBillNo = p_BillNo
                    And Ssdwmid In (Wmid2, Wmid3, Wmid4, Wmid5)
                    And SsdVc5 = '3'
                    And SsdVc6 = '0') Loop
        Begin
          Select Nvl(Sum(XSSL + PFSL), 0)
            Into l_Xssl
            From SaleGoodsDay
           Where Exists (Select 1
                    From salecostday_supset
                   Where scdsdate = sgddate
                     And scdsmkt = sgdmkt
                     And scdsmfid = sgdmfid
                     And scdscatid = sgdcatid
                     And scdssupid = sgdsupid
                     And scdswmid = sgdwmid
                     And scdstaxtype = sgdtaxtype
                     And scdsxstax = sgdxstax
                     And scdshsrq = sgdhsrq
                     And scdsmd = sgdmd
                     And scdsbrand = sgdbrand
                     And scdstmtype = sgdtmtype
                     And SCDSJSBILLNO = p_BillNo
                     And ScdsMfid = Vr.Ssdmfid
                     and scdsjjtax   = sgdjjtax )
             And SGDKL = vr.ssdn62
             and sgdjjtax= vr.ssdn80
             And decode(sgdtmtype,
                        '2',
                        '特卖超额',
                        '3',
                        '普通特卖',
                        '保底超额') = vr.ssdvc10;
        Exception
          When Others Then
            l_Xssl := 0;
        End;
        Update SupSettleDet
           Set SsdN74 = l_Xssl
         Where SsdBillNo = p_BillNo
           And SsdRowNo = vr.SsdRowNo;
      End Loop;
    
    End If;
  End SaleQtyStatis;

  Procedure initssdsrow(v_scdsdet In Out salecostday_set%Rowtype) Is
  Begin
    v_scdsdet.scdsdate     := currentdate;
    v_scdsdet.scdsmkt      := Null;
    v_scdsdet.scdsmfid     := Null;
    v_scdsdet.scdssupid    := b_hd.sshsupid;
    v_scdsdet.scdswmid     := b_hd.sshwmid;
    v_scdsdet.scdsjsbillno := b_hd.sshbillno;
    v_scdsdet.scdsisqs     := b_isqs;
    v_scdsdet.scdshsrq1    := b_hd.sshlastdate;
    v_scdsdet.scdshsrq2    := b_hd.sshthisdate;
    v_scdsdet.scdsxssr     := 0;
    v_scdsdet.scdsml       := 0;
    v_scdsdet.scdsjjje     := 0;
    v_scdsdet.scdskl       := 0;
    v_scdsdet.scdsnum1     := 0;
    v_scdsdet.scdsnum2     := 0;
    v_scdsdet.scdsnum3     := 0;
    v_scdsdet.scdsnum4     := 0;
    v_scdsdet.scdsnum5     := 0;
  End;
  Procedure initdetrow(v_det In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
  Begin
    v_det.ssdn1  := 0; --含税进价金额
    v_det.ssdn2  := 0; --不含税进价金额
    v_det.ssdn3  := 0; --含税售价金额
    v_det.ssdn4  := 0; --含税进价调整金额
    v_det.ssdn5  := 0; --不含税进价调整金额
    v_det.ssdn6  := 0; ----进项税额 15-16
    v_det.ssdn7  := 0; --含税总折扣
    v_det.ssdn8  := 0; --含税供应商折扣
    v_det.ssdn9  := 0; --含税销售收入
    v_det.ssdn10 := 0; --含税销售毛利
    v_det.ssdn11 := 0; --销项税

    v_det.ssdn13 := 0; --损溢不含税进价金额
    v_det.ssdn14 := 0; --损溢含税售价金额
    v_det.ssdn15 := 0; --含税应付金额(预计)    9 - 1 + 4 - 8
    v_det.ssdn16 := 0; --不含税应付金额(预计)  9 - 11 - 2 + 5 - 8 * （1 - 11/9);
    v_det.ssdn17 := 0; --进货含税进价金额
    v_det.ssdn18 := 0; --进货不含税进价金额
    v_det.ssdn19 := 0; --进货含税进价调整金额
    v_det.ssdn20 := 0; --进货不含税进价调整金额
    v_det.ssdn21 := 0; --保底金额
    v_det.ssdn22 := 0; --保底扣率
    v_det.ssdn23 := 0; --保底提成
    v_det.ssdn24 := 0; --超额
    v_det.ssdn25 := 0; --超额扣率
    v_det.ssdn26 := 0; --超额提成
    v_det.ssdn27 := 0; --合同扣率
    v_det.ssdn28 := 0; --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
    v_det.ssdn29 := 0; --销售应提(不含保底、超额)
    v_det.ssdn30 := 0; --扣款合计
    v_det.ssdn31 := 0; --供应商承担会员 2004.04.15
    v_det.ssdn32 := 0; --合同定义的保底毛利
    v_det.ssdn33 := 0; --供应商承担促销
    v_det.ssdn34 := 0; --供应商承担授权
    v_det.ssdn35 := 0; --经销进项税率
    v_det.ssdn36 := 0; --经销 出入库单售价金额
    v_det.ssdn37 := 0; --销售成本 销售进价含税金额 + 销售含税调整 - 供应商进价折扣承担
    -- 1 + 4 - 8
    v_det.ssdn38 := 0; --结算调整（帐扣费用）
    v_det.ssdn39 := 0; --正常销售收入
    v_det.ssdn40 := 0; --特卖销售收入
    v_det.ssdn41 := 0; --特卖销售收入(保底)
    v_det.ssdn42 := 0; --特卖销售收入(超额)
    v_det.ssdn43 := 0; --特卖销售收入(不保底不超额)
    v_det.ssdn44 := 0; --按数量提取费用的销售数量
    v_det.ssdn45 := 0; --信用卡收入(内)
    v_det.ssdn46 := 0; --信用卡收入(外)
    v_det.ssdn47 := 0; --VIP1销售收入
    v_det.ssdn48 := 0; --VIP2销售收入
    v_det.ssdn49 := 0; --返券金额
    v_det.ssdn50 := 0; --收券金额
    --信用卡收入  1-10
    v_det.ssdn51 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn52 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn53 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn54 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn55 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn56 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn57 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn58 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn59 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn60 := 0;
    --结算销售及保底超额分扣率明细，ssdvc5='3','4'
    v_det.ssdn61 := 0; --销售收入                   --VIP折扣1
    v_det.ssdn62 := 0; --扣率                       --VIP折扣2
    v_det.ssdn63 := 0; --销售成本                   --VIP折扣3
    v_det.ssdn64 := 0; --总折扣                     --VIP折扣4
    v_det.ssdn65 := 0; --供应商承担折扣              --VIP折扣5
    v_det.ssdn66 := 0; --含税调整
    v_det.ssdn67 := 0; --售价金额
    v_det.ssdn68 := 0; --mzk收入
    v_det.ssdn69 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn70 := 0;
    -- add
    v_det.ssdn71 := 0; --不含税销售收入
    v_det.ssdn72 := 0; --租赁租金
    v_det.ssdn73 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn74 := 0; --销售数量
    v_det.ssdn75 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn76 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn77 := 0; --付款方式不计收入
    v_det.ssdn78 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn79 := 0;
    v_det.ssdn80 := 0;
  End initdetrow;

  Procedure insertscds(i_scds In salecostday_set%Rowtype) Is
  Begin
    Insert Into salecostday_set Values i_scds;
  End;
  Procedure insertdetail(i_det In supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
  Begin
    Insert Into supsettledet Values i_det;
  End insertdetail;

  --统计日期段销售
  Procedure salesupdate(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                        i_supid     In Varchar2,
                        i_wmid      In Char,
                        i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                        i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                        i_startdate In Date,
                        i_enddate   In Date,
                        o_det       In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
    lbrand contmanaframe.cmfbrand%Type;
  Begin
    -- 取得品牌
    Begin
      Select cmfbrand
        Into lbrand
        From contmanaframe
       Where cmfcontno = i_contno
         And cmfmfid = i_mfid
         And cmfmarket = i_mkt
         And cmfbrand = '0';
      --全部品牌
      Select nvl(Sum(ssdfysl), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdccardi), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdccardo), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdvip1sr), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdvip2sr), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdvip3sr), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdvip4sr), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdvip5sr), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdfqje), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdsqje), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy1, ssdxyksr1)), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy2, ssdxyksr2)), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy3, ssdxyksr3)), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy4, ssdxyksr4)), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy5, ssdxyksr5)), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy6, ssdxyksr6)), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy7, ssdxyksr7)), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy8, ssdxyksr8)), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy9, ssdxyksr9)), 0),
             nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy10, ssdxyksr10)), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk1), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk2), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk3), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk4), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk5), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdn4), 0),
             nvl(Sum(ssdn2), 0)
        Into o_det.ssdn44,
             o_det.ssdn45,
             o_det.ssdn46,
             o_det.ssdn47,
             o_det.ssdn48,
             o_det.ssdn78,
             o_det.ssdn79,
             o_det.ssdn80,
             o_det.ssdn49,
             o_det.ssdn50,
             o_det.ssdn51,
             o_det.ssdn52,
             o_det.ssdn53,
             o_det.ssdn54,
             o_det.ssdn55,
             o_det.ssdn56,
             o_det.ssdn57,
             o_det.ssdn58,
             o_det.ssdn59,
             o_det.ssdn60,
             o_Det.Ssdn61,
             o_Det.Ssdn62,
             o_Det.Ssdn63,
             o_Det.Ssdn64,
             o_Det.Ssdn65,
             o_det.ssdn68,
             o_det.ssdn69
        From salesupday
       Where ssdmkt = i_mkt
         And ssdmfid = i_mfid
         And ssdsupid = i_supid
         And ssdwmid = i_wmid
         And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) >=
             i_startdate
         And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) <= i_enddate
         And Not Exists (Select *
                From salecostday_supset
               Where scdsdate = ssddate
                 And scdsmkt = ssdmkt
                 And scdsmfid = ssdmfid
                 And scdscatid = ssdcatid
                 And scdssupid = ssdsupid
                 And scdswmid = ssdwmid
                 And scdstaxtype = ssdtaxtype
                 And scdsxstax = ssdxstax
                 And scdshsrq = ssdhsrq
                 And scdsmd = ssdmd
                 And scdsbrand = ssdbrand
                 And scdstmtype = ssdtmtype
                 And scdsjsflag = 'Y')
         And Not Exists (Select *
                From salecostday_supset
               Where scdsdate = ssddate
                 And scdsmkt = ssdmkt
                 And scdsmfid = ssdmfid
                 And scdscatid = ssdcatid
                 And scdssupid = ssdsupid
                 And scdswmid = ssdwmid
                 And scdstaxtype = ssdtaxtype
                 And scdsxstax = ssdxstax
                 And scdshsrq = ssdhsrq
                 And scdsmd = ssdmd
                 And scdsbrand = ssdbrand
                 And scdstmtype = ssdtmtype
                 And (scdsjsflag = 'N'and scdscontno<>i_contno));
    Exception
      When Others Then
        --部分品牌
        Select nvl(Sum(ssdfysl), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdccardi), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdccardo), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdvip1sr), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdvip2sr), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdvip3sr), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdvip4sr), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdvip5sr), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdfqje), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdsqje), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy1, ssdxyksr1)), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy2, ssdxyksr2)), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy3, ssdxyksr3)), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy4, ssdxyksr4)), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy5, ssdxyksr5)), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy6, ssdxyksr6)), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy7, ssdxyksr7)), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy8, ssdxyksr8)), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy9, ssdxyksr9)), 0),
               nvl(Sum(Decode(b_CreditMode, 'B', ssdxykfy10, ssdxyksr10)),
                   0),
               Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk1), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk2), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk3), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk4), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(ssdvipzk5), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdn4), 0),
               nvl(Sum(ssdn2), 0)
          Into o_det.ssdn44,
               o_det.ssdn45,
               o_det.ssdn46,
               o_det.ssdn47,
               o_det.ssdn48,
               o_det.ssdn78,
               o_det.ssdn79,
               o_det.ssdn80,
               o_det.ssdn49,
               o_det.ssdn50,
               o_det.ssdn51,
               o_det.ssdn52,
               o_det.ssdn53,
               o_det.ssdn54,
               o_det.ssdn55,
               o_det.ssdn56,
               o_det.ssdn57,
               o_det.ssdn58,
               o_det.ssdn59,
               o_det.ssdn60,
               o_Det.Ssdn61,
               o_Det.Ssdn62,
               o_Det.Ssdn63,
               o_Det.Ssdn64,
               o_Det.Ssdn65,
               o_det.ssdn68,
               o_det.ssdn69
          From salesupday
         Where ssdmkt = i_mkt
           And ssdmfid = i_mfid
           And ssdsupid = i_supid
           And ssdwmid = i_wmid
           And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) >=
               i_startdate
           And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) <=
               i_enddate
           And Not Exists
         (Select *
                  From salecostday_supset
                 Where scdsdate = ssddate
                   And scdsmkt = ssdmkt
                   And scdsmfid = ssdmfid
                   And scdscatid = ssdcatid
                   And scdssupid = ssdsupid
                   And scdswmid = ssdwmid
                   And scdstaxtype = ssdtaxtype
                   And scdsxstax = ssdxstax
                   And scdshsrq = ssdhsrq
                   And scdsmd = ssdmd
                   And scdsbrand = ssdbrand
                   And scdstmtype = ssdtmtype
                   And scdsjsflag = 'Y')
           And Not Exists (Select *
                From salecostday_supset
               Where scdsdate = ssddate
                 And scdsmkt = ssdmkt
                 And scdsmfid = ssdmfid
                 And scdscatid = ssdcatid
                 And scdssupid = ssdsupid
                 And scdswmid = ssdwmid
                 And scdstaxtype = ssdtaxtype
                 And scdsxstax = ssdxstax
                 And scdshsrq = ssdhsrq
                 And scdsmd = ssdmd
                 And scdsbrand = ssdbrand
                 And scdstmtype = ssdtmtype
                 And (scdsjsflag = 'N'and scdscontno<>i_contno))        
           And ssdbrand In (Select cmfbrand
                              From contmanaframe
                             Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                               And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                               And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                               And cmfbrand <> '0');
    End;
  End salesupdate;

  --获取最大税率
  Function fgetmaxsl(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                     i_supid     In Varchar2,
                     i_wmid      In Char,
                     i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                     i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                     i_startdate In Date,
                     i_enddate   In Date,
                     i_flag      In Char) Return number is
    l_sl number;
  Begin
    l_sl := 0.00;
    Select max(SCDXSTAX)
      into l_sl
      From salecostday
     Where scdmkt = i_mkt
       And scdmfid = i_mfid
       And scdsupid = i_supid
       And scdwmid = i_wmid
       And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) >= i_startdate
       And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) <= i_enddate
       And (b_isqs = '1' Or i_flag = 'Y' Or
           (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
            (Select *
                From salecostday_supset
               Where b_isqs = '0'
                 And scdsdate = scddate
                 And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                 And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                 And scdscatid = scdcatid
                 And scdssupid = scdsupid
                 And scdswmid = scdwmid
                 And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                 And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                 And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                 And scdsmd = scdmd
                 And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                 And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                 and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                 And scdsjsflag = 'Y')))
        And (b_isqs = '1' Or i_flag = 'Y' Or
           (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
            (Select *
                From salecostday_supset
               Where b_isqs = '0'
                 And scdsdate = scddate
                 And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                 And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                 And scdscatid = scdcatid
                 And scdssupid = scdsupid
                 And scdswmid = scdwmid
                 And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                 And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                 And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                 And scdsmd = scdmd
                 And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                 And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                 and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                 And (scdsjsflag = 'N' and scdscontno<>i_contno))));         
  
    Return l_sl;
  End fgetmaxsl;

  --统计日期段销售
  Procedure saledate(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                     i_supid     In Varchar2,
                     i_wmid      In Char,
                     i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                     i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                     i_startdate In Date,
                     i_enddate   In Date,
                     i_unionflag In Char Default 'N',
                     o_det       In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
    lbrand contmanaframe.cmfbrand%Type;
  Begin
    -- 取得品牌
    Begin
      Select cmfbrand
        Into lbrand
        From contmanaframe
       Where cmfcontno = i_contno
         And cmfmfid = i_mfid
         And cmfmarket = i_mkt
         And cmfbrand = '0';
      --全部品牌
      Select Nvl(Sum(n1), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(N2), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n3), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n4), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n5), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n6), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n7), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n8), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n9), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n10), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n11), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n39), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n40), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n41), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n42), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n43), 0),
             Nvl(Sum(n77), 0)/*,
             SCDXSTAX*/
        Into o_det.ssdn1,
             o_det.ssdn2,
             o_det.ssdn3,
             o_det.ssdn4,
             o_det.ssdn5,
             o_det.ssdn6,
             o_det.ssdn7,
             o_det.ssdn8,
             o_det.ssdn9,
             o_det.ssdn10,
             o_det.ssdn11,
             o_det.ssdn39,
             o_det.ssdn40,
             o_det.ssdn41,
             o_det.ssdn42,
             o_det.ssdn43,
             o_det.ssdn77/*,
             o_det.ssdn80*/
        From (Select decode(scdtmtype,
                            '2',
                            '特卖超额',
                            '3',
                            '普通特卖',
                            '保底超额') gd,
                     decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl) scdkl,
                     --SCDXSTAX,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xshsjjje, 0) + nvl(pfhsjjje, 0)), 2) n1,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xsbhsjjje, 0) + nvl(pfbhsjjje, 0)), 2) n2,
                     round(nvl(Sum((xssjje + pfsjje)), 0), 2) n3,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xshsjjad, 0) + nvl(pfhsjjad, 0)), 2) n4,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xsbhsjjad, 0) + nvl(pfbhsjjad, 0)), 2) n5,
                     0 n6,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xstotzk, 0) + nvl(pftotzk, 0)), 2) n7,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xssupzk, 0) + nvl(pfsupzk, 0)), 2) n8,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xssr, 0) + nvl(pfsr, 0)), 2) n9,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xsjjml, 0) + nvl(pfjjml, 0)), 2) n10, --先四舍五入再汇总，20150701
                     round(Sum(nvl(xszzse, 0) + nvl(pfzzse, 0)), 2) n11,
                     round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) *
                                   (xssr + pfsr))),
                               0),
                           2) n39,
                     round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '0', 0, 1) *
                                   (xssr + pfsr))),
                               0),
                           2) n40,
                     round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) *
                                   (xssr + pfsr))),
                               0),
                           2) n41,
                     round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) *
                                   (xssr + pfsr))),
                               0),
                           2) n42,
                     round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) *
                                   (xssr + pfsr))),
                               0),
                           2) n43,
                  --   round(nvl(Sum(nvl(scdzfje, 0)), 0), 2) n77
                   0 n77
                From salecostday
               Where scdmkt = i_mkt
                 And scdmfid = i_mfid
                 And scdsupid = i_supid
                 And scdwmid = i_wmid
                 And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) >=
                     i_startdate
                 And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) <=
                     i_enddate
                 And (b_isqs = '1' Or
                     (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                      (Select *
                          From salecostday_supset
                         Where b_isqs = '0'
                           And scdsdate = scddate
                           And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                           And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                           And scdscatid = scdcatid
                           And scdssupid = scdsupid
                           And scdswmid = scdwmid
                           And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                           And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                           And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                           And scdsmd = scdmd
                           And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                           And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                           And scdsjsflag = 'Y'
                           and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax)))
                 And (b_isqs = '1' Or
                     (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                      (Select *
                          From salecostday_supset
                         Where b_isqs = '0'
                           And scdsdate = scddate
                           And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                           And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                           And scdscatid = scdcatid
                           And scdssupid = scdsupid
                           And scdswmid = scdwmid
                           And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                           And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                           And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                           And scdsmd = scdmd
                           And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                           And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                           And (scdsjsflag = 'N' and scdscontno<>i_contno)
                           and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax)))          
               Group By decode(scdtmtype,
                               '2',
                               '特卖超额',
                               '3',
                               '普通特卖',
                               '保底超额'),
                        decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl),
                        SCDXSTAX)
       /*group by SCDXSTAX*/;
      o_det.ssdn80 := 0.13; 
      o_det.ssdn15 := o_det.ssdn9 - o_det.ssdn10;
      If o_det.ssdn1 + o_det.ssdn4 = 0 Then
        o_det.ssdn16 := o_det.ssdn2 + o_det.ssdn5 - round(o_det.ssdn8, 2);
      Else
        o_det.ssdn16 := o_det.ssdn2 + o_det.ssdn5 -
                        round(o_det.ssdn8 * ((o_det.ssdn2 + o_det.ssdn5) /
                              (o_det.ssdn1 + o_det.ssdn4)),
                              2);
      End If;
      o_det.ssdn6  := o_det.ssdn15 - o_det.ssdn16;
      o_det.ssdn37 := o_det.ssdn1 + o_det.ssdn4 - o_det.ssdn8;
      --更新已结算销售
      If b_isqs = '0' Then
        Insert Into salecostday_supset
          Select Distinct scddate,
                          scdmkt,
                          scdmfid,
                          scdcatid,
                          scdsupid,
                          scdwmid,
                          scdtaxtype,
                          scdxstax,
                          scdhsrq,
                          scdmd,
                          scdbrand,
                          scdtmtype,
                          'N',
                          b_hd.sshbillno,
                          '1',
                          scdjjtax,
                          i_contno
            From salecostday
           Where scdmkt = i_mkt
             And scdmfid = i_mfid
             And scdsupid = i_supid
             And scdwmid = i_wmid
             And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) >=
                 i_startdate
             And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) <=
                 i_enddate
             And Not Exists (Select *
                    From salecostday_supset
                   Where scdsdate = scddate
                     And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                     And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                     And scdscatid = scdcatid
                     And scdssupid = scdsupid
                     And scdswmid = scdwmid
                     And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                     And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                     And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                     And scdsmd = scdmd
                     And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                      and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                     And scdstmtype = scdtmtype);
        --未发生销售的费用，也要插入SaleCostDay_SupSet
        Insert Into salecostday_supset
          Select Distinct ssddate,
                          ssdmkt,
                          ssdmfid,
                          ssdcatid,
                          ssdsupid,
                          ssdwmid,
                          ssdtaxtype,
                          ssdxstax,
                          ssdhsrq,
                          ssdmd,
                          ssdbrand,
                          ssdtmtype,
                          'N',
                          b_hd.sshbillno,
                          '2',
                          ssdxstax,  --wj暂时记录销售税率
                          i_contno
            From salesupday
           Where ssdmkt = i_mkt
             And ssdmfid = i_mfid
             And ssdsupid = i_supid
             And ssdwmid = i_wmid
             And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) >=
                 i_startdate
             And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) <=
                 i_enddate
             And Not Exists (Select *
                    From salecostday_supset
                   Where scdsdate = ssddate
                     And scdsmkt = ssdmkt
                     And scdsmfid = ssdmfid
                     And scdscatid = ssdcatid
                     And scdssupid = ssdsupid
                     And scdswmid = ssdwmid
                     And scdstaxtype = ssdtaxtype
                     And scdsxstax = ssdxstax
                     And scdshsrq = ssdhsrq
                        --AND scdsmd = ssdmd
                     And scdsbrand = ssdbrand
                     And scdstmtype = ssdtmtype);
      
      End If;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        --部分品牌
        Select Nvl(Sum(n1), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(N2), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n3), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n4), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n5), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n6), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n7), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n8), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n9), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n10), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n11), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n39), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n40), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n41), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n42), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n43), 0),
               Nvl(Sum(n77), 0)/*,
               SCDXSTAX*/
          Into o_det.ssdn1,
               o_det.ssdn2,
               o_det.ssdn3,
               o_det.ssdn4,
               o_det.ssdn5,
               o_det.ssdn6,
               o_det.ssdn7,
               o_det.ssdn8,
               o_det.ssdn9,
               o_det.ssdn10,
               o_det.ssdn11,
               o_det.ssdn39,
               o_det.ssdn40,
               o_det.ssdn41,
               o_det.ssdn42,
               o_det.ssdn43,
               o_det.ssdn77/*,
               o_det.ssdn80*/
          From (Select decode(scdtmtype,
                              '2',
                              '特卖超额',
                              '3',
                              '普通特卖',
                              '保底超额') gd,
                       decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl) scdkl,
                       --SCDXSTAX,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xshsjjje, 0) + nvl(pfhsjjje, 0)), 2) n1,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xsbhsjjje, 0) + nvl(pfbhsjjje, 0)), 2) n2,
                       round(nvl(Sum((xssjje + pfsjje)), 0), 2) n3,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xshsjjad, 0) + nvl(pfhsjjad, 0)), 2) n4,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xsbhsjjad, 0) + nvl(pfbhsjjad, 0)), 2) n5,
                       0 n6,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xstotzk, 0) + nvl(pftotzk, 0)), 2) n7,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xssupzk, 0) + nvl(pfsupzk, 0)), 2) n8,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xssr, 0) + nvl(pfsr, 0)), 2) n9,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xsjjml, 0) + nvl(pfjjml, 0)), 2) n10, --先四舍五入再汇总，20150701
                       round(Sum(nvl(xszzse, 0) + nvl(pfzzse, 0)), 2) n11,
                       round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) *
                                     (xssr + pfsr))),
                                 0),
                             2) n39,
                       round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '0', 0, 1) *
                                     (xssr + pfsr))),
                                 0),
                             2) n40,
                       round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) *
                                     (xssr + pfsr))),
                                 0),
                             2) n41,
                       round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) *
                                     (xssr + pfsr))),
                                 0),
                             2) n42,
                       round(nvl(Sum((decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) *
                                     (xssr + pfsr))),
                                 0),
                             2) n43,
                       0 n77
                  From salecostday
                 Where scdmkt = i_mkt
                   And scdmfid = i_mfid
                   And scdsupid = i_supid
                   And scdwmid = i_wmid
                   And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) >=
                       i_startdate
                   And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) <=
                       i_enddate
                   And (b_isqs = '1' Or
                       (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                        (Select *
                            From salecostday_supset
                           Where b_isqs = '0'
                             And scdsdate = scddate
                             And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                             And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                             And scdscatid = scdcatid
                             And scdssupid = scdsupid
                             And scdswmid = scdwmid
                             And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                             And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                             And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                             And scdsmd = scdmd
                             And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                             And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                              and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                             And scdsjsflag = 'Y')))
                   And (b_isqs = '1' Or
                       (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                        (Select *
                            From salecostday_supset
                           Where b_isqs = '0'
                             And scdsdate = scddate
                             And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                             And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                             And scdscatid = scdcatid
                             And scdssupid = scdsupid
                             And scdswmid = scdwmid
                             And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                             And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                             And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                             And scdsmd = scdmd
                             And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                             And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                              and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                             And (scdsjsflag = 'N' and scdscontno<>i_contno))))          
                   And scdbrand In (Select cmfbrand
                                      From contmanaframe
                                     Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                                       And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                                       And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                                       And cmfbrand <> '0')
                 Group By decode(scdtmtype,
                                 '2',
                                 '特卖超额',
                                 '3',
                                 '普通特卖',
                                 '保底超额'),
                          decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl),
                          SCDXSTAX)
         /*group by SCDXSTAX*/;
         o_det.ssdn80 := 0.13;
        o_det.ssdn15 := o_det.ssdn9 - o_det.ssdn10;
        If o_det.ssdn1 + o_det.ssdn4 = 0 Then
          o_det.ssdn16 := o_det.ssdn2 + o_det.ssdn5 - round(o_det.ssdn8, 2);
        Else
          o_det.ssdn16 := o_det.ssdn2 + o_det.ssdn5 -
                          round(o_det.ssdn8 * ((o_det.ssdn2 + o_det.ssdn5) /
                                (o_det.ssdn1 + o_det.ssdn4)),
                                2);
        End If;
        o_det.ssdn6  := o_det.ssdn15 - o_det.ssdn16;
        o_det.ssdn37 := o_det.ssdn1 + o_det.ssdn4 - o_det.ssdn8;
        If b_isqs = '0' Then
          Insert Into salecostday_supset
            Select Distinct scddate,
                            scdmkt,
                            scdmfid,
                            scdcatid,
                            scdsupid,
                            scdwmid,
                            scdtaxtype,
                            scdxstax,
                            scdhsrq,
                            scdmd,
                            scdbrand,
                            scdtmtype,
                            'N',
                            b_hd.sshbillno,
                            '1',
                            scdjjtax,
                            i_contno 
              From salecostday
             Where scdmkt = i_mkt
               And scdmfid = i_mfid
               And scdsupid = i_supid
               And scdwmid = i_wmid
               And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) >=
                   i_startdate
               And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) <=
                   i_enddate
               And Not Exists
             (Select *
                      From salecostday_supset
                     Where scdsdate = scddate
                       And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                       And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                       And scdscatid = scdcatid
                       And scdssupid = scdsupid
                       And scdswmid = scdwmid
                       And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                       And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                       And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                       And scdsmd = scdmd
                       And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                       And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                       and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax)
               And scdbrand In (Select cmfbrand
                                  From contmanaframe
                                 Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                                   And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                                   And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                                   And cmfbrand <> '0');
          --更新已结算其它销售
          Insert Into salecostday_supset
            Select Distinct ssddate,
                            ssdmkt,
                            ssdmfid,
                            ssdcatid,
                            ssdsupid,
                            ssdwmid,
                            ssdtaxtype,
                            ssdxstax,
                            ssdhsrq,
                            ssdmd,
                            ssdbrand,
                            ssdtmtype,
                            'N',
                            b_hd.sshbillno,
                            '2',
                            ssdxstax, -- wj 暂时记录销售税率
                            i_contno
              From salesupday
             Where ssdmkt = i_mkt
               And ssdmfid = i_mfid
               And ssdsupid = i_supid
               And ssdwmid = i_wmid
               And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) >=
                   i_startdate
               And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, SsdDate, SsdHsrq) <=
                   i_enddate
               And Not Exists
             (Select *
                      From salecostday_supset
                     Where scdsdate = ssddate
                       And scdsmkt = ssdmkt
                       And scdsmfid = ssdmfid
                       And scdscatid = ssdcatid
                       And scdssupid = ssdsupid
                       And scdswmid = ssdwmid
                       And scdstaxtype = ssdtaxtype
                       And scdsxstax = ssdxstax
                       And scdshsrq = ssdhsrq
                       And scdsbrand = ssdbrand
                       And scdstmtype = ssdtmtype)
               And ssdbrand In (Select cmfbrand
                                  From contmanaframe
                                 Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                                   And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                                   And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                                   And cmfbrand <> '0');
        End If;
    End;
  End saledate;
  --统计日期段销售
  Procedure saledate(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                     i_supid     In Varchar2,
                     i_wmid      In Char,
                     i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                     i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                     i_startdate In Date,
                     i_enddate   In Date,
                     i_flag      In Char Default 'N', --是否统计已结算销售数据
                     i_unionflag In Char Default 'N',
                     o_ssd       In Out tssd) Is
    lbrand contmanaframe.cmfbrand%Type;
  Begin
    -- 取得品牌
    Begin
      Select cmfbrand
        Into lbrand
        From contmanaframe
       Where cmfcontno = i_contno
         And cmfmfid = i_mfid
         And cmfmarket = i_mkt
         And cmfbrand = '0';
      --全部品牌
      Select --正常商品
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xshsjjje + pfhsjjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjje + pfbhsjjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xssjje + pfsjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjad + pfbhsjjad)), 0),
       0,
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xssr + pfsr)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xszzse + pfzzse)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * 0), 0),
       --保底特卖
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xshsjjje + pfhsjjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjje + pfbhsjjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xssjje + pfsjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjad + pfbhsjjad)), 0),
       0,
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xssr + pfsr)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xszzse + pfzzse)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * 0), 0),
       --超额特卖
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xshsjjje + pfhsjjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjje + pfbhsjjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xssjje + pfsjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjad + pfbhsjjad)), 0),
       0,
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xssr + pfsr)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xszzse + pfzzse)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * 0), 0),
       --普通特卖
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xshsjjje + pfhsjjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjje + pfbhsjjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xssjje + pfsjje)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjad + pfbhsjjad)), 0),
       0,
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xssr + pfsr)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xszzse + pfzzse)), 0),
       nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * 0), 0) /*,
             SCDXSTAX,
             SCDXSTAX,
             SCDXSTAX,
             SCDXSTAX*/
        Into o_ssd.det0.ssdn1,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn2,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn3,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn4,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn5,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn6,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn7,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn8,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn9,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn10,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn11,
             o_ssd.det0.ssdn77,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn1,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn2,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn3,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn4,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn5,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn6,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn7,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn8,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn9,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn10,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn11,
             o_ssd.det1.ssdn77,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn1,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn2,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn3,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn4,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn5,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn6,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn7,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn8,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn9,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn10,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn11,
             o_ssd.det2.ssdn77,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn1,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn2,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn3,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn4,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn5,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn6,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn7,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn8,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn9,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn10,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn11,
             o_ssd.det3.ssdn77 /*,
                   o_ssd.det0.ssdn80,
                   o_ssd.det1.ssdn80,
                   o_ssd.det2.ssdn80,
                   o_ssd.det3.ssdn80*/
        From (Select decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl),
                     scdtmtype,
                     --fgetmaxsl(i_contno,i_supid,i_wmid,i_mkt,i_mfid,i_startdate,i_enddate,i_flag) SCDXSTAX,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xshsjjje, 0)), 2) xshsjjje,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xsbhsjjje, 0)), 2) xsbhsjjje,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xssjje, 0)), 2) xssjje,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xshsjjad, 0)), 2) xshsjjad,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xsbhsjjad, 0)), 2) xsbhsjjad,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xstotzk, 0)), 2) xstotzk,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xssupzk, 0)), 2) xssupzk,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xssr, 0)), 2) xssr,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xsjjml, 0)), 2) xsjjml,
                     round(Sum(nvl(xszzse, 0)), 2) xszzse,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pfhsjjje, 0)), 2) pfhsjjje,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pfbhsjjje, 0)), 2) pfbhsjjje,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pfsjje, 0)), 2) pfsjje,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pfhsjjad, 0)), 2) pfhsjjad,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pfbhsjjad, 0)), 2) pfbhsjjad,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pftotzk, 0)), 2) pftotzk,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pfsupzk, 0)), 2) pfsupzk,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pfsr, 0)), 2) pfsr,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pfjjml, 0)), 2) pfjjml,
                     round(Sum(nvl(pfzzse, 0)), 2) pfzzse,
                     round(Sum(nvl(scdzfsupzk, 0)), 2) scdzfsupzk,
                     0 scdzfje
                From salecostday
               Where scdmkt = i_mkt
                 And scdmfid = i_mfid
                 And scdsupid = i_supid
                 And scdwmid = i_wmid
                 And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) >=
                     i_startdate
                 And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) <=
                     i_enddate
                 And (b_isqs = '1' Or i_flag = 'Y' Or
                     (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                      (Select *
                          From salecostday_supset
                         Where b_isqs = '0'
                           And scdsdate = scddate
                           And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                           And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                           And scdscatid = scdcatid
                           And scdssupid = scdsupid
                           And scdswmid = scdwmid
                           And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                           And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                           And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                           And scdsmd = scdmd
                           And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                           And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                           and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                           And scdsjsflag = 'Y')))
                And (b_isqs = '1' Or i_flag = 'Y' Or
                     (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                      (Select *
                          From salecostday_supset
                         Where b_isqs = '0'
                           And scdsdate = scddate
                           And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                           And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                           And scdscatid = scdcatid
                           And scdssupid = scdsupid
                           And scdswmid = scdwmid
                           And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                           And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                           And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                           And scdsmd = scdmd
                           And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                           And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                           and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                           And (scdsjsflag = 'N' and scdscontno<>i_contno))))           
               Group By decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl), scdtmtype --,fgetmaxsl(i_contno,i_supid,i_wmid,i_mkt,i_mfid,i_startdate,i_enddate,i_flag)
              )
      --group by SCDXSTAX
      ;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        --部分品牌
        Select --正常商品
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xshsjjje + pfhsjjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjje + pfbhsjjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xssjje + pfsjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjad + pfbhsjjad)), 0),
         0,
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xssr + pfsr)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * (xszzse + pfzzse)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '0', 1, 0) * 0), 0),
         --保底特卖
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xshsjjje + pfhsjjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjje + pfbhsjjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xssjje + pfsjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjad + pfbhsjjad)), 0),
         0,
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xssr + pfsr)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * (xszzse + pfzzse)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '1', 1, 0) * 0), 0),
         --超额特卖
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xshsjjje + pfhsjjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjje + pfbhsjjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xssjje + pfsjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjad + pfbhsjjad)), 0),
         0,
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xssr + pfsr)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * (xszzse + pfzzse)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '2', 1, 0) * 0), 0),
         --普通特卖
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xshsjjje + pfhsjjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjje + pfbhsjjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xssjje + pfsjje)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xsbhsjjad + pfbhsjjad)), 0),
         0,
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xssr + pfsr)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * (xszzse + pfzzse)), 0),
         nvl(Sum(decode(scdtmtype, '3', 1, 0) * 0), 0) /*,
                                 SCDXSTAX,
                                 SCDXSTAX,
                                 SCDXSTAX,
                                 SCDXSTAX*/
          Into o_ssd.det0.ssdn1,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn2,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn3,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn4,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn5,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn6,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn7,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn8,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn9,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn10,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn11,
               o_ssd.det0.ssdn77,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn1,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn2,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn3,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn4,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn5,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn6,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn7,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn8,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn9,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn10,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn11,
               o_ssd.det1.ssdn77,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn1,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn2,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn3,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn4,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn5,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn6,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn7,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn8,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn9,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn10,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn11,
               o_ssd.det2.ssdn77,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn1,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn2,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn3,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn4,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn5,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn6,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn7,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn8,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn9,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn10,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn11,
               o_ssd.det3.ssdn77 /*,
                                       o_ssd.det0.ssdn80,
                                       o_ssd.det1.ssdn80,
                                       o_ssd.det2.ssdn80,
                                       o_ssd.det3.ssdn80*/
          From (Select decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl),
                       scdtmtype,
                       --fgetmaxsl(i_contno,i_supid,i_wmid,i_mkt,i_mfid,i_startdate,i_enddate,i_flag) SCDXSTAX,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xshsjjje, 0)), 2) xshsjjje,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xsbhsjjje, 0)), 2) xsbhsjjje,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xssjje, 0)), 2) xssjje,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xshsjjad, 0)), 2) xshsjjad,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xsbhsjjad, 0)), 2) xsbhsjjad,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xstotzk, 0)), 2) xstotzk,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xssupzk, 0)), 2) xssupzk,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xssr, 0)), 2) xssr,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xsjjml, 0)), 2) xsjjml,
                       round(Sum(nvl(xszzse, 0)), 2) xszzse,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pfhsjjje, 0)), 2) pfhsjjje,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pfbhsjjje, 0)), 2) pfbhsjjje,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pfsjje, 0)), 2) pfsjje,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pfhsjjad, 0)), 2) pfhsjjad,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pfbhsjjad, 0)), 2) pfbhsjjad,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pftotzk, 0)), 2) pftotzk,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pfsupzk, 0)), 2) pfsupzk,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pfsr, 0)), 2) pfsr,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pfjjml, 0)), 2) pfjjml,
                       round(Sum(nvl(pfzzse, 0)), 2) pfzzse,
                       round(Sum(nvl(scdzfsupzk, 0)), 2) scdzfsupzk,
                       0 scdzfje
                  From SaleCostDay
                 Where scdmkt = i_mkt
                   And scdmfid = i_mfid
                   And scdsupid = i_supid
                   And scdwmid = i_wmid
                   And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) >=
                       i_startdate
                   And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) <=
                       i_enddate
                   And (b_isqs = '1' Or i_flag = 'Y' Or
                       (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                        (Select *
                            From salecostday_supset
                           Where b_isqs = '0'
                             And scdsdate = scddate
                             And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                             And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                             And scdscatid = scdcatid
                             And scdssupid = scdsupid
                             And scdswmid = scdwmid
