                             And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                             And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                             And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                             And scdsmd = scdmd
                             And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                             And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                             And scdsjsflag = 'Y'
                             and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax)))
                   And (b_isqs = '1' Or i_flag = 'Y' Or
                       (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                        (Select *
                            From salecostday_supset
                           Where b_isqs = '0'
                             And scdsdate = scddate
                             And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                             And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                             And scdscatid = scdcatid
                             And scdssupid = scdsupid
                             And scdswmid = scdwmid
                             And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                             And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                             And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                             And scdsmd = scdmd
                             And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                             And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                             And (scdsjsflag = 'N' and scdscontno<>i_contno)
                             and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax)))          
                   And scdbrand In (Select cmfbrand
                                      From contmanaframe
                                     Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                                       And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                                       And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                                       And cmfbrand <> '0')
                 Group By decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl), scdtmtype /*,SCDXSTAX*/
                )
        --group by SCDXSTAX
        ;
    End;
  End saledate;

  --平衡点考核时通过手工费用退回的保底提成需要加入核算
  Procedure AdjQsByCharge(i_contno In Varchar2,
                          i_supid  In Varchar2,
                          i_wmid   In Char,
                          i_mkt    In Varchar2,
                          i_mfid   In Varchar2,
                          o_adjamt Out Number) Is
  
  Begin
    Select Nvl(Sum(sscmoney), 0)
      Into o_adjamt
      From supsetcharge
     Where ssccontno In
           (i_contno, Decode(b_isqs, '1', b_unioncontno, Null))
       And sscsupid = i_supid
       And sscwmid = i_wmid
       And sscmarket = i_mkt
       And sscmfid = i_mfid
       And ssctype = '1'
       And sscflag = 'Y'
       And Nvl(sscisqs, 'N') <> 'Y'
       And sscid = AdjQsChargeId;
    --更新费用已清算状态
    Update supsetcharge
       Set sscisqs = 'Y', sscqssettleno = b_hd.sshbillno
     Where ssccontno In
           (i_contno, Decode(b_isqs, '1', b_unioncontno, Null))
       And sscsupid = i_supid
       And sscwmid = i_wmid
       And sscmarket = i_mkt
       And sscmfid = i_mfid
       And ssctype = '1'
       And sscflag = 'Y'
       And Nvl(sscisqs, 'N') <> 'Y'
       And sscid = AdjQsChargeId;
  End AdjQsByCharge;

  --梦之岛客户化过程
  --联合老系统数据保底
  Procedure SaleDateUnion(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                          i_supid     In Varchar2,
                          i_wmid      In Char,
                          i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                          i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                          i_startdate In Date,
                          i_enddate   In Date,
                          o_sr        Out Number,
                          o_ml        Out Number) Is
  
  Begin
    Select Nvl(Sum(Round(Nvl(sr, 0), 2)), 0),
           Nvl(Sum(Round(Nvl(ml, 0), 2)), 0)
      Into o_sr, o_ml
      From his_saledata
     Where supid = i_supid
       And wmid = i_wmid
       And contno In (i_contno, Decode(b_isqs, '1', b_unioncontno, Null))
       And mkt = i_mkt
       And period >= to_char(i_startdate, 'YYYYMM')
       And period <= to_char(i_enddate, 'YYYYMM');
  End SaleDateUnion;

  --梦之岛客户化过程
  --联合老系统数据清算
  Procedure SaleDateUnion_Qs(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                             i_supid     In Varchar2,
                             i_wmid      In Char,
                             i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                             i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                             i_startdate In Date,
                             i_enddate   In Date,
                             o_tc        Out Number) Is
  Begin
    /*由于存在跨合同的联合清算，系统只允许清算一次，取消清算时间段限制*/
    Select Nvl(Sum(Nvl(tc, 0)), 0)
      Into o_tc
      From his_salebdce a
     Where supid = i_supid
       And wmid = i_wmid
       And contno = i_contno
       And mkt = i_mkt
       And Exists (Select 'x'
              From his_contbd b
             Where b.supid = a.supid
               And b.contno = a.contno
               And b.mkt = a.mkt
               And to_char(b.edate, 'YYYYMM') = a.period
               And flag = 'Y')
    /*AND period >= to_char(i_startdate,'YYYYMM')
    AND period <= to_char(i_enddate,'YYYYMM')*/
    ;
  End SaleDateUnion_Qs;

  Procedure ins_ssd_bykl(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                         i_supid     In Varchar2,
                         i_wmid      In Char,
                         i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                         i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                         i_startdate In Date,
                         i_enddate   In Date) Is
    lbrand      contmanaframe.cmfbrand%Type;
    row_ssd     supsettledet%Rowtype;
    l_startdate Date;
    l_msg       Varchar2(1000);
  Begin
    If b_isqs = '0' Then
      --考虑到合同变更柜组引起的柜组未结销售，因此最长允许结算到上次结算前6个月
      l_startdate := add_months(i_startdate, -6);
    Else
      l_startdate := i_startdate;
    End If;
    row_ssd.ssdbillno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
    row_ssd.ssdmarket   := i_mkt;
    row_ssd.ssdmfid     := i_mfid;
    row_ssd.ssdwmid     := i_wmid;
    row_ssd.ssdcontno   := i_contno;
    row_ssd.ssdybillno  := Null;
    row_ssd.ssdydjbh    := Null;
    row_ssd.ssdlastdate := i_startdate;
    row_ssd.ssdthisdate := i_enddate;
    row_ssd.ssdvc5      := '3';
    row_ssd.ssdvc6      := '0';
    -- 取得品牌
    Begin
      Select cmfbrand
        Into lbrand
        From contmanaframe
       Where cmfcontno = i_contno
         And cmfmfid = i_mfid
         And cmfmarket = i_mkt
         And cmfbrand = '0';
      --全部品牌
      For vr In (Select decode(scdtmtype,
                               '2',
                               '特卖超额',
                               '3',
                               '普通特卖',
                               '保底超额') gd,
                        decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl) scdkl,
                        SCDXSTAX,
                        round(nvl(Sum((xssr + pfsr )), 0),
                              2) sr,
                        
                        round(nvl(Sum((xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0), 2) cb,
                        round(nvl(Sum((xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0), 2) zzk,
                        round(nvl(Sum((xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0), 2) supzk,
                        round(nvl(Sum((xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0), 2) tz,
                        round(nvl(Sum((xssjje + pfsjje)), 0), 2) sjje,
                        0 bjsr,
                         scdjjtax
                   From salecostday
                  Where scdmkt = i_mkt
                    And scdmfid = i_mfid
                    And scdsupid = i_supid
                    And scdwmid = i_wmid
                    And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) >=
                        l_startdate
                    And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) <=
                        i_enddate
                    And (b_isqs = '1' Or
                        (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                         (Select *
                             From salecostday_supset
                            Where b_isqs = '0'
                              And scdsdate = scddate
                              And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                              And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                              And scdscatid = scdcatid
                              And scdssupid = scdsupid
                              And scdswmid = scdwmid
                              And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                              And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                              And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                              And scdsmd = scdmd
                              And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                              And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                               and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                              And scdsjsflag = 'Y')))
                   And (b_isqs = '1' Or
                        (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                         (Select *
                             From salecostday_supset
                            Where b_isqs = '0'
                              And scdsdate = scddate
                              And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                              And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                              And scdscatid = scdcatid
                              And scdssupid = scdsupid
                              And scdswmid = scdwmid
                              And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                              And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                              And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                              And scdsmd = scdmd
                              And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                              And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                               and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                              And (scdsjsflag = 'N'and scdscontno<>i_contno))))           
                  Group By decode(scdtmtype,
                                  '2',
                                  '特卖超额',
                                  '3',
                                  '普通特卖',
                                  '保底超额'),
                           decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl),
                           SCDXSTAX,
                           scdjjtax
                  Order By 2) Loop
        initdetrow(row_ssd);
        row_ssd.ssdn61 := vr.sr;
        If row_ssd.ssdwmid = '2' Then
          If vr.sjje = 0 Then
            row_ssd.ssdn62 := 0;
          Else
            row_ssd.ssdn62 := round(vr.cb / vr.sjje, 4);
          End If;
        Else
          row_ssd.ssdn62 := vr.scdkl;
        End If;
        row_ssd.ssdn63   := vr.cb;
        row_ssd.ssdn64   := vr.zzk;
        row_ssd.ssdn65   := vr.supzk;
        row_ssd.ssdn66   := vr.tz;
        row_ssd.ssdn67   := vr.sjje;
        row_ssd.ssdn77   := vr.bjsr;
        row_ssd.ssdvc10  := vr.gd;
        b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
        row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
        row_ssd.ssdn80   := vr.scdjjtax;
        insertdetail(row_ssd);
      End Loop;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        l_msg := Sqlerrm;
        --部分品牌
        For vr In (Select decode(scdtmtype,
                                 '2',
                                 '特卖超额',
                                 '3',
                                 '普通特卖',
                                 '保底超额') gd,
                          decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl) scdkl,
                          SCDXSTAX,
                          round(nvl(Sum((xssr + pfsr )), 0),
                                2) sr,
                          round(nvl(Sum((xsjjml + pfjjml)), 0), 2) cb,
                          round(nvl(Sum((xstotzk + pftotzk)), 0), 2) zzk,
                          round(nvl(Sum((xssupzk + pfsupzk)), 0), 2) supzk,
                          round(nvl(Sum((xshsjjad + pfhsjjad)), 0), 2) tz,
                          round(nvl(Sum((xssjje + pfsjje)), 0), 2) sjje,
                          0 bjsr,
                          scdjjtax
                     From salecostday
                    Where scdmkt = i_mkt
                      And scdmfid = i_mfid
                      And scdsupid = i_supid
                      And scdwmid = i_wmid
                      And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) >=
                          l_startdate
                      And Decode(b_DateType, DateType_FS, ScdDate, scdhsrq) <=
                          i_enddate
                      And (b_isqs = '1' Or
                          (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                           (Select *
                               From salecostday_supset
                              Where b_isqs = '0'
                                And scdsdate = scddate
                                And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                                And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                                And scdscatid = scdcatid
                                And scdssupid = scdsupid
                                And scdswmid = scdwmid
                                And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                                And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                                And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                                And scdsmd = scdmd
                                And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                                And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                                 and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                                And scdsjsflag = 'Y')))
                      And (b_isqs = '1' Or
                          (b_isqs = '0' And Not Exists
                           (Select *
                               From salecostday_supset
                              Where b_isqs = '0'
                                And scdsdate = scddate
                                And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                                And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                                And scdscatid = scdcatid
                                And scdssupid = scdsupid
                                And scdswmid = scdwmid
                                And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                                And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                                And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                                And scdsmd = scdmd
                                And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                                And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                                 and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                                And (scdsjsflag = 'N'and scdscontno<>i_contno))))          
                      And scdbrand In (Select cmfbrand
                                         From contmanaframe
                                        Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                                          And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                                          And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                                          And cmfbrand <> '0')
                    Group By decode(scdtmtype,
                                    '2',
                                    '特卖超额',
                                    '3',
                                    '普通特卖',
                                    '保底超额'),
                             decode(scdwmid, '2', 0, scdkl),
                             SCDXSTAX,
                             scdjjtax
                    Order By 2) Loop
          initdetrow(row_ssd);
          row_ssd.ssdn61   := vr.sr;
          row_ssd.ssdn62   := vr.scdkl;
          row_ssd.ssdn63   := vr.cb;
          row_ssd.ssdn64   := vr.zzk;
          row_ssd.ssdn65   := vr.supzk;
          row_ssd.ssdn66   := vr.tz;
          row_ssd.ssdn67   := vr.sjje;
          row_ssd.ssdn77   := vr.bjsr;
          row_ssd.ssdvc10  := vr.gd;
          b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
          row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
          row_ssd.ssdn80   := vr.scdjjtax;
          insertdetail(row_ssd);
        End Loop;
    End;
  End ins_ssd_bykl;

  Procedure InitContBd(i_contno In Varchar2,
                       i_mkt    In Varchar2,
                       i_mfid   In Varchar2) Is
  Begin
    SettleSupExt.Sp_init_Bd(i_Contno, i_Mkt, i_Mfid);
  End;

  --得到保底时间范围
  Procedure SaleBdRange(i_contno      In Varchar2,
                        i_mkt         In Varchar2,
                        i_mfid        In Varchar2,
                        i_startdate   In Date,
                        i_enddate     In Date,
                        o_isbd        Out Char,
                        o_bdstartdate Out Date,
                        o_bdenddate   Out Date) Is
    Cursor cur_bd Is
      Select *
        From contbd
       Where cbcontno = i_contno
         And cbflag = 'Y'
         And cbmkt = i_mkt
         And (cbmfid = i_mfid or cbmfid = '0')
         And cbeffdate <= i_enddate
       Order By cblapdate desc;
    l_isenddate Boolean;
    l_seq       Number;
    row_lastbd  contbd%Rowtype;
  Begin
    o_isbd      := 'N';
    l_isenddate := False;
    initbd;
    l_seq := 1;
    For row_bd In cur_bd Loop
      If Not l_isenddate And row_bd.cbisrunbd = 'Y' And
         Nvl(row_bd.cbisbd, 'N') <> 'Y' And row_bd.cblapdate <= i_enddate Then
        o_bdenddate := row_bd.cblapdate;
        l_isenddate := True;
        o_isbd      := 'Y';
      End If;
      If Nvl(row_bd.cbisbd, 'N') = 'Y' Then
        --允许跨帐期保底
        --EXIT;
        --记录跳跃保底点
        If o_bdstartdate Is Not Null And o_bdenddate Is Not Null Then
          addbd(l_seq, o_bdstartdate, o_bdenddate);
        End If;
        l_isenddate   := False;
        o_bdstartdate := Null;
        o_bdenddate   := Null;
      Elsif o_bdstartdate Is Not Null And Nvl(row_bd.cbisbd, 'N') <> 'Y' And
            row_bd.cbisrunbd = 'Y' Then
        --记录上一个相邻的保底点
        If o_bdstartdate Is Not Null And o_bdenddate Is Not Null Then
          addbd(l_seq, o_bdstartdate, o_bdenddate);
        End If;
        l_seq         := l_seq + 1;
        o_bdenddate   := row_bd.cblapdate;
        o_bdstartdate := row_bd.cbeffdate;
        SettleSupExt.Sp_SetQ_Bd(i_ContNo, Row_Bd.Cbseqno);
      Else
        If l_isenddate Then
          o_bdstartdate := row_bd.cbeffdate;
          SettleSupExt.Sp_SetQ_Bd(i_ContNo, Row_Bd.Cbseqno);
        Else
          o_isbd := 'N';
        End If;
      End If;
    End Loop;
    --记录最后一个保底点
    If o_bdstartdate Is Not Null And o_bdenddate Is Not Null Then
      addbd(l_seq, o_bdstartdate, o_bdenddate);
    End If;
    If b_bd.COUNT > 0 Then
      sortbd;
    End If;
    If o_isbd = 'N' Then
      o_bdstartdate := Null;
      o_bdenddate   := Null;
    End If;
  End SaleBdRange;

  /*联合合同清算
    1.本期结算是否进行联合合同清算
    2.如本期结算需联合合同清算，则获得联合合同号
  */
  Procedure GetUnionBdCont(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                           i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                           i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                           i_startdate In Date,
                           i_enddate   In Date) Is
    l_unionqsdate Date;
  Begin
    If b_cont.cmchar4 = 'Y' And b_cont.cmchar5 Is Not Null Then
      Select Max(cblapdate)
        Into l_unionqsdate
        From contbd
       Where cbcontno = i_contno
         And cbflag = 'Y'
         And cbmkt = i_mkt
         And cbmfid = i_mfid
         And cbisrunqs = 'Y'
         And Nvl(cbisqs, 'N') <> 'Y';
      If l_unionqsdate Is Not Null Then
        If i_enddate >= l_unionqsdate Then
          b_unioncontno := b_cont.cmchar5;
        End If;
      End If;
    End If;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      b_unioncontno := Null;
  End GetUnionBdCont;

  --得到清算的时间范围
  /*迁移数据处理：
  1.在第一次平衡点考核时核算迁移期间
  2.要判断要核算的迁移期间不能与本系统期间重叠，如果重叠不计算迁移期间
  3.支持2份合同联合平衡点考核*/
  Procedure SaleQsRange(i_contno      In Varchar2,
                        i_mkt         In Varchar2,
                        i_mfid        In Varchar2,
                        i_startdate   In Date,
                        i_enddate     In Date,
                        o_isqs        Out Char,
                        o_qsstartdate Out Date,
                        o_qsenddate   Out Date) Is
    Cursor cur_qs Is
      Select *
        From contbd
       Where cbcontno In (i_contno, b_unioncontno)
         And cbflag = 'Y'
         And cbmkt = i_mkt
         And cbmfid = i_mfid
         And cbeffdate <= i_enddate
       Order By cblapdate Desc;
    l_isenddate      Boolean;
    l_ishisqs        Number;
    l_hisqsstartdate Date;
    l_seq            Number;
    l_unionstartdate Date;
    l_unionenddate   Date;
    l_isunion        Boolean;
    i                Number;
  Begin
    l_unionstartdate := Null;
    l_unionenddate   := Null;
    o_isqs           := 'N';
    l_isenddate      := False;
    initqs;
    l_seq     := 1;
    l_isunion := False;
    For row_qs In cur_qs Loop
      If Not l_isenddate And row_qs.cbisrunqs = 'Y' And
         Nvl(row_qs.cbisqs, 'N') <> 'Y' And row_qs.cblapdate <= i_enddate Then
        o_qsenddate := row_qs.cblapdate;
        l_isenddate := True;
        o_isqs      := 'Y';
        If l_unionenddate Is Null Then
          l_unionenddate := o_qsenddate;
        End If;
      End If;
      If Nvl(row_qs.cbisqs, 'N') = 'Y' Then
        --允许跨帐期保底
        --EXIT;
        --记录跳跃保底点
        If o_qsstartdate Is Not Null And o_qsenddate Is Not Null Then
          --属于联合保底合同的清算不处理
          If Not (fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, o_qsstartdate) = 'Y' And
              fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, o_qsenddate) = 'Y') Then
            addqs(l_seq, o_qsstartdate, o_qsenddate, 'N');
          End If;
        End If;
        If row_qs.cbcontno = b_unioncontno Then
          l_unionstartdate := row_qs.cbeffdate;
        End If;
        l_isenddate   := False;
        o_qsstartdate := Null;
        o_qsenddate   := Null;
      Elsif (o_qsstartdate Is Not Null And Nvl(row_qs.cbisqs, 'N') <> 'Y' And
            row_qs.cbisrunqs = 'Y') Then
        --记录上一个相邻的保底点
        If o_qsstartdate Is Not Null And o_qsenddate Is Not Null Then
          If Not (fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, o_qsstartdate) = 'Y' And
              fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, o_qsenddate) = 'Y') Then
            addqs(l_seq, o_qsstartdate, o_qsenddate, 'N');
          End If;
        End If;
        l_seq         := l_seq + 1;
        o_qsenddate   := row_qs.cblapdate;
        o_qsstartdate := row_qs.cbeffdate;
        If row_qs.cbcontno = b_unioncontno Then
          l_unionstartdate := row_qs.cbeffdate;
        End If;
        SettleSupExt.Sp_SetQ_Qs(i_ContNo, Row_qs.Cbseqno);
      Elsif row_qs.cbcontno = b_unioncontno And Not l_isunion Then
        l_isunion := True;
        --记录上一个相邻的保底点
        If o_qsstartdate Is Not Null And o_qsenddate Is Not Null Then
          If Not (fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, o_qsstartdate) = 'Y' And
              fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, o_qsenddate) = 'Y') Then
            addqs(l_seq, o_qsstartdate, o_qsenddate, 'N');
          End If;
        End If;
        l_seq         := l_seq + 1;
        o_qsenddate   := row_qs.cblapdate;
        o_qsstartdate := row_qs.cbeffdate;
        If row_qs.cbcontno = b_unioncontno Then
          l_unionstartdate := row_qs.cbeffdate;
        End If;
      Else
        If l_isenddate Then
          o_qsstartdate := row_qs.cbeffdate;
          If row_qs.cbcontno = b_unioncontno Then
            l_unionstartdate := row_qs.cbeffdate;
          End If;
          SettleSupExt.Sp_SetQ_Qs(i_ContNo, Row_qs.Cbseqno);
        Else
          o_isqs := 'N';
        End If;
      End If;
    End Loop;
  
    If o_isqs = 'N' Then
      o_qsstartdate := Null;
      o_qsenddate   := Null;
    Else
      Select Count(*)
        Into l_ishisqs
        From contbd
       Where cbcontno In (i_contno, b_unioncontno)
         And cbmkt = i_mkt
         And cbmfid = i_mfid
         And cbisrunqs = 'Y'
         And Nvl(cbisqs, 'N') = 'Y';
      If l_ishisqs <= 0 Then
        Select Min(sdate)
          Into l_hisqsstartdate
          From his_contbd
         Where contno = i_contno
           And mkt = i_mkt
           And mfid = i_mfid
           And flag = 'Y';
        If l_hisqsstartdate Is Not Null Then
          o_qsstartdate := l_hisqsstartdate;
        End If;
      End If;
    End If;
  
    --记录最后一个保底点
    If o_qsstartdate Is Not Null And o_qsenddate Is Not Null Then
      If Not (fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, o_qsstartdate) = 'Y' And
          fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, o_qsenddate) = 'Y') Then
        addqs(l_seq, o_qsstartdate, o_qsenddate, 'N');
      End If;
    End If;
    If b_qs.COUNT > 0 Then
      sortqs;
    End If;
    --增加联合合同清算期
    If b_unioncontno Is Not Null And l_unionstartdate Is Not Null And
       l_unionenddate Is Not Null Then
      l_isunion := True;
      For i In 1 .. b_qs.COUNT Loop
        If b_qs(i).startdate = l_unionstartdate And b_qs(i)
           .enddate = l_unionenddate Then
          l_isunion := False;
          Exit;
        End If;
      End Loop;
      If l_isunion Then
        l_seq := l_seq + 1;
        If Not (fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, l_unionstartdate) = 'Y' And
            fChkIsBdPeriod(b_unioncontno, l_unionenddate) = 'Y') Then
          addqs(l_seq, l_unionstartdate, l_unionenddate, 'Y');
        End If;
      End If;
    End If;
  End SaleQsRange;

  --统计销售及保底超额
  Procedure salestat(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                     i_supid     In Varchar2,
                     i_wmid      In Char,
                     i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                     i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                     i_startdate In Date,
                     i_enddate   In Date) Is
    Cursor cur_bd Is
      Select cbeffdate,
             cblapdate,
             greatest(cbeffdate, i_startdate) startdate,
             least(cblapdate, i_enddate) enddate,
             cbflag,
             cbsum,
             cbrate,
             cbsum1,
             cbrate1,
             cbsum2,
             cbrate2,
             cbsum3,
             cbrate3,
             cbsum4,
             cbrate4,
             cbsum5,
             cbrate5,
             cbsum6,
             cbrate6,
             cbisrunbd
        From contbd
       Where cbcontno = i_contno
         And cbflag = 'Y'
         And cbmkt = i_mkt
         And cbmfid = i_mfid
         And cbeffdate <= i_enddate
         And cblapdate >= i_startdate
         And b_isqs = '0'
         And b_ispop = '0'
      Union
      Select cqeffdate,
             cqlapdate,
             greatest(cqeffdate, i_startdate) startdate,
             least(cqlapdate, i_enddate) enddate,
             cqflag,
             cqsum,
             cqrate,
             cqsum1,
             cqrate1,
             cqsum2,
             cqrate2,
             cqsum3,
             cqrate3,
             cqsum4,
             cqrate4,
             cqsum5,
             cqrate5,
             cqsum6,
             cqrate6,
             'N'
        From contqs
       Where cqcontno = i_contno
         And cqflag = 'Y'
         And cqmkt = i_mkt
         And cqmfid = i_mfid
         And cqeffdate <= i_enddate
         And cqlapdate >= i_startdate
         And b_isqs = '1'
         And b_ispop = '0'
      Union
      Select PSHSDATE,
             pshedate,
             greatest(PSHSDATE, i_startdate) startdate,
             least(PSHEDATE, i_enddate) enddate,
             PSHSTATUS,
             PSHTARGETSALES,
             PSHBASEKL,
             PSHOUTAGEINDEX1,
             PSHOUTAGERATE1,
             PSHOUTAGEINDEX2,
             PSHOUTAGERATE2,
             PSHOUTAGEINDEX3,
             PSHOUTAGERATE3,
             PSHOUTAGEINDEX4,
             PSHOUTAGERATE4,
             PSHOUTAGEINDEX5,
             PSHOUTAGERATE5,
             0,
             0,
             'N'
        From Popsettlehead
       Where b_ispop = '1'
         And pshbillno = b_popbillno
       Order By startdate;
  
    l_ssd         tssd;
    l_startdate   Date;
    l_bdstartdate Date;
    l_bd          Boolean;
    l_ce          Boolean;
    l_tm          Boolean;
    l_bdmode      Char(1); --保底类型（1－自然月，2－保底期）
    l_cemode      Char(1); --超额类型（1－全额，2－差额）
    l_bdtype      Char(1); --保底方式（1－毛利保底，2－销售保底）
    l_fsdays      Number; --发生天数
    l_bddays      Number; --保底(超额)天数
    l_htkl        Number; --合同扣率
    l_bdsum       Number;
    l_bdml        Number;
    l_cesum       Number;
    l_tmsum       Number;
    i             Number;
    ldayrate      Number;
    row_ssd       supsettledet%Rowtype;
  Begin
    If i_wmid = '1' Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If b_isqs = '0' And b_ispop = '0' Then
      --考虑到合同变更柜组引起的柜组未结销售，因此最长允许结算到上次结算前6个月
      l_startdate := add_months(i_startdate, -6);
    Else
      l_startdate := i_startdate;
    End If;
    --统计整个结算期销售
    saledate(i_contno,
             i_supid,
             i_wmid,
             i_mkt,
             i_mfid,
             l_startdate,
             i_enddate,
             'N',
             b_detrow);
    b_detrow.ssdn28     := b_detrow.ssdn9 + b_detrow.ssdn77; --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
    b_detrow.ssdn29     := b_detrow.ssdn10; --销售应提(不含保底、超额)
    row_ssd.ssdbillno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
    row_ssd.ssdmarket   := i_mkt;
    row_ssd.ssdmfid     := i_mfid;
    row_ssd.ssdwmid     := i_wmid;
    row_ssd.ssdcontno   := i_contno;
    row_ssd.ssdybillno  := Null;
    row_ssd.ssdydjbh    := Null;
    row_ssd.ssdlastdate := i_startdate;
    row_ssd.ssdthisdate := i_enddate;
    row_ssd.ssdvc5      := '3';
    If i_wmid = '5' And b_ispop = '0' Then
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      --租赁算租金
    
      l_bddays := last_day(trunc(i_enddate)) - trunc(i_enddate, 'MON') + 1;
      l_fsdays := trunc(i_enddate) - trunc(i_startdate) + 1;
    
      Begin
        Select round(nvl(Sum(cmfcharter), 0) * l_fsdays / l_bddays, 2)
          Into b_detrow.ssdn23
          From contmanaframe
         Where cmfcontno = i_contno
           And cmfmarket = i_mkt
           And cmfmfid = i_mfid;
      Exception
        When Others Then
          b_detrow.ssdn23 := 0;
      End;
    
      If b_detrow.ssdn23 <> 0 Then
        row_ssd.ssdvc5   := '6';
        row_ssd.ssdn61   := 0;
        row_ssd.ssdn62   := 0;
        row_ssd.ssdn63   := b_detrow.ssdn23;
        row_ssd.ssdvc6   := '6';
        row_ssd.ssdvc10  := '租金[' ||
                            TO_CHAR(trunc(i_startdate), 'YYYYMMDD') || '-' ||
                            TO_CHAR(trunc(i_enddate), 'YYYYMMDD') || ']';
        b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
        row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
        insertdetail(row_ssd);
        row_ssd.ssdvc5 := '3';
      End If;
    End If;
    -- ELSE
  
    l_bdmode := b_cont.cmbysettle;
    l_cemode := b_cont.cmyfkmode;
    l_bdtype := b_cont.cmweek5;
    --代销联营统计保底超额
    For row_bd In cur_bd Loop
      --第一段时间向前推六个月
      If row_bd.startdate = i_startdate Then
        l_bdstartdate := l_startdate;
      Else
        l_bdstartdate := row_bd.startdate;
      End If;
      initdetrow(l_ssd.det0);
      initdetrow(l_ssd.det1);
      initdetrow(l_ssd.det2);
      initdetrow(l_ssd.det3);
      saledate(i_contno,
               i_supid,
               i_wmid,
               i_mkt,
               i_mfid,
               l_bdstartdate,
               row_bd.enddate,
               'N',
               'N',
               l_ssd);
      /* l_ssd.det0.ssdn80 :=fgetmaxsl(i_contno,i_supid,i_wmid,i_mkt,i_mfid,l_bdstartdate,row_bd.enddate,'N');
      l_ssd.det1.ssdn80 :=fgetmaxsl(i_contno,i_supid,i_wmid,i_mkt,i_mfid,l_bdstartdate,row_bd.enddate,'N');
      l_ssd.det2.ssdn80 :=fgetmaxsl(i_contno,i_supid,i_wmid,i_mkt,i_mfid,l_bdstartdate,row_bd.enddate,'N');
      l_ssd.det3.ssdn80 :=fgetmaxsl(i_contno,i_supid,i_wmid,i_mkt,i_mfid,l_bdstartdate,row_bd.enddate,'N');*/
      --初始化超额基数
      initce;
      If l_bdmode = bdmodemon Then
        --失效日期 - 生效日期 共多少个月 +
        --失效日期所有月天数占本月天数的比例 +
        --生效日期所有月剩余天数占本月天数的比例
        --
        ldayrate := trunc(months_between(trunc(row_bd.enddate, 'MON'),
                                         trunc(row_bd.startdate, 'MON'))) - 1 +
                    round((trunc(row_bd.enddate) -
                          trunc(row_bd.enddate, 'MON') + 1) /
                          (last_day(trunc(row_bd.enddate)) -
                          trunc(row_bd.enddate, 'MON') + 1),
                          10) + round((last_day(trunc(row_bd.startdate)) -
                                      trunc(row_bd.startdate) + 1) /
                                      (last_day(trunc(row_bd.startdate)) -
                                      trunc(row_bd.startdate, 'MON') + 1),
                                      10);
      
      Else
        --实际发生天数
        l_fsdays := trunc(row_bd.enddate) - trunc(row_bd.startdate) + 1;
        --按有效期保底取有效期天数
        l_bddays := trunc(row_bd.cblapdate) - trunc(row_bd.cbeffdate) + 1;
        ldayrate := round(l_fsdays / l_bddays, 10);
      End If;
      If b_ispop = '1' Then
        Select round((trunc(row_bd.enddate) - trunc(row_bd.startdate) + 1) /
                     (trunc(pshedate) - trunc(PSHSDATE) + 1),
                     10)
          Into ldayrate
          From Popsettlehead
         Where pshbillno = b_popbillno;
      End If;
      --保底超额计算
      l_bd    := False;
      l_ce    := False;
      l_tm    := False;
      l_bdsum := 0;
      l_cesum := 0;
      l_tmsum := 0;
      l_bdml  := 0;
      l_htkl  := nvl(row_bd.cbrate, 0);
    
      --设置超额基数数组
      If row_bd.cbsum1 > 0 And row_bd.cbrate1 >= 0 And
         l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 >=
         round(row_bd.cbsum1 * ldayrate, 2) Then
        addce(round(row_bd.cbsum1 * ldayrate, 2), row_bd.cbrate1);
      End If;
      If row_bd.cbsum2 > 0 And row_bd.cbrate2 >= 0 And
         l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 >=
         round(row_bd.cbsum2 * ldayrate, 2) Then
        addce(round(row_bd.cbsum2 * ldayrate, 2), row_bd.cbrate2);
      End If;
      If row_bd.cbsum3 > 0 And row_bd.cbrate3 >= 0 And
         l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 >=
         round(row_bd.cbsum3 * ldayrate, 2) Then
        addce(round(row_bd.cbsum3 * ldayrate, 2), row_bd.cbrate3);
      End If;
      If row_bd.cbsum4 > 0 And row_bd.cbrate4 >= 0 And
         l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 >=
         round(row_bd.cbsum4 * ldayrate, 2) Then
        addce(round(row_bd.cbsum4 * ldayrate, 2), row_bd.cbrate4);
      End If;
      If row_bd.cbsum5 > 0 And row_bd.cbrate5 >= 0 And
         l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 >=
         round(row_bd.cbsum5 * ldayrate, 2) Then
        addce(round(row_bd.cbsum5 * ldayrate, 2), row_bd.cbrate5);
      End If;
      sortce; --按基数从低到高排序
      If b_ce.COUNT > 0 Then
        --有超额
        /*If l_htkl Is Null Or l_htkl = 0 Then
          l_htkl := b_ce(1).cerate;
        End If;*/
        --超额只按正常商品收入比较
        If l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 >= b_ce(1).cesum Then
          l_ce := True;
        End If;
      End If;
      --有保底
      If row_bd.cbsum > 0 And row_bd.cbrate > 0 Then
        l_bdsum := round(row_bd.cbsum * ldayrate, 2);
        l_bdml  := round(l_bdsum * row_bd.cbrate, 2);
        If l_bdtype = bdtypeml Then
          --毛利保底,比较保底时按正常商品毛利＋保底特卖毛利
          If l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 < l_bdml Then
            l_bd := True;
            l_ce := False;
          End If;
        Elsif l_bdtype = BdTypeFb Then
          If l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 +
             l_ssd.det1.ssdn77 < l_bdsum Then
            l_bd   := True;
            l_ce   := False;
            l_bdml := -1 * round((l_bdsum -
                                 (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                                 (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77)) *
                                 row_bd.cbrate,
                                 2);
            l_bdml := l_bdml + l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10;
            If b_AllowNeg = 'N' And l_bdml < 0 Then
              l_bdml := 0;
            End If;
          End If;
        Else
          --销售保底,比较保底时按正常商品收入＋保底特卖收入
          If l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 +
             l_ssd.det1.ssdn77 < l_bdsum Then
            l_bd   := True;
            l_ce   := False;
            l_bdml := l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 +
                      round((l_bdsum -
                            (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                            (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77)) *
                            row_bd.cbrate,
                            2);
          End If;
        End If;
      End If;
      If i_wmid = '4' And row_bd.cbsum6 > 0 And row_bd.cbrate6 > 0 Then
        --有特卖超额
        l_tmsum := round(row_bd.cbsum6 * ldayrate, 2);
        --超额特卖收入
        If l_ssd.det2.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det2.ssdn77 >= l_tmsum Then
          l_tm := True;
        End If;
      End If;
      If l_ce And Not l_bd Then
        --超额
        b_detrow.ssdvc4 := l_cemode;
        -- b_detrow.ssdn80 := fgetmaxsl(i_contno,i_supid,i_wmid,i_mkt,i_mfid,l_bdstartdate,row_bd.enddate,'N');
        If l_cemode = cemodeqe Then
          --全额
          --[[[[ EORV-1026 =  =P~ 2018.11.06
          /*l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := round(l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 -
          (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) *
          (l_htkl - b_ce(b_ce.COUNT).cerate),
          2);*/
          l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 -
                               round((l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) *
                                     (l_htkl - b_ce(b_ce.COUNT).cerate),
                                     2);
          --]]]] ---------------------------
          initdetrow(row_ssd);
          row_ssd.ssdn61  := l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77;
          row_ssd.ssdn62  := - (l_htkl - b_ce(b_ce.COUNT).cerate);
          row_ssd.ssdn63  := round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
          row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '3';
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '让扣(' || to_char(b_ce(b_ce.COUNT).cesum) || '/' ||
                             to_char(b_ce(b_ce.COUNT).cerate * 100) || '%)';
          If b_ispop = '1' Then
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := row_ssd.ssdvc10 || '[促销结算单' || b_popbillno || ']';
          End If;
          b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
          row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
          insertdetail(row_ssd);
        Else
          --差额
          For i In Reverse 1 .. b_ce.COUNT Loop
            initdetrow(row_ssd);
            If i = b_ce.COUNT Then
              --[[[[ EORV-1026 =  =P~ 2018.11.06
              /*l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := round(l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 -
              ((l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 +
              l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) - b_ce(i)
              .cesum) *
              (l_htkl - b_ce(i).cerate),
              2);*/
              l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 -
                                   round(((l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 +
                                         l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) - b_ce(i)
                                         .cesum) *
                                         (l_htkl - b_ce(i).cerate),
                                         2);
              --]]]] ----------------------------
              row_ssd.ssdn61 := (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) - b_ce(i)
                               .cesum;
            Else
              l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 -
                                   round((b_ce(i + 1).cesum - b_ce(i).cesum) *
                                         (l_htkl - b_ce(i).cerate),
                                         2);
              row_ssd.ssdn61    := b_ce(i + 1).cesum - b_ce(i).cesum;
            End If;
            row_ssd.ssdn62  := - (l_htkl - b_ce(i).cerate);
            row_ssd.ssdn63  := round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
            row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '4';
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '让扣(' || to_char(b_ce(i).cesum) || '/' ||
                               to_char(b_ce(i).cerate * 100) || '%)';
            If b_ispop = '1' Then
              row_ssd.ssdvc10 := row_ssd.ssdvc10 || '[促销结算单' || b_popbillno || ']';
            End If;
            b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
            row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
            insertdetail(row_ssd);
          End Loop;
        End If;
        --(超额毛利+保底特卖毛利)低于保底毛利仍按保底计算
        If l_bdtype = bdtypeml And
           l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 < l_bdml Then
          l_bd := True;
          l_ce := False;
        Else
          b_detrow.ssdn26 := b_detrow.ssdn26 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn26;
          If b_ispop = '1' Then
            b_detrow.ssdn26 := b_detrow.ssdn26 - l_ssd.det0.ssdn10;
          End If;
          b_detrow.ssdn28 := b_detrow.ssdn28 -
                             (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77); --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
          b_detrow.ssdn29 := b_detrow.ssdn29 - l_ssd.det0.ssdn10; --销售应提(不含保底、超额)
        End If;
      End If;
      If l_bd And Not l_ce Then
        --保底
        --b_detrow.ssdn80 := fgetmaxsl(i_contno,i_supid,i_wmid,i_mkt,i_mfid,l_bdstartdate,row_bd.enddate,'N');
        b_detrow.ssdn23 := b_detrow.ssdn23 + l_bdml;
        b_detrow.ssdn28 := b_detrow.ssdn28 -
                           (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 +
                           l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77); --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
        b_detrow.ssdn29 := b_detrow.ssdn29 -
                           (l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10); --销售应提(不含保底、超额)
        --保底部分的结算明细
        Delete From supsettledet
         Where ssdbillno = b_hd.sshbillno
           And ssdwmid = i_wmid
           And ssdcontno = i_contno
           And ssdmarket = i_mkt
           And ssdmfid = i_mfid
           And ssdvc5 = '3'
           And b_ispop = 'N'
           And ssdvc6 In ('3', '4');
        initdetrow(row_ssd);
        If l_bdtype = bdtypeml Then
          row_ssd.ssdn61  := (l_bdsum -
                             (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                             (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77));
          row_ssd.ssdn62  := row_bd.cbrate;
          row_ssd.ssdn63  := l_bdml - l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 - l_ssd.det1.ssdn10;
          row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '1';
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '保扣差额(' || to_char(l_bdsum) || '/' ||
                             to_char(row_bd.cbrate * 100) || '%)';
        Elsif l_BdType = BdTypeFb Then
          --反保底
          row_ssd.ssdn61  := (l_bdsum -
                             (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                             (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77));
          row_ssd.ssdn62  := row_bd.cbrate;
          row_ssd.ssdn63  := -1 * round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
          row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '2';
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '反保底差额(' || to_char(l_bdsum) || '/' ||
                             to_char(row_bd.cbrate * 100) || '%)';
        Else
          row_ssd.ssdn61  := (l_bdsum -
                             (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                             (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77));
          row_ssd.ssdn62  := row_bd.cbrate;
          row_ssd.ssdn63  := round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
          row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '2';
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '保扣差额(' || to_char(l_bdsum) || '/' ||
                             to_char(row_bd.cbrate * 100) || '%)';
        End If;
        If b_ispop = '1' Then
          b_detrow.ssdn23 := b_detrow.ssdn23 - l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 -
                             l_ssd.det1.ssdn10;
        End If;
        If b_ispop = '1' Then
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := row_ssd.ssdvc10 || '[促销结算单' || b_popbillno || ']';
        End If;
        b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
        row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
        insertdetail(row_ssd);
      End If;
      If l_tm Then
        --特卖超额
        --[[[[ EORV-1026 =  =P~ 2018.11.06
        /*l_ssd.det2.ssdn26 := round(l_ssd.det2.ssdn10 -
        (l_ssd.det2.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det2.ssdn77) *
        (l_htkl - row_bd.cbrate6),
        2);*/
        l_ssd.det2.ssdn26 := l_ssd.det2.ssdn10 -
                             round((l_ssd.det2.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det2.ssdn77) *
                                   (l_htkl - row_bd.cbrate6),
                                   2);
        --]]]] ---------------------------                           
        b_detrow.ssdn26 := b_detrow.ssdn26 + l_ssd.det2.ssdn26;
        b_detrow.ssdn28 := b_detrow.ssdn28 -
                           (l_ssd.det2.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det2.ssdn77); --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
        b_detrow.ssdn29 := b_detrow.ssdn29 - l_ssd.det2.ssdn10; --销售应提(不含保底、超额)
        --特卖超额的特卖码结算明细
        initdetrow(row_ssd);
        row_ssd.ssdn61  := l_ssd.det2.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det2.ssdn77;
        row_ssd.ssdn62  := - (l_htkl - row_bd.cbrate6);
        row_ssd.ssdn63  := round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
        row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '5'; --特卖超额
        row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '让扣(' || to_char(row_bd.cbsum6) || '/' ||
                           to_char(row_bd.cbrate6 * 100) || '%)';
        If b_ispop = '1' Then
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := row_ssd.ssdvc10 || '[促销结算单' || b_popbillno || ']';
        End If;
        b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
        row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
        insertdetail(row_ssd);
      End If;
      If b_ispop = '1' Then
        b_detrow.ssdn9  := 0;
        b_detrow.ssdn77 := 0;
      End If;
      /*  b_hd.sshn1 := b_dettot.ssdn9;
      b_hd.sshn2 := b_dettot.ssdn1;
      b_hd.sshn3 := b_dettot.ssdn8;
      b_hd.sshn4 := b_dettot.ssdn4;
      
      b_hd.sshn7    := b_dettot.ssdn28; --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
      b_hd.sshn8    := b_dettot.ssdn29; --销售提成
      b_hd.sshogdje := b_dettot.ssdn10; --应提成金额
      b_hd.sshmgdje := b_dettot.ssdn23; --保底提成额
      b_hd.sshaqdje := b_dettot.ssdn26; --超额提成额+特卖超额*/
    End Loop;
    -- END IF;
  End salestat;

  --计算保底，梦之岛方式-按月定义，季度保底
  /*更新历史：
    1、暂时只考虑毛利保底，不支持销售保底和超额
    2、同时支持毛利保底和销售保底模式，但毛利保底时不支持超额
    3、毛利保底同时可以支持超额
  */
  Procedure SaleStatBdByRange(i_contno      In Varchar2,
                              i_supid       In Varchar2,
                              i_wmid        In Char,
                              i_mkt         In Varchar2,
                              i_mfid        In Varchar2,
                              i_startdate   In Date,
                              i_enddate     In Date,
                              i_isbd        In Char,
                              i_bdstartdate In Date,
                              i_bdenddate   In Date,
                              i_seq         In Number, --结算期标志
                              i_unionflag   In Char Default 'N',
                              o_bdtc        Out Number, --保底提成
                              o_xstc        Out Number, --销售提成
                              o_cetc        Out Number, --超额提成
                              o_xskhtc      Out Number --销售考核提成
                              ) Is
    l_ssd        tssd;
    l_ssdxs      tssd;
    l_startdate  Date;
    l_bdmode     Char(1); --保底类型（1－自然月，2－保底期）
    l_bdtype     Char(1); --保底方式（1－毛利保底，2－销售保底）
    l_bd         Boolean;
    l_ce         Boolean;
    l_xs         Boolean;
    l_bdml       Number;
    l_bdsum      Number;
    l_cesum1     Number;
    l_cesum2     Number;
    l_cesum3     Number;
    l_cesum4     Number;
    l_cesum5     Number;
    l_cesum6     Number;
    l_bdrate     Number(5, 4);
    l_cemode1    Char(1);
    l_cerate1    Number(5, 4);
    l_cemode2    Char(1);
    l_cerate2    Number(5, 4);
    l_cemode3    Char(1);
    l_cerate3    Number(5, 4);
    l_cemode4    Char(1);
    l_cerate4    Number(5, 4);
    l_cemode5    Char(1);
    l_cerate5    Number(5, 4);
    l_cemode6    Char(1);
    l_cerate6    Number(5, 4);
    l_cesalekh   number;
    l_cesalerate number(5, 4);
    ldayrate     Number;
    row_ssd      supsettledet%Rowtype;
    l_fsdays     Number; --发生天数
    l_bddays     Number; --保底(超额)天数
    l_xstc       Number;
    l_unionsr    Number; --老系统联合保底的实际发生收入
    l_unionml    Number; --老系统联合保底的实际发生毛利
    l_sr         Number; --保底期间总收入
    l_detrow     supsettledet%Rowtype;
    l_cmkhfs     char(1); --1按销售收入2按差额3按考核指标
  Begin
    If i_wmid = '1' Then
      Return;
    End If;
    o_bdtc   := 0;
    o_xstc   := 0;
    o_cetc   := 0;
    o_xskhtc := 0;
    If b_isqs = '0' Then
      --考虑到合同变更柜组引起的柜组未结销售，因此最长允许结算到上次结算前6个月
      l_startdate := add_months(i_startdate, -6);
    Else
      l_startdate := i_startdate;
    End If;
    --统计整个结算期销售
    --计算第一期保底时才记入正常销售收入和提成
    If i_seq <= 1 And b_isqs = '0' Then
      saledate(i_contno,
               i_supid,
               i_wmid,
               i_mkt,
               i_mfid,
               l_startdate,
               i_enddate,
               i_unionflag,
               b_detrow);
      b_detrow.ssdn28 := b_detrow.ssdn9 + b_detrow.ssdn77; --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
      b_detrow.ssdn29 := b_detrow.ssdn10; --销售应提(不含保底、超额)
    Elsif b_isqs = '1' Then
      saledate(i_contno,
               i_supid,
               i_wmid,
               i_mkt,
               i_mfid,
               i_bdstartdate,
               i_bdenddate,
               i_unionflag,
               l_detrow);
      o_xstc := o_xstc + l_detrow.ssdn10;
    End If;
    --初始化
    row_ssd.ssdbillno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
    row_ssd.ssdmarket   := i_mkt;
    row_ssd.ssdmfid     := i_mfid;
    row_ssd.ssdwmid     := i_wmid;
    row_ssd.ssdcontno   := i_contno;
    row_ssd.ssdybillno  := Null;
    row_ssd.ssdydjbh    := Null;
    row_ssd.ssdlastdate := i_startdate;
    row_ssd.ssdthisdate := i_enddate;
    row_ssd.ssdvc5      := '3';
    If i_wmid = '5' And i_seq <= 1 And b_isqs = '0' Then
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      --租赁算租金
      l_bddays := last_day(trunc(i_enddate)) - trunc(i_enddate, 'MON') + 1;
      l_fsdays := trunc(i_enddate) - trunc(i_startdate) + 1;
    
      Begin
        Select round(nvl(Sum(cmfcharter), 0) * l_fsdays / l_bddays, 2)
          Into b_detrow.ssdn23
          From contmanaframe
         Where cmfcontno = i_contno
           And cmfmarket = i_mkt
           And cmfmfid = i_mfid;
      Exception
        When Others Then
          b_detrow.ssdn23 := 0;
      End;
    
      If b_detrow.ssdn23 <> 0 Then
        row_ssd.ssdvc5   := '6';
        row_ssd.ssdn61   := 0;
        row_ssd.ssdn62   := 0;
        row_ssd.ssdn63   := b_detrow.ssdn23;
        row_ssd.ssdvc6   := '6';
        row_ssd.ssdvc7   := Null;
        row_ssd.ssdvc10  := '租金[' ||
                            TO_CHAR(trunc(i_startdate), 'YYYYMMDD') || '-' ||
                            TO_CHAR(trunc(i_enddate), 'YYYYMMDD') || ']';
        row_ssd.ssdvc9   := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
        b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
        row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
        insertdetail(row_ssd);
        row_ssd.ssdvc5 := '3';
      End If;
    End If;
    --计算保底
    If i_isbd <> 'Y' Or (i_bdstartdate Is Null Or i_bdenddate Is Null) Then
      Return;
    End If;
  
    l_bdmode := b_cont.cmbysettle;
    --保底方式（1－毛利保底，2－销售保底）
    l_bdtype := b_cont.cmweek5;
  
    l_bd := False;
    l_ce := False;
    l_xs := False;
  
    Select Nvl(Sum(Nvl(cbprofit, 0)), 0),
           Nvl(Sum(Nvl(cbsum, 0)), 0),
           Nvl(Sum(Nvl(cbsum1, 0)), 0),
           Nvl(Sum(Nvl(cbsum2, 0)), 0),
           Nvl(Sum(Nvl(cbsum3, 0)), 0),
           Nvl(Sum(Nvl(cbsum4, 0)), 0),
           Nvl(Sum(Nvl(cbsum5, 0)), 0),
           Nvl(Sum(Nvl(cbsum6, 0)), 0),
           nvl(sum(nvl(cbsalekh, 0)), 0)
      Into l_bdml,
           l_bdsum,
           l_cesum1,
           l_cesum2,
           l_cesum3,
           l_cesum4,
           l_cesum5,
           l_cesum6,
           l_cesalekh
      From contbd
     Where cbcontno In (i_contno, Decode(b_isqs, '1', b_unioncontno, Null))
       And cbflag = 'Y'
       And cbmkt = i_mkt
       And cbmfid = i_mfid
       And cbeffdate <= i_bdenddate
       And cblapdate >= i_bdstartdate
          --AND b_isqs = '0'
       And b_ispop = '0';
    If l_bdtype = bdtypeml Then
      If l_bdml <= 0 And l_cesum1 <= 0 And l_cesum2 <= 0 And l_cesum3 <= 0 And
         l_cesum4 <= 0 And l_cesum5 <= 0 And l_cesum6 <= 0 Then
        Return;
      End If;
    Else
      If l_bdsum <= 0 And l_cesum1 <= 0 And l_cesum2 <= 0 And l_cesum3 <= 0 And
         l_cesum4 <= 0 And l_cesum5 <= 0 And l_cesum6 <= 0 Then
        Return;
      End If;
    End If;
  
    Select nvl(cbrate, 0),
           cbmode1,
           cbrate1,
           cbmode2,
           cbrate2,
           cbmode3,
           cbrate3,
           cbmode4,
           cbrate4,
           cbmode5,
           cbrate5,
           cbmode6,
           cbrate6,
           cbsalerate
      Into l_bdrate,
           l_cemode1,
           l_cerate1,
           l_cemode2,
           l_cerate2,
           l_cemode3,
           l_cerate3,
           l_cemode4,
           l_cerate4,
           l_cemode5,
           l_cerate5,
           l_cemode6,
           l_cerate6,
           l_cesalerate
      From contbd
     Where cbcontno = i_contno
       And cbflag = 'Y'
       And cbmkt = i_mkt
       And cbmfid = i_mfid
       And cblapdate = i_bdenddate
       And rownum = 1;
  
    --初始化超额基数
    InitCeList;
  
    --只能按月进行保底
    /*IF l_bdmode = bdmodemon THEN
      --失效日期 - 生效日期 共多少个月 +
      --失效日期所有月天数占本月天数的比例 +
      --生效日期所有月剩余天数占本月天数的比例
      ldayrate := trunc(months_between(trunc(i_bdenddate,'MON'),trunc(i_bdstartdate,'MON'))) - 1
                  +
                  Round((trunc(i_bdenddate) - trunc(i_bdenddate,'MON') + 1) / (last_day(trunc(i_bdenddate)) - trunc(i_bdenddate,'MON') + 1),10)
                  +
                  Round((last_day(trunc(i_bdstartdate)) - trunc(i_bdstartdate) + 1) / (last_day(trunc(i_bdstartdate)) - trunc(i_bdstartdate,'MON') + 1),10);
    END IF;*/
    ldayrate := 1;
    initdetrow(l_ssdxs.det0);
    initdetrow(l_ssdxs.det1);
    initdetrow(l_ssdxs.det2);
    initdetrow(l_ssdxs.det3);
    saledate(i_contno,
             i_supid,
             i_wmid,
             i_mkt,
             i_mfid,
             l_startdate,
             i_enddate,
             'N',
             i_unionflag,
             l_ssdxs);
  
    initdetrow(l_ssd.det0);
    initdetrow(l_ssd.det1);
    initdetrow(l_ssd.det2);
    initdetrow(l_ssd.det3);
    saledate(i_contno,
             i_supid,
             i_wmid,
             i_mkt,
             i_mfid,
             i_bdstartdate,
             i_bdenddate,
             'Y',
             i_unionflag,
             l_ssd);
    /*SaleDateUnion(i_contno, i_supid, i_wmid, i_mkt, i_mfid, i_bdstartdate,i_bdenddate,
    l_unionsr,l_unionml);*/
    l_unionsr := 0;
    l_unionml := 0;
  
    If l_cemode1 In (CeModeQe, CeModeCe) And l_cesum1 > 0 And
       l_cerate1 >= 0 And l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_unionsr >=
       round(l_cesum1 * ldayrate, 2) Then
      AddCeRec(l_cemode1, round(l_cesum1 * ldayrate, 2), l_cerate1);
    End If;
    If l_cemode2 In (CeModeQe, CeModeCe) And l_cesum2 > 0 And
       l_cerate2 >= 0 And l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_unionsr >=
       round(l_cesum2 * ldayrate, 2) Then
      AddCeRec(l_cemode2, round(l_cesum2 * ldayrate, 2), l_cerate2);
    End If;
    If l_cemode3 In (CeModeQe, CeModeCe) And l_cesum3 > 0 And
       l_cerate3 >= 0 And l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_unionsr >=
       round(l_cesum3 * ldayrate, 2) Then
      AddCeRec(l_cemode3, round(l_cesum3 * ldayrate, 2), l_cerate3);
    End If;
    If l_cemode4 In (CeModeQe, CeModeCe) And l_cesum4 > 0 And
       l_cerate4 >= 0 And l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_unionsr >=
       round(l_cesum4 * ldayrate, 2) Then
      AddCeRec(l_cemode4, round(l_cesum4 * ldayrate, 2), l_cerate4);
    End If;
    If l_cemode5 In (CeModeQe, CeModeCe) And l_cesum5 > 0 And
       l_cerate5 >= 0 And l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_unionsr >=
       round(l_cesum5 * ldayrate, 2) Then
      AddCeRec(l_cemode5, round(l_cesum5 * ldayrate, 2), l_cerate5);
    End If;
    If l_cemode6 In (CeModeQe, CeModeCe) And l_cesum6 > 0 And
       l_cerate6 >= 0 And l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_unionsr >=
       round(l_cesum6 * ldayrate, 2) Then
      AddCeRec(l_cemode6, round(l_cesum6 * ldayrate, 2), l_cerate6);
    End If;
    SortCeList; --按基数从低到高排序
  
    If b_celist.COUNT > 0 Then
      --有超额
      /*If l_bdrate Is Null Or l_bdrate = 0 Then
        l_bdrate := b_celist(1).cerate;
      End If;*/
      If l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_unionsr >= b_celist(1)
        .cesum Then
        l_ce := True;
      End If;
    End If;
  
    --有保底
    If l_bdsum > 0 And l_bdrate > 0 And l_bdml > 0 Then
      l_bdsum := Round(l_bdsum * ldayrate, 2);
      l_bdml  := Round(l_bdml * ldayrate, 2);
      If l_bdtype = bdtypeml Then
        --毛利保底,比较保底时按正常商品毛利＋保底特卖毛利
        If l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 + l_unionml < l_bdml Then
          l_bd := True;
          l_ce := False;
        End If;
        If b_isqs = '1' Then
          b_qsvalue.bdmode  := bdtypeml;
          b_qsvalue.bdvalue := l_bdml;
        End If;
      Elsif l_bdtype = BdTypeFb Then
        --反销售保底,比较保底时按正常商品收入-保底调整
        If l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 +
           l_ssd.det1.ssdn77 + l_unionsr < l_bdsum Then
          l_bd   := True;
          l_ce   := False;
          l_bdml := l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 + l_unionml -
                    round((l_bdsum - (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                          (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77) -
                          l_unionsr) * l_bdrate,
                          2);
          If b_AllowNeg = 'N' And l_bdml < 0 Then
            l_bdml := 0;
          End If;
        End If;
        If b_isqs = '1' Then
          b_qsvalue.bdmode  := BdTypeFb;
          b_qsvalue.bdvalue := l_bdsum;
        End If;
      Else
        --销售保底,比较保底时按正常商品收入＋保底特卖收入
        If l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 +
           l_ssd.det1.ssdn77 + l_unionsr < l_bdsum Then
          l_bd   := True;
          l_ce   := False;
          l_bdml := l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 + l_unionml +
                    round((l_bdsum - (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                          (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77) -
                          l_unionsr) * l_bdrate,
                          2);
        End If;
        If b_isqs = '1' Then
          b_qsvalue.bdmode  := BdTypeXs;
          b_qsvalue.bdvalue := l_bdsum;
        End If;
      End If;
    End If;
  
    If l_ce And Not l_bd Then
      l_sr              := l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_unionsr;
      l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_unionml;
      For i In Reverse 1 .. b_celist.COUNT Loop
        If b_celist(i).cemode = cemodeqe Then
          --全额
          --[[[[ EORV-1026 =  =P~ 2018.11.06
          /*l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := round(l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 - (l_sr) * (l_bdrate - b_celist(i)
          .cerate),
          2);*/
          l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 -
                               round((l_sr) *
                                     (l_bdrate - b_celist(i).cerate),
                                     2);
          --]]]] ----------------------------
          initdetrow(row_ssd);
          row_ssd.ssdn61  := l_sr;
          row_ssd.ssdn62  := - (l_bdrate - b_celist(i).cerate);
          row_ssd.ssdn63  := Round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
          row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '7'; --考核点考核
          row_ssd.ssdvc7  := '3'; --全额超额
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '超额完成,让扣(' || to_char(b_celist(i).cesum) || '/' ||
                             to_char(b_celist(i).cerate * 100) || '%)';
          row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          row_ssd.ssdd2   := i_bdenddate;
          If b_isqs = '0' Then
            b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
            row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
            insertdetail(row_ssd);
          Elsif b_isqs = '1' Then
            b_qsvalue.cevalue := b_celist(i).cesum;
            b_qsvalue.cerate  := b_celist(i).cerate;
          End If;
          Exit;
        Else
          initdetrow(row_ssd);
          If i = b_celist.COUNT Then
            --[[[[ EORV-1026 =  =P~ 2018.11.06
            /*l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := Round(l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 -
            (l_sr - b_celist(i).cesum) *
            (l_bdrate - b_celist(i).cerate),
            2);*/
            l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 -
                                 Round((l_sr - b_celist(i).cesum) *
                                       (l_bdrate - b_celist(i).cerate),
                                       2);
            --]]]] --------------------------
            row_ssd.ssdn61 := l_sr - b_celist(i).cesum;
          Else
            --[[[[ EORV-1026 =  =P~ 2018.11.06
            /*l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := Round(l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 -
            (b_celist(i + 1).cesum - b_celist(i)
            .cesum) *
            (l_bdrate - b_celist(i).cerate),
            2);*/
            l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 := l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 -
                                 Round((b_celist(i + 1).cesum - b_celist(i)
                                       .cesum) *
                                       (l_bdrate - b_celist(i).cerate),
                                       2);
            --]]]] -----------------------------
            row_ssd.ssdn61 := b_celist(i + 1).cesum - b_celist(i).cesum;
          End If;
          l_sr            := b_celist(i).cesum;
          row_ssd.ssdn62  := - (l_bdrate - b_celist(i).cerate);
          row_ssd.ssdn63  := Round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
          row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '7'; --考核点考核
          row_ssd.ssdvc7  := '4'; --差额超额
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '超额完成,让扣(' || to_char(b_celist(i).cesum) || '/' ||
                             to_char(b_celist(i).cerate * 100) || '%)';
          row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          row_ssd.ssdd2   := i_bdenddate;
          If b_isqs = '0' Then
            b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
            row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
            insertdetail(row_ssd);
          Elsif b_isqs = '1' Then
            If i = b_celist.COUNT Then
              b_qsvalue.cevalue := b_celist(i).cesum;
              b_qsvalue.cerate  := b_celist(i).cerate;
            End If;
          End If;
        End If;
      End Loop;
    
      --毛利保底方式，如果有超额，判断超额提成后是否达到毛利保底，没有达到毛利保底的还是按毛利保底提成
      If l_bdtype = bdtypeml And
         l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 < l_bdml Then
        l_bd := True;
        l_ce := False;
      Else
        If b_isqs = '0' Then
          If i_seq = 1 Then
            l_xstc          := (l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_unionml) -
                               b_detrow.ssdn29;
            b_detrow.ssdn28 := b_detrow.ssdn28 -
                               (l_ssdxs.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77); --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
            b_detrow.ssdn29 := b_detrow.ssdn29 - l_ssdxs.det0.ssdn10; --销售应提(不含保底、超额)
          Else
            l_xstc := l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_unionml;
          End If;
          b_detrow.ssdn26 := b_detrow.ssdn26 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn26 - l_xstc;
        Else
          o_xstc := o_xstc - l_ssd.det0.ssdn10;
          o_cetc := o_cetc + l_ssd.det0.ssdn26;
        End If;
        If b_isqs = '1' Then
          b_qsvalue.resid := cmsTypeCe;
        End If;
      End If;
    End If;
  
    If l_bd And Not l_ce Then
      --保底金额需要减之前结算单里的提成金额
      --之前未保底时的销售提成
      If b_isqs = '0' Then
        If i_seq = 1 Then
          l_xstc := (l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 + l_unionml) -
                    b_detrow.ssdn29;
          --减去正常销售
          b_detrow.ssdn28 := b_detrow.ssdn28 -
                             (l_ssdxs.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 +
                             l_ssdxs.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77); --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
          b_detrow.ssdn29 := b_detrow.ssdn29 -
                             (l_ssdxs.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssdxs.det1.ssdn10); --销售应提(不含保底、超额)
        Else
          l_xstc := l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 + l_unionml;
        End If;
        --本期产生的提成记入保底提成
        b_detrow.ssdn23 := b_detrow.ssdn23 + l_bdml - l_xstc;
      
        --保底部分的结算明细
        Delete From supsettledet
         Where ssdbillno = b_hd.sshbillno
           And ssdwmid = i_wmid
           And ssdcontno = i_contno
           And ssdmarket = i_mkt
           And ssdmfid = i_mfid
           And ssdvc5 = '3'
           And ssdvc6 = '7'
           And ssdvc7 In ('3', '4')
           And ssdd2 = i_bdenddate;
      Else
        o_xstc := o_xstc - (l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn10);
        o_bdtc := o_bdtc + l_bdml;
      End If;
    
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      If l_bdtype = bdtypeml Then
        row_ssd.ssdn61 := l_bdsum - (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                          (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77) -
                          l_unionsr;
        row_ssd.ssdn62 := l_bdrate;
        row_ssd.ssdn63 := l_bdml - l_ssd.det0.ssdn10 - l_ssd.det1.ssdn10 -
                          l_unionml;
        --row_ssd.ssdvc6 := '1';
        --row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '保扣差额(' || to_char(l_bdml) || ')';
        row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '7'; --考核点考核
        row_ssd.ssdvc7  := '1'; --毛利保底
        row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,毛利' || to_char(l_bdml) || '元';
        row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
        row_ssd.ssdn75  := -1 * row_ssd.ssdn63;
      Elsif l_BdType = BdTypeFb Then
        --反保底
        row_ssd.ssdn61  := (l_bdsum -
                           (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                           (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77) -
                           l_unionsr);
        row_ssd.ssdn62  := l_bdrate;
        row_ssd.ssdn63  := -1 * Round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
        row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '7'; --考核点考核
        row_ssd.ssdvc7  := '2'; --销售反保底
        row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,反保底(' || to_char(l_bdsum) || '/' ||
                           to_char(l_bdrate * 100) || '%)';
        row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
        row_ssd.ssdn75  := -1 * row_ssd.ssdn63;
      Else
        row_ssd.ssdn61 := l_bdsum - (l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77) -
                          (l_ssd.det1.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det1.ssdn77) -
                          l_unionsr;
        row_ssd.ssdn62 := l_bdrate;
        row_ssd.ssdn63 := Round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
        --row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '2';
        --row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '保扣差额(' || to_char(l_bdsum) || '/' || to_char(row_bd.cbrate * 100) || '%)';
        row_ssd.ssdvc6  := '7'; --考核点考核
        row_ssd.ssdvc7  := '2'; --销售保底
        row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,销售' || to_char(l_bdsum) || '元';
        row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
        row_ssd.ssdn75  := -1 * row_ssd.ssdn63;
      End If;
      row_ssd.ssdd2 := i_bdenddate;
      If b_isqs = '0' Then
        b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
        row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
        insertdetail(row_ssd);
      Elsif b_isqs = '1' Then
        b_qsvalue.resid := cmsTypeBd;
      End If;
    End If;
  
    if l_cesalekh > 0 And l_cesalerate > 0 then
      l_sr := l_ssd.det0.ssdn9 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn77 + l_ssd.det2.ssdn9 +
              l_ssd.det2.ssdn77;
      if l_sr < round(l_cesalekh, 2) Then
        l_bd := false;
        l_xs := true;
        initdetrow(row_ssd);
        if b_cont.cmkhfs = '1' or b_cont.cmkhfs is null then
          row_ssd.ssdn61 := l_sr;
        elsif b_cont.cmkhfs = '2' then
          row_ssd.ssdn61 := l_cesalekh - l_sr;
        else
          row_ssd.ssdn61 := l_cesalekh;
        end if;
        row_ssd.ssdn62    := l_cesalerate;
        row_ssd.ssdn63    := Round(row_ssd.ssdn61 * row_ssd.ssdn62, 2);
        l_ssd.det0.ssdn73 := row_ssd.ssdn63;
        row_ssd.ssdvc6    := '7'; --考核点考核
        row_ssd.ssdvc7    := '7'; --销售未完成
        row_ssd.ssdvc10   := '销售考核未完成,加扣(' || to_char(row_ssd.ssdn61) || '×' ||
                             to_char(l_cesalerate * 100) || '%)';
        row_ssd.ssdvc9    := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
        row_ssd.ssdd2     := i_bdenddate;
        If b_isqs = '0' Then
          b_detrow.ssdn73  := b_detrow.ssdn73 + l_ssd.det0.ssdn73;
          b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
          row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
          insertdetail(row_ssd);
          --本期产生的提成记入销售考核提成
          o_xskhtc := o_xskhtc + l_ssd.det0.ssdn73;
        Else
          o_xskhtc := o_xskhtc + l_ssd.det0.ssdn73;
        End If;
      end if;
    end if;
  
    /*If Not l_bd And Not l_ce and not l_xs Then
      --达到保底未超额的也体现出来
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      row_ssd.ssdn61 := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn62 := l_bdrate;
      row_ssd.ssdn63 := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdvc6 := '7'; --考核点考核
      row_ssd.ssdvc7  := '';
      row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '本期考核完成，无调整！';
      row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
      \*If l_bdtype = bdtypeml Then
        row_ssd.ssdvc7  := '1'; --毛利保底
        row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,毛利' || to_char(l_bdml) || '元';
        row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
      Else
        row_ssd.ssdvc7  := '2'; --销售保底
        row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,销售' || to_char(l_bdsum) || '元';
        row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
      End If;*\
      row_ssd.ssdd2 := i_bdenddate;
      If b_isqs = '0' Then
        b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
        row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
        insertdetail(row_ssd);
      Elsif b_isqs = '1' Then
        b_qsvalue.resid := cmsTypeZc;
      End If;
    End If;*/
  
  End SaleStatBdByRange;

  --计算保底，梦之岛方式-按月定义，合同期清算平衡
  /*更新历史：
    1、暂时只考虑毛利保底，不支持销售保底和超额
    2、同时支持毛利保底和销售保底模式，但毛利保底时不支持超额
    3、毛利保底同时可以支持超额
  */
  Procedure SaleStatQsByRange(i_contno      In Varchar2,
                              i_supid       In Varchar2,
                              i_wmid        In Char,
                              i_mkt         In Varchar2,
                              i_mfid        In Varchar2,
                              i_startdate   In Date,
                              i_enddate     In Date,
                              i_isqs        In Char,
                              i_qsstartdate In Date,
                              i_qsenddate   In Date,
                              i_unionflag   In Char) Is
    row_ssd        supsettledet%Rowtype;
    l_qsbdtc       Number; --清算保底提成金额
    l_qsxstc       Number; --清算销售提成金额
    l_qscetc       Number; --清算超额提成金额
    l_qsxskhtc     number; --清算考核提成金额
    l_qstc         Number;
    l_bdtc         Number; --考核点保底提成金额
    l_xstc         Number; --考核点销售提成金额
    l_cetc         Number; --考核点超额提成金额
    l_xskhtc       Number; --考核点销售任务考核提成
    l_tc           Number;
    l_adjchargeamt Number;
    l_unionsr      Number;
    l_unionml      Number;
    l_unionbdml    Number;
    l_hasqs        Boolean := False;
  Begin
    If i_wmid = '1' Then
      Return;
    End If;
  
    If i_isqs <> 'Y' Then
      Return;
    End If;
  
    row_ssd.ssdbillno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
    row_ssd.ssdmarket   := i_mkt;
    row_ssd.ssdmfid     := i_mfid;
    row_ssd.ssdwmid     := i_wmid;
    row_ssd.ssdcontno   := i_contno;
    row_ssd.ssdybillno  := Null;
    row_ssd.ssdydjbh    := Null;
    row_ssd.ssdlastdate := i_startdate;
    row_ssd.ssdthisdate := i_enddate;
    row_ssd.ssdvc5      := '3';
  
    b_qsvalue := Null;
    --1.计算清算期的应提成金额
    SaleStatBdByRange(i_contno,
                      i_supid,
                      i_wmid,
                      i_mkt,
                      i_mfid,
                      i_startdate,
                      i_enddate,
                      'Y',
                      i_qsstartdate,
                      i_qsenddate,
                      2,
                      i_unionflag,
                      l_qsbdtc,
                      l_qsxstc,
                      l_qscetc,
                      l_qsxskhtc);
    l_qstc := l_qsbdtc + l_qsxstc + l_qscetc + l_qsxskhtc;
  
    --2.1.获得核算点上的已提成金额
    Select Sum(Nvl(decode(ssdvc6, '0', ssdn63, 0), 0)), --销售提成金额
           Sum(Nvl(Decode(ssdvc6,
                          '7',
                          Decode(ssdvc7, '1', 1, '2', 1, 0),
                          '8',
                          Decode(i_unionflag, 'Y', 1, 0),
                          0) * ssdn63,
                   0)), --保底提成金额
           Sum(Nvl(decode(ssdvc6, '7', Decode(ssdvc7, '3', 1, '4', 1, 0), 0) *
                   ssdn63,
                   0)), --超额提成金额
           Sum(Nvl(Decode(ssdvc6, '7', Decode(ssdvc7, '7', 1, 0), 0) *
                   ssdn63,
                   0)) --考核提成金额
      Into l_xstc, l_bdtc, l_cetc, l_xskhtc
      From supsettledet
     Where /*ssdthisdate <= i_qsenddate
                                                                                             AND ssdthisdate >= i_qsstartdate*/
     Decode(ssdvc6,
            '7',
            Nvl(ssdd2, ssdthisdate),
            '8',
            Nvl(ssdd2, ssdthisdate),
            ssdthisdate) <= i_qsenddate
     And Decode(ssdvc6,
            '7',
            Nvl(ssdd2, ssdthisdate),
            '8',
            Nvl(ssdd2, ssdthisdate),
            ssdthisdate) >= i_qsstartdate
     And ssdcontno In (i_contno, Decode(i_unionflag, 'Y', b_unioncontno, Null))
     And ssdmarket = i_mkt
     And ssdmfid = i_mfid
     And ssdvc5 = '3'
     And ((ssdvc6 In ('0', '7')) Or (ssdvc6 = '8' And i_unionflag = 'Y'));
  
    --2.2.统计手工费用调整的保底提成
    AdjQsByCharge(i_contno, i_supid, i_wmid, i_mkt, i_mfid, l_adjchargeamt);
    /*--2.3 处理历史数据的提成
    --2.3.1 销售提成
    SaleDateUnion(i_contno, i_supid, i_wmid, i_mkt, i_mfid, i_qsstartdate,i_qsenddate,
                  l_unionsr,l_unionml);
    --2.3.2 保底清算提成
    SaleDateUnion_Qs(i_contno, i_supid, i_wmid, i_mkt, i_mfid, i_qsstartdate,i_qsenddate,
                     l_unionbdml);*/
    /*l_unionsr   := 0;
    l_unionml   := 0;
    l_unionbdml := 0;
    l_bdtc      := l_bdtc + l_unionbdml + l_adjchargeamt;
    l_xstc      := l_xstc + l_unionml;
    l_tc        := l_bdtc + l_xstc + l_cetc + l_xskhtc;*/
  
    /*--3.比较清算期计算的提成金额与核算点上的已提成金额比较，进行多退少补
    If Abs(l_qstc - l_tc) >= 0.1 Then
      b_detrow.ssdn23 := b_detrow.ssdn23 + (l_qstc - l_tc);
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      If b_cont.cmkl = 0 Then
        row_ssd.ssdn61 := 0;
      Else
        row_ssd.ssdn61 := Round((l_qstc - l_tc) / b_cont.cmkl, 2);
      End If;
      row_ssd.ssdn62 := b_cont.cmkl; --合同主扣率
      row_ssd.ssdn63 := l_qstc - l_tc;
      --row_ssd.ssdvc6 := '1';
      --row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '清算:保扣差额(' || to_char(l_bdml) || ')';
      row_ssd.ssdvc6 := '8';
      If i_unionflag = 'Y' Then
        row_ssd.ssdvc7 := '6';
        --row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '目标毛利' || to_char(l_qstc) || '元,实际毛利' || to_char(l_tc) || '元(联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || '])';
        If b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeZc Then
          If b_qsvalue.bdmode = bdtypeml Then
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,联合毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) ||
                               '元,联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || ']';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '已完成,联合毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
          Else
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,联合销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) ||
                               '元,联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || ']';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '已完成,联合销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
          End If;
        Elsif b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeBd Then
          If b_qsvalue.bdmode = bdtypeml Then
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,联合毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) ||
                               '元,联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || ']';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '未完成,联合毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
          Else
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,联合销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) ||
                               '元,联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || ']';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '未完成,联合销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
          End If;
        Elsif b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeCe Then
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '超额完成,' || to_char(b_qsvalue.cevalue) || '/' ||
                             to_char(b_qsvalue.cerate * 100) || '%),联合合同[' ||
                             b_unioncontno || ']';
          row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '超额完成,' || to_char(b_qsvalue.cevalue) || '/' ||
                             to_char(b_qsvalue.cerate * 100) || '%)';
        End If;
        row_ssd.ssdvc8 := b_unioncontno;
      Else
        row_ssd.ssdvc7 := '5';
        --row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '目标毛利' || to_char(l_qstc) || '元,实际毛利' || to_char(l_tc) || '元';
        If b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeZc Then
          If b_qsvalue.bdmode = bdtypeml Then
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          Else
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          End If;
        Elsif b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeBd Then
          If b_qsvalue.bdmode = bdtypeml Then
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          Else
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          End If;
        Elsif b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeCe Then
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '超额完成,' || to_char(b_qsvalue.cevalue) || '/' ||
                             to_char(b_qsvalue.cerate * 100) || '%)';
          row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
        End If;
        row_ssd.ssdvc8 := Null;
      End If;
      row_ssd.ssdd2    := i_qsenddate;
      b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
      row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
      insertdetail(row_ssd);
    Else
      --b_detrow.ssdn23 := b_detrow.ssdn23 + (l_qstc - l_tc);
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      row_ssd.ssdn61 := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn62 := b_cont.cmkl;
      row_ssd.ssdn63 := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdvc6 := '8';
      If i_unionflag = 'Y' Then
        row_ssd.ssdvc7 := '6';
        --row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '目标毛利' || to_char(l_qstc) || '元(联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || '])';
        If b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeZc Then
          If b_qsvalue.bdmode = bdtypeml Then
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,联合毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) ||
                               '元,联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || ']';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '已完成,联合毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
          Else
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,联合销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) ||
                               '元,联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || ']';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '已完成,联合销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
          End If;
        Elsif b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeBd Then
          If b_qsvalue.bdmode = bdtypeml Then
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,联合毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) ||
                               '元,联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || ']';
