            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '未完成,联合毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
          Else
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,联合销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) ||
                               '元,联合合同[' || b_unioncontno || ']';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '未完成,联合销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
          End If;
        Elsif b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeCe Then
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '超额完成,' || to_char(b_qsvalue.cevalue) || '/' ||
                             to_char(b_qsvalue.cerate * 100) || '%),联合合同[' ||
                             b_unioncontno || ']';
          row_ssd.ssdvc9  := '超额完成,' || to_char(b_qsvalue.cevalue) || '/' ||
                             to_char(b_qsvalue.cerate * 100) || '%)';
        End If;
        row_ssd.ssdvc8 := b_unioncontno;
      Else
        row_ssd.ssdvc7 := '5';
        --row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '目标毛利' || to_char(l_qstc) || '元';
        If b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeZc Then
          If b_qsvalue.bdmode = bdtypeml Then
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          Else
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '已完成,销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          End If;
        Elsif b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeBd Then
          If b_qsvalue.bdmode = bdtypeml Then
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,毛利' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          Else
            row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '未完成,销售' || to_char(b_qsvalue.bdvalue) || '元';
            row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
          End If;
        Elsif b_qsvalue.resid = cmsTypeCe Then
          row_ssd.ssdvc10 := '超额完成,' || to_char(b_qsvalue.cevalue) || '/' ||
                             to_char(b_qsvalue.cerate * 100) || '%)';
          row_ssd.ssdvc9  := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
        End If;
        row_ssd.ssdvc8 := Null;
      End If;
      row_ssd.ssdd2    := i_qsenddate;
      b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
      row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
      insertdetail(row_ssd);
    End If;*/
    --3.1销售提成清算
    If abs(l_qsxstc - l_xstc) >= 0.01 Then
      b_detrow.ssdn29 := b_detrow.ssdn29 + (l_qsxstc - l_xstc);
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      row_ssd.ssdn61   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn62   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn63   := l_qsxstc - l_xstc;
      row_ssd.ssdvc6   := '8';
      row_ssd.ssdvc7   := '0';
      row_ssd.ssdvc10  := '清算,调整销售扣率提成' || to_char(row_ssd.ssdn63) || '元';
      row_ssd.ssdvc9   := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
      row_ssd.ssdvc8   := Null;
      row_ssd.ssdd2    := i_qsenddate;
      b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
      row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
      insertdetail(row_ssd);
      l_hasqs := True;
    End If;
    --3.1保底提成清算
    If abs(l_qsbdtc - l_bdtc) >= 0.01 Then
      b_detrow.ssdn23 := b_detrow.ssdn23 + (l_qsbdtc - l_bdtc);
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      row_ssd.ssdn61   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn62   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn63   := l_qsbdtc - l_bdtc;
      row_ssd.ssdvc6   := '8';
      row_ssd.ssdvc7   := '8';
      row_ssd.ssdvc10  := '清算,调整保底提成' || to_char(row_ssd.ssdn63) || '元';
      row_ssd.ssdvc9   := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
      row_ssd.ssdvc8   := Null;
      row_ssd.ssdd2    := i_qsenddate;
      b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
      row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
      insertdetail(row_ssd);
      l_hasqs := True;
    End If;
    --3.2销售考核部分清算
    If abs(l_qsxskhtc - l_xskhtc) >= 0.01 Then
      b_detrow.ssdn73 := b_detrow.ssdn73 + (l_qsxskhtc - l_xskhtc);
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      row_ssd.ssdn61   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn62   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn63   := l_qsxskhtc - l_xskhtc;
      row_ssd.ssdvc6   := '8';
      row_ssd.ssdvc7   := '9';
      row_ssd.ssdvc10  := '清算,调整销售考核提成' || to_char(row_ssd.ssdn63) || '元';
      row_ssd.ssdvc9   := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
      row_ssd.ssdvc8   := Null;
      row_ssd.ssdd2    := i_qsenddate;
      b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
      row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
      insertdetail(row_ssd);
      l_hasqs := True;
    End If;
    --3.3超额销售部分清算
    If abs(l_qscetc - l_cetc) >= 0.01 Then
      b_detrow.ssdn26 := b_detrow.ssdn26 + (l_qscetc - l_cetc);
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      row_ssd.ssdn61   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn62   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn63   := l_qscetc - l_cetc;
      row_ssd.ssdvc6   := '8';
      row_ssd.ssdvc7   := '3';
      row_ssd.ssdvc10  := '清算,调整超额销售提成' || to_char(row_ssd.ssdn63) || '元';
      row_ssd.ssdvc9   := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
      row_ssd.ssdvc8   := Null;
      row_ssd.ssdd2    := i_qsenddate;
      b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
      row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
      insertdetail(row_ssd);
      l_hasqs := True;
    End If;
    --如果没进行任何调整，记录一下空，表示清算过程处理过了
    If Not l_hasqs Then
      initdetrow(row_ssd);
      row_ssd.ssdn61   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn62   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdn63   := 0;
      row_ssd.ssdvc6   := '8';
      row_ssd.ssdvc7   := '';
      row_ssd.ssdvc10  := '清算完成,无任何调整！';
      row_ssd.ssdvc9   := row_ssd.ssdvc10;
      row_ssd.ssdvc8   := Null;
      row_ssd.ssdd2    := i_qsenddate;
      b_rowno          := b_rowno + 1;
      row_ssd.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
      insertdetail(row_ssd);
      l_hasqs := True;
    End If;
  End SaleStatQsByRange;

  Procedure Popsalebdce(i_Contno    In Varchar2,
                        i_Supid     In Varchar2,
                        i_Wmid      In Char,
                        i_Mkt       In Varchar2,
                        i_Mfid      In Varchar2,
                        i_Startdate In Date,
                        i_Enddate   In Date) Is
  Begin
    For vr In (Select *
                 From Popsettlehead
                Where pshstatus In ('Y', 'S', 'T')
                  And ((pshsdate <= i_Startdate And
                      nvl(pshedate, stopdate) >= i_Startdate) Or
                      (pshsdate <= i_Enddate And
                      nvl(pshedate, stopdate) >= i_Enddate) Or
                      (pshsdate >= i_Startdate And
                      nvl(pshedate, stopdate) <= i_Enddate))
                  And pshcontno = i_Contno
                  And pshmfid = i_mfid) Loop
      b_ispop     := '1';
      b_popbillno := vr.pshbillno;
      initdetrow(b_detrow);
      salestat(i_contno,
               i_supid,
               i_wmid,
               i_mkt,
               i_mfid,
               greatest(vr.pshsdate, i_startdate),
               least(nvl(vr.pshedate, vr.stopdate), i_enddate));
      b_detrow.ssdn9    := 0;
      b_detrow.ssdn77   := 0;
      b_detrow.ssdn1    := 0;
      b_detrow.ssdn8    := 0;
      b_detrow.ssdn4    := 0;
      b_detrow.ssdn28   := 0;
      b_detrow.ssdn29   := 0;
      b_detrow.ssdn10   := 0;
      b_rowno           := b_rowno + 1;
      b_detrow.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
      insertdetail(b_detrow);
      adddettot(b_dettot, b_detrow);
      b_ispop     := '0';
      b_popbillno := Null;
    End Loop;
  End;

  --统计历史结算保底
  Procedure hisbddate(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                      i_supid     In Varchar2,
                      i_wmid      In Char,
                      i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                      i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                      i_startdate In Date,
                      i_enddate   In Date) Is
  Begin
    Select b_detrow.ssdn23 - nvl(Sum(ssdn23), 0),
           b_detrow.ssdn26 - nvl(Sum(ssdn26), 0),
           b_detrow.ssdn29 - nvl(Sum(ssdn29), 0) - nvl(Sum(ssdn38), 0), --修改，清算不加入票减费用
           -- b_detrow.ssdn29 - nvl(Sum(ssdn29), 0),
           b_detrow.ssdn23,
           b_detrow.ssdn26,
           b_detrow.ssdn29,
           nvl(Sum(ssdn23), 0),
           nvl(Sum(ssdn26), 0),
           nvl(Sum(ssdn29), 0) - nvl(Sum(ssdn38), 0) --修改，清算不加入票减费用
    --  nvl(Sum(ssdn29), 0)
      Into b_detrow.ssdn23,
           b_detrow.ssdn26,
           b_detrow.ssdn29,
           b_detrow.ssdn45,
           b_detrow.ssdn46,
           b_detrow.ssdn47,
           b_detrow.ssdn48,
           b_detrow.ssdn49,
           b_detrow.ssdn50
      From supsettledet, supsettlehead
     Where ssdbillno = sshbillno
       And sshthisdate <= i_enddate
       And sshthisdate >= i_startdate
       And sshcontno = i_contno
       And sshsupid = i_supid
       And sshwmid = i_wmid
       And ssdmarket = i_mkt
       And ssdmfid = i_mfid;
  
  End hisbddate;

  --计算内部领用
  Procedure mflydate(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                     i_supid     In Varchar2,
                     i_wmid      In Char,
                     i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                     i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                     i_startdate In Date,
                     i_enddate   In Date) Is
    lbrand contmanaframe.cmfbrand%Type;
  
  Begin
    If b_hd.sshdjlb Not In (billtypewm2, billtypewm3) Then
      Return;
    End If;
  
    -- 取得品牌
    Begin
      Select cmfbrand
        Into lbrand
        From contmanaframe
       Where cmfcontno = i_contno
         And cmfmfid = i_mfid
         And cmfmarket = i_mkt
         And cmfbrand = '0';
    
      --全部品牌
      Select nvl(Sum(nvl(jglhsjjje, 0) + nvl(jgln13, 0)), 0) * -1
        Into b_detrow.ssdn36
        From jxcgoodslist
       Where jgltran In ('B', 'c')
         And jglsupid = i_supid
         And jglwmid = i_wmid
         And jglmfid = i_mfid
         And jglmarket = i_mkt
         And jgldate <= i_enddate
         And jgldate >= i_startdate;
    
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Select nvl(Sum(nvl(jglhsjjje, 0) + nvl(jgln13, 0)), 0) * -1
          Into b_detrow.ssdn36
          From jxcgoodslist
         Where jgltran In ('B', 'c')
           And jglsupid = i_supid
           And jglwmid = i_wmid
           And jglmfid = i_mfid
           And jglmarket = i_mkt
           And jgldate <= i_enddate
           And jgldate >= i_startdate
           And jglppcode In (Select cmfbrand
                               From contmanaframe
                              Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                                And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                                And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                                And cmfbrand <> '0');
      
    End;
  
  End mflydate;

  Procedure genfqcharge(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                        i_supid     In Varchar2,
                        i_wmid      In Char,
                        i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                        i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                        i_startdate In Date,
                        i_enddate   In Date,
                        o_det       In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
    lbrand contmanaframe.cmfbrand%Type;
    lssc   supsetcharge%Rowtype;
    lsum   Number(12, 2);
    lcc    codecharge%Rowtype;
    Liszk  Varchar2(20);
  Begin
    Begin
      --Select * Into lcc From codecharge Where cccode = 'Z7';
      Select * Into lcc From codecharge Where cccode = '66';
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Return;
    End;
    Begin
      Select Cscisdeduct
        Into Liszk
        From Contsupcharge
       Where Csccontno = i_Contno
         And Cscchargecode = '66'--'Z7'
         And rownum = 1;
      Lcc.ccflag := Liszk;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Null;
    End;
  
    -- 取得品牌
    Begin
      Select cmfbrand
        Into lbrand
        From contmanaframe
       Where cmfcontno = i_contno
         And cmfmfid = i_mfid
         And cmfmarket = i_mkt
         And cmfbrand = '0';
    
      Select nvl(Sum(ssfsum), 0)
        Into lsum
        From supsetfqfy
       Where ssfsupid = i_supid
         And ssfwmid = i_wmid
         And ssfmkt = i_mkt
         And ssfmfid = i_mfid
         And ssfdate >= i_startdate
         And ssfdate <= i_enddate;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Select nvl(Sum(ssfsum), 0)
          Into lsum
          From supsetfqfy
         Where ssfsupid = i_supid
           And ssfwmid = i_wmid
           And ssfmkt = i_mkt
           And ssfmfid = i_mfid
           And ssfdate >= i_startdate
           And ssfdate <= i_enddate
           And ssfppcode In (Select cmfbrand
                               From contmanaframe
                              Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                                And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                                And cmfmarket = i_mkt
                                And cmfbrand <> '0');
    End;
  
    --07.01.30 精度 >>>>
    lsum := fround(lsum, lcc.ccnum1);
    -- <<<<
    If lsum <> 0 Then
      --负数也显示
      sp_billseq('G01', lssc.sscbillno, 'N');
      lssc.sscrowno  := 1;
      lssc.sscdjbh   := lssc.sscbillno;
      lssc.ssctype   := '0';
      lssc.sscflag   := 'M';
      lssc.sscsupid  := i_supid;
      lssc.sscwmid   := i_wmid;
      lssc.sscmarket := i_mkt;
      lssc.sscmfid   := i_mfid;
      lssc.sscdate   := i_enddate;
      lssc.sscfsdate := i_enddate;
      lssc.sscfsmon  := to_char(i_enddate, 'YYYYMM');
      lssc.sscid     := lcc.cccode;
      lssc.sscname   := lcc.ccname;
      lssc.sscmoney  := lsum;
      lssc.sscjsno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
      lssc.ssccontno := i_contno;
      lssc.inputor   := b_hd.inputor;
      lssc.inputdate := Sysdate;
      -- 记录是否帐扣
      lssc.person1       := lcc.ccflag;
      lssc.sscmemo       := '活动券分摊';
      lssc.person2       := lcc.ccprt;
      lssc.sscsetpl      := b_hd.sshmkt;
      lssc.sscgdmoney    := 0;
      lssc.sscmoneyupper := fmoney2chn(lsum);
      lssc.Sscnum2       := nvl(lcc.Ccnum5, 0); --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
      lssc.Sscnum3       := round(lssc.sscmoney / (1 + lssc.Sscnum2), 2); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
      Insert Into supsetcharge
        (sscbillno,
         sscrowno,
         sscdjbh,
         ssctype,
         sscflag,
         sscsupid,
         sscwmid,
         sscmarket,
         sscmfid,
         sscdate,
         sscfsdate,
         sscfsmon,
         sscid,
         sscname,
         sscmoney,
         sscjsno,
         ssccontno,
         inputor,
         inputdate,
         auditor,
         auditdate,
         person1,
         person2,
         person3,
         person4,
         person5,
         sscmemo,
         sscsetpl,
         sscgdmoney,
         sscmoneyupper,
         Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
         Sscnum3) --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
      Values
        (lssc.sscbillno,
         lssc.sscrowno,
         lssc.sscdjbh,
         lssc.ssctype,
         lssc.sscflag,
         lssc.sscsupid,
         lssc.sscwmid,
         lssc.sscmarket,
         lssc.sscmfid,
         lssc.sscdate,
         lssc.sscfsdate,
         lssc.sscfsmon,
         lssc.sscid,
         lssc.sscname,
         lssc.sscmoney,
         lssc.sscjsno,
         lssc.ssccontno,
         lssc.inputor,
         lssc.inputdate,
         lssc.auditor,
         lssc.auditdate,
         lssc.person1,
         lssc.person2,
         lssc.person3,
         lssc.person4,
         lssc.person5,
         lssc.sscmemo,
         lssc.sscsetpl,
         lssc.sscgdmoney,
         lssc.sscmoneyupper,
         lssc.Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
         lssc.Sscnum3); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
    
      If lssc.person1 = 'Y' Then
        --帐扣费用
        o_det.ssdn38 := o_det.ssdn38 + lssc.sscmoney;
      Elsif lssc.person1 = 'N' Then
        o_det.ssdn30 := o_det.ssdn30 + lssc.sscmoney;
      Else
        o_det.ssdn70 := o_det.ssdn70 + lssc.sscmoney;
      End If;
    End If;
  End genfqcharge;

  --积分费用
  Procedure Genbjfftcharge(i_Contno    In Varchar2,
                           i_Supid     In Varchar2,
                           i_Wmid      In Char,
                           i_Mkt       In Varchar2,
                           i_Mfid      In Varchar2,
                           i_Startdate In Date,
                           i_Enddate   In Date,
                           o_det       In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
    Lssc Supsetcharge%Rowtype;
    Lsum Number(12, 4);
    lPP  Number(12, 4);
    Lcc  Codecharge%Rowtype;
  
  Begin
    Begin
      Select * Into Lcc From Codecharge Where Cccode = 'Z8';
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Return;
    End;
  
    Lsum := 0;
    For vpp In (Select Distinct cmfbrand
                  From contmanaframe
                 Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                   And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                   And cmfmarket = i_mkt) Loop
      Select Nvl(Sum(Bgdje), 0)
        Into lPP
        From Bjfsupftday
       Where Bgddate >= i_Startdate
         And Bgddate <= i_Enddate
         And Bgdsupid = i_Supid
         And Bgdwmid = i_Wmid
         And Bgdmfid = i_Mfid
         And Bgdmkt = i_Mkt
         And (BgdPpcode = vpp.cmfbrand Or vpp.cmfbrand = '0');
    
      lSUM := lSUM + lPP;
    End Loop;
  
    If Lsum = 0 Or Lsum Is Null Then
      Return;
    End If;
  
    Lsum := Fround(Lsum, Lcc.Ccnum1);
    Sp_Billseq('G01', Lssc.Sscbillno, 'N');
    Lssc.Sscrowno  := 1;
    Lssc.Sscdjbh   := Lssc.Sscbillno;
    Lssc.Ssctype   := '0';
    Lssc.Sscflag   := 'M';
    Lssc.Sscsupid  := i_Supid;
    Lssc.Sscwmid   := i_Wmid;
    Lssc.Sscmarket := i_Mkt;
    Lssc.Sscmfid   := i_Mfid;
    Lssc.Sscdate   := i_Enddate;
    Lssc.Sscfsdate := i_Enddate;
    Lssc.Sscfsmon  := To_Char(i_Enddate, 'YYYYMM');
    Lssc.Sscid     := Lcc.Cccode;
    Lssc.Sscname   := Lcc.Ccname;
    Lssc.Sscmoney  := Lsum;
    Lssc.Sscjsno   := b_Hd.Sshbillno;
    Lssc.Ssccontno := i_Contno;
    Lssc.Inputor   := b_Hd.Inputor;
    Lssc.Inputdate := Sysdate;
    -- 记录是否帐扣
    Lssc.Person1       := Lcc.Ccflag;
    Lssc.Sscmemo       := '积分分摊';
    Lssc.Person2       := Lcc.Ccprt;
    Lssc.Sscsetpl      := b_Hd.Sshmkt;
    Lssc.Sscgdmoney    := 0;
    Lssc.Sscmoneyupper := Fmoney2chn(Lsum);
    lssc.Sscnum2       := nvl(lcc.Ccnum5, 0); --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
    lssc.Sscnum3       := round(lssc.sscmoney / (1 + lssc.Sscnum2), 2); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
    Insert Into Supsetcharge
      (Sscbillno,
       Sscrowno,
       Sscdjbh,
       Ssctype,
       Sscflag,
       Sscsupid,
       Sscwmid,
       Sscmarket,
       Sscmfid,
       Sscdate,
       Sscfsdate,
       Sscfsmon,
       Sscid,
       Sscname,
       Sscmoney,
       Sscjsno,
       Ssccontno,
       Inputor,
       Inputdate,
       Auditor,
       Auditdate,
       Person1,
       Person2,
       Person3,
       Person4,
       Person5,
       Sscmemo,
       Sscsetpl,
       Sscgdmoney,
       Sscmoneyupper,
       Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
       Sscnum3) --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
    Values
      (Lssc.Sscbillno,
       Lssc.Sscrowno,
       Lssc.Sscdjbh,
       Lssc.Ssctype,
       Lssc.Sscflag,
       Lssc.Sscsupid,
       Lssc.Sscwmid,
       Lssc.Sscmarket,
       Lssc.Sscmfid,
       Lssc.Sscdate,
       Lssc.Sscfsdate,
       Lssc.Sscfsmon,
       Lssc.Sscid,
       Lssc.Sscname,
       Lssc.Sscmoney,
       Lssc.Sscjsno,
       Lssc.Ssccontno,
       Lssc.Inputor,
       Lssc.Inputdate,
       Lssc.Auditor,
       Lssc.Auditdate,
       Lssc.Person1,
       Lssc.Person2,
       Lssc.Person3,
       Lssc.Person4,
       Lssc.Person5,
       Lssc.Sscmemo,
       Lssc.Sscsetpl,
       Lssc.Sscgdmoney,
       Lssc.Sscmoneyupper,
       lssc.Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
       lssc.Sscnum3); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
  
    If Lssc.Person1 = 'Y' Then
      --帐扣费用
      o_det.Ssdn38 := o_det.Ssdn38 + Lssc.Sscmoney;
    Elsif lssc.Person1 = 'N' Then
      o_det.Ssdn30 := o_det.Ssdn30 + Lssc.Sscmoney;
    Else
      o_det.Ssdn70 := o_det.Ssdn70 + Lssc.Sscmoney;
    End If;
  End;
  --积分费用
  Procedure Genparkftcharge(i_Contno    In Varchar2,
                            i_Supid     In Varchar2,
                            i_Wmid      In Char,
                            i_Mkt       In Varchar2,
                            i_Mfid      In Varchar2,
                            i_Startdate In Date,
                            i_Enddate   In Date,
                            o_det       In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
    Lssc Supsetcharge%Rowtype;
    Lsum Number(12, 4);
    lPP  Number(12, 4);
    Lcc  Codecharge%Rowtype;
  
  Begin
    Begin
      Select * Into Lcc From Codecharge Where Cccode = 'Z9';
    
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Return;
      
    End;
  
    Lsum := 0;
    For vpp In (Select Distinct cmfbrand
                  From contmanaframe
                 Where cmfcontno = i_contno
                   And cmfmfid = i_mfid
                   And cmfmarket = i_mkt) Loop
      Select Nvl(Sum(Bgdje), 0)
        Into lPP
        From dbusrmkt.Bparksupftday
       Where Bgddate >= i_Startdate
         And Bgddate <= i_Enddate
         And Bgdsupid = i_Supid
         And Bgdwmid = i_Wmid
         And Bgdmfid = i_Mfid
         And Bgdmkt = i_Mkt
         And (BgdPpcode = vpp.cmfbrand Or vpp.cmfbrand = '0');
    
      lSUM := lSUM + lPP;
    End Loop;
  
    If Lsum = 0 Or Lsum Is Null Then
      Return;
    End If;
  
    Lsum := Fround(Lsum, Lcc.Ccnum1);
    Sp_Billseq('G01', Lssc.Sscbillno, 'N');
    Lssc.Sscrowno  := 1;
    Lssc.Sscdjbh   := Lssc.Sscbillno;
    Lssc.Ssctype   := '0';
    Lssc.Sscflag   := 'M';
    Lssc.Sscsupid  := i_Supid;
    Lssc.Sscwmid   := i_Wmid;
    Lssc.Sscmarket := i_Mkt;
    Lssc.Sscmfid   := i_Mfid;
    Lssc.Sscdate   := i_Enddate;
    Lssc.Sscfsdate := i_Enddate;
    Lssc.Sscfsmon  := To_Char(i_Enddate, 'YYYYMM');
    Lssc.Sscid     := Lcc.Cccode;
    Lssc.Sscname   := Lcc.Ccname;
    Lssc.Sscmoney  := Lsum;
    Lssc.Sscjsno   := b_Hd.Sshbillno;
    Lssc.Ssccontno := i_Contno;
    Lssc.Inputor   := b_Hd.Inputor;
    Lssc.Inputdate := Sysdate;
    -- 记录是否帐扣
    Lssc.Person1       := Lcc.Ccflag;
    Lssc.Sscmemo       := '停车券分摊';
    Lssc.Person2       := Lcc.Ccprt;
    Lssc.Sscsetpl      := b_Hd.Sshmkt;
    Lssc.Sscgdmoney    := 0;
    Lssc.Sscmoneyupper := Fmoney2chn(Lsum);
    lssc.Sscnum2       := nvl(lcc.Ccnum5, 0); --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
    lssc.Sscnum3       := round(lssc.sscmoney / (1 + lssc.Sscnum2), 2); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
    Insert Into Supsetcharge
      (Sscbillno,
       Sscrowno,
       Sscdjbh,
       Ssctype,
       Sscflag,
       Sscsupid,
       Sscwmid,
       Sscmarket,
       Sscmfid,
       Sscdate,
       Sscfsdate,
       Sscfsmon,
       Sscid,
       Sscname,
       Sscmoney,
       Sscjsno,
       Ssccontno,
       Inputor,
       Inputdate,
       Auditor,
       Auditdate,
       Person1,
       Person2,
       Person3,
       Person4,
       Person5,
       Sscmemo,
       Sscsetpl,
       Sscgdmoney,
       Sscmoneyupper,
       Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
       Sscnum3) --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
    Values
      (Lssc.Sscbillno,
       Lssc.Sscrowno,
       Lssc.Sscdjbh,
       Lssc.Ssctype,
       Lssc.Sscflag,
       Lssc.Sscsupid,
       Lssc.Sscwmid,
       Lssc.Sscmarket,
       Lssc.Sscmfid,
       Lssc.Sscdate,
       Lssc.Sscfsdate,
       Lssc.Sscfsmon,
       Lssc.Sscid,
       Lssc.Sscname,
       Lssc.Sscmoney,
       Lssc.Sscjsno,
       Lssc.Ssccontno,
       Lssc.Inputor,
       Lssc.Inputdate,
       Lssc.Auditor,
       Lssc.Auditdate,
       Lssc.Person1,
       Lssc.Person2,
       Lssc.Person3,
       Lssc.Person4,
       Lssc.Person5,
       Lssc.Sscmemo,
       Lssc.Sscsetpl,
       Lssc.Sscgdmoney,
       Lssc.Sscmoneyupper,
       lssc.Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
       lssc.Sscnum3); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
  
    If Lssc.Person1 = 'Y' Then
      --帐扣费用
      o_det.Ssdn38 := o_det.Ssdn38 + Lssc.Sscmoney;
    Elsif lssc.person1 = 'N' Then
      o_det.Ssdn30 := o_det.Ssdn30 + Lssc.Sscmoney;
    Else
      o_det.Ssdn70 := o_det.Ssdn70 + Lssc.Sscmoney;
    End If;
  
  End;

  --满赠费用
  Procedure Genmzftcharge(i_Contno    In Varchar2,
                          i_Supid     In Varchar2,
                          i_Wmid      In Char,
                          i_Mkt       In Varchar2,
                          i_Mfid      In Varchar2,
                          i_Startdate In Date,
                          i_Enddate   In Date,
                          o_det       In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
    Lssc Supsetcharge%Rowtype;

  Begin
    Begin
      Select * Into Lcc From Codecharge Where Cccode = 'Z6';
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Return;
    End;
  
    /*Lsum := 0;

                  From contmanaframe

    Lssc.Ssccontno := i_Contno;
    Lssc.Inputor   := b_Hd.Inputor;
    Lssc.Inputdate := Sysdate;
    -- 记录是否帐扣

    Values
       (Lssc.Sscbillno,
        Lssc.Sscrowno,

  Procedure Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd In Out Settlepaydet%Rowtype) Is
  Begin
    In_Spd.Spdxssr := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdtc   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdyf   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdsf   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdjh   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdzkfd := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdyfk  := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdsy   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdzj   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdfy1  := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdfy2  := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdykp  := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdkp   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdn1   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdn2   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdn3   := 0;
    In_Spd.Spdn4   := 0;
  End;
  Procedure R$settlepaydet(In_Spd In Out Settlepaydet%Rowtype) Is
  Begin
    In_Spd.Spdyf := In_Spd.Spdxssr - In_Spd.Spdtc + In_Spd.Spdjh -
                    In_Spd.Spdzkfd - In_Spd.Spdyfk - In_Spd.Spdsy -
                    In_Spd.Spdzj - In_Spd.Spdfy1 - In_Spd.Spdfy2 +
                    In_spd.spdn1;
    In_Spd.Spdsf := 0; --In_Spd.Spdyf
    In_Spd.Spdkp := In_Spd.Spdxssr - In_Spd.Spdtc + In_Spd.Spdjh -
                    In_Spd.Spdzkfd - In_Spd.Spdzj - In_Spd.Spdfy1 +
                    In_spd.spdn1;
    Update Settlepaydet
       Set Spdxssr = Spdxssr + In_Spd.Spdxssr,
           Spdtc   = Spdtc + In_Spd.Spdtc,
           Spdyf   = Spdyf + In_Spd.Spdyf,
           Spdsf   = Spdsf + In_Spd.Spdsf,
           Spdjh   = Spdjh + In_Spd.Spdjh,
           Spdzkfd = Spdzkfd + In_Spd.Spdzkfd,
           Spdyfk  = Spdyfk + In_Spd.Spdyfk,
           Spdsy   = Spdsy + In_Spd.Spdsy,
           Spdzj   = Spdzj + In_Spd.Spdzj,
           Spdfy1  = Spdfy1 + In_Spd.Spdfy1,
           Spdfy2  = Spdfy2 + In_Spd.Spdfy2,
           spdkp   = spdkp + In_Spd.spdkp,
           Spdn1   = Spdn1 + In_Spd.Spdn1,
           Spdn2   = Spdn2 + In_Spd.Spdn2,
           Spdn3   = Spdn3 + In_Spd.Spdn3,
           Spdn4   = Spdn4 + In_Spd.Spdn4,
           spdykp  = spdykp + In_Spd.spdykp
     Where Spdsupid = In_Spd.Spdsupid
       And Spdwmid = In_Spd.Spdwmid
       And Spdmkt = In_Spd.Spdmkt
       And Spdmfid = In_Spd.Spdmfid
       And Spdmcontno = In_Spd.Spdmcontno
       And Spdcontno = In_Spd.Spdcontno
       And Spdbillno = In_Spd.Spdbillno
       And Spddjlb = In_Spd.Spddjlb
       And Spdjssdate = In_Spd.Spdjssdate
       And Spdjsedate = In_Spd.Spdjsedate;
    If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Or Sql%Rowcount Is Null Then
      Insert Into Settlepaydet Values In_Spd;
    End If;
  End;
  Procedure Gensettlepaydet(p_Billno In Varchar2) Is
    r_Ssh  Supsettlehead%Rowtype;
    In_Spd Settlepaydet%Rowtype;
  Begin
    Delete From Settlepaydet Where Spdbillno = p_Billno;
    Select * Into r_Ssh From Supsettlehead Where Sshbillno = p_Billno;
  
    In_Spd.Spdsupid   := r_Ssh.Sshsupid;
    In_Spd.Spdwmid    := r_Ssh.Sshwmid;
    In_Spd.Spdmkt     := r_Ssh.Sshmkt;
    In_Spd.Spdmcontno := r_Ssh.Sshcontno;
    In_Spd.Spdcontno  := r_Ssh.Sshcontno;
    In_Spd.Spdbillno  := r_Ssh.Sshbillno;
    In_Spd.Spddjlb    := r_Ssh.Sshdjlb;
    In_Spd.Spdjssdate := r_Ssh.Sshlastdate + 1;
    In_Spd.Spdjsedate := r_Ssh.Sshthisdate;
    --In_Spd.Spdchr1    := 'N';
    For Vr In (Select Sppmfid, Sum(Sppactpay) Yfje
                 From Supprepay
                Where Sppsettleno = p_Billno
                  And Spptype = '1'
                Group By Sppmfid) Loop
      In_Spd.Spdmfid := Vr.Sppmfid;
      Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
      In_Spd.Spdyfk := Vr.Yfje;
      R$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
    End Loop;
    For Vr In (Select Sppmfid, Sum(sppuhxmoney) Yfje
                 From Supprepay, Supprepay_Usage
                Where Spptype = '2'
                  And sppusetno = p_Billno
                  And sppubillno = sppbillno
                Group By Sppmfid) Loop
      In_Spd.Spdmfid := Vr.Sppmfid;
      Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
      In_Spd.Spdyfk := Vr.Yfje;
      R$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
    End Loop;
    --票扣费用生成
    For Vr In (Select Sscmfid,
                      Sum(decode(person1, 'Y', sscmoney, 0)) fyje1,
                      Sum(decode(person1, 'N', sscmoney, 0)) fyje2
                 From supsetcharge
                Where sscjsno = p_Billno
                  And Sscflag Not In ('G', 'N')
                Group By Sscmfid) Loop
      In_Spd.Spdmfid := Vr.Sscmfid;
      Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
      In_Spd.Spdfy1 := Vr.fyje1;
      In_Spd.Spdfy2 := Vr.fyje2;
      R$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
    End Loop;
  
    For Vr In (Select Ssdmfid, Sum(Ssdn63) zj
                 From Supsettledet
                Where Ssdvc5 = '6'
                  And Ssdbillno = p_Billno
                Group By Ssdmfid) Loop
      In_Spd.Spdmfid := Vr.Ssdmfid;
      Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
      In_Spd.Spdzj := Vr.zj;
      R$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
    End Loop;
    If r_Ssh.Sshdjlb = Billtypeoth Then
      For Vr In (Select Ssdmfid,
                        Sum(Decode(Ssdvc6, '0', Ssdn61 - Ssdn77, 0)) Xssr,
                        Sum(Ssdn63) Tc,
                        Sum(Decode(Ssdvc6, '0', Ssdn61 - Ssdn77, 0)) -
                        Sum(Ssdn63) Yfje
                   From Supsettledet
                  Where Ssdvc5 = '3'
                    And Ssdbillno = p_Billno
                  Group By Ssdmfid) Loop
        In_Spd.Spdmfid := Vr.Ssdmfid;
        Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
        In_Spd.Spdxssr := Vr.Xssr;
        In_Spd.Spdtc   := Vr.Tc;
        R$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
      End Loop;
    
    Elsif r_Ssh.Sshdjlb = Billtypewm1 Then
      For Vr In (Select Ssdmfid, Sum(Ssdn8) Zkfd
                   From Supsettledet_Ex
                  Where Ssdbillno = p_Billno
                  Group By Ssdmfid) Loop
        In_Spd.Spdmfid := Vr.Ssdmfid;
        Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
        In_Spd.Spdzkfd := Vr.Zkfd;
        R$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
      End Loop;
      For Vr In (Select Ssdmfid, Sum(Ssdn15) Jhje, Sum(Ssdn21) Yfk
                   From Supsettledet, Supsettlehead
                  Where Ssdbillno = Sshbillno
                    And Sshbillno = p_Billno
                  Group By Ssdmfid) Loop
        In_Spd.Spdmfid := Vr.Ssdmfid;
        Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
        In_Spd.Spdjh  := Vr.Jhje;
        In_Spd.Spdyfk := Vr.Yfk;
        R$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
      End Loop;
    
    Elsif r_Ssh.Sshdjlb In (Billtypewm2, Billtypewm3) Then
      For Vr In (Select Ssdmfid,
                        Sum(Ssdn9) Xssr,
                        Sum((Ssdn29 + Ssdn23 + Ssdn26)) Tc,
                        Sum(Ssdn36) ly,
                        Sum(Nvl(Ssdn35, 0)) Sy
                   From Supsettledet, Supsettlehead
                  Where Ssdbillno = Sshbillno
                    And Sshbillno = p_Billno
                    And Ssdvc5 = '2'
                  Group By Ssdmfid) Loop
        In_Spd.Spdmfid := Vr.Ssdmfid;
        Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
        In_Spd.Spdxssr := Vr.Xssr;
        In_Spd.Spdtc   := Vr.Tc;
        In_Spd.Spdsy   := Vr.Sy;
        in_spd.spdn1   := Vr.ly;
        R$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
      End Loop;
    
    Elsif r_Ssh.Sshdjlb = Billtypeqsd Then
      For Vr In (Select Ssdmfid, Sum((Ssdn29 + Ssdn23 + Ssdn26)) Tc
                 
                   From Supsettledet
                  Where Ssdbillno = p_Billno
                    And Ssdvc5 = '2'
                  Group By Ssdmfid) Loop
        In_Spd.Spdmfid := Vr.Ssdmfid;
        Init$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
        In_Spd.Spdtc := Vr.Tc;
        R$settlepaydet(In_Spd);
      End Loop;
    End If;
  End;
  Procedure contcharge(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                       i_supid     In Varchar2,
                       i_wmid      In Char,
                       i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                       i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                       i_startdate In Date,
                       i_enddate   In Date,
                       o_det       In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
    Cursor cur_csc Is
      Select contsupcharge.*,
             contsupcharge.ROWID,
             ccdeftype,
             ccprt,
             ccnum1,
             greatest(csceffdate, i_startdate) startdate,
             least(csclapdate, i_enddate) enddate,
             codecharge.Ccnum5 tax --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
        From contsupcharge, codecharge
       Where csccontno = i_contno
         And cscmarket = i_mkt
         And cscmfid = i_mfid
         And cscflag = 'N'
         And cscismcjs <> '4'
         And csceffdate <= i_enddate
         And csclapdate >= i_startdate
         And cscchargecode = cccode;
  
    --liulei 090924  cscismcjs<>'4' 购物中心预收性费用排除掉
    l_startdate Date;
    l_money     Number;
    l_expmoney  Number;
    l_detrow    supsettledet%Rowtype;
    l_ssc       supsetcharge%Rowtype;
    l_begindate Date;
    l_enddate   Date;
    l_dayrate   Number;
    l_amount    Number;
    l_a         Varchar2(2);
    l_b         Number;
  Begin
    For row_csc In cur_csc Loop
      l_money     := 0;
      l_begindate := row_csc.startdate;
      l_enddate   := row_csc.enddate;
      If row_csc.cscismcjs = setmodemy Then
        --每月
        If row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypegdje Then
          --固定金额
          -- EORV-1012 =  =P~ 2018.09.07 比例由6位小数扩大到保留10位小数
          l_dayrate := trunc(months_between(trunc(row_csc.enddate, 'MON'),
                                            trunc(row_csc.startdate, 'MON'))) - 1 +
                       round((trunc(row_csc.enddate) -
                             trunc(row_csc.enddate, 'MON') + 1) /
                             (last_day(trunc(row_csc.enddate)) -
                             trunc(row_csc.enddate, 'MON') + 1),
                             10) + round((last_day(trunc(row_csc.startdate)) -
                                         trunc(row_csc.startdate) + 1) /
                                         (last_day(trunc(row_csc.startdate)) -
                                         trunc(row_csc.startdate, 'MON') + 1),
                                         10);
          l_money   := round(row_csc.cscvalue * l_dayrate, 2);
        End If;
      
        --liulei 090710
      Elsif row_csc.cscismcjs = setmodemt Then
        --每天
        Select row_csc.enddate - row_csc.startdate
          Into l_dayrate
          From dual;
      
        l_money := round(row_csc.cscvalue * l_dayrate, 2);
      
      Else
        --每次/一次
        If row_csc.ccdeftype In (chargetypexssr,
                                 chargetypexsje,
                                 chargetypexssl,
                                 chargetypexscb,
                                 chargetypetmxs,
                                 chargetypezcxs,
                                 chargetypevip1,
                                 chargetypevip2,
                                 chargetypevip3,
                                 chargetypevip4,
                                 chargetypevip5,
                                 chargetypexyki,
                                 chargetypexyko,
                                 chargetypefqje,
                                 chargetypesqje,
                                 chargetypexyk1,
                                 chargetypexyk2,
                                 chargetypexyk3,
                                 chargetypexyk4,
                                 chargetypexyk5,
                                 chargetypexyk6,
                                 chargetypexyk7,
                                 chargetypexyk8,
                                 chargetypexyk9,
                                 chargetypexyk10,
                                 chargetypemzk,
                                 chargetypexfjf,
                                 chargetypetaxpayerxssr,
                                 ChargeTypeVipZk1,
                                 ChargeTypeVipZk2,
                                 ChargeTypeVipZk3,
                                 ChargeTypeVipZk4,
                                 ChargeTypeVipZk5) Then
          If row_csc.startdate = i_startdate Then
            l_startdate := add_months(row_csc.startdate, -6);
          Else
            l_startdate := row_csc.startdate;
          
          End If;
        
          initdetrow(l_detrow);
          saledate(i_contno,
                   i_supid,
                   i_wmid,
                   i_mkt,
                   i_mfid,
                   l_startdate,
                   row_csc.enddate,
                   'N',
                   l_detrow);
          salesupdate(i_contno,
                      i_supid,
                      i_wmid,
                      i_mkt,
                      i_mfid,
                      l_startdate,
                      row_csc.enddate,
                      l_detrow);
        End If;
      
        If row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypegdje Then
          l_money := row_csc.cscvalue;
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexssr Then
          l_money    := round(l_detrow.ssdn9 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getchargeexp(i_contno,
                                           i_supid,
                                           i_wmid,
                                           i_mkt,
                                           i_mfid,
                                           l_startdate,
                                           row_csc.enddate,
                                           row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                           row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                           row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexsje Then
          l_money    := round(l_detrow.ssdn3 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getchargeexp(i_contno,
                                           i_supid,
                                           i_wmid,
                                           i_mkt,
                                           i_mfid,
                                           l_startdate,
                                           row_csc.enddate,
                                           row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                           row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                           row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypeyfje Then
          If i_wmid = '1' Then
            Select round((nvl(Sum(ssdn15), 0) - o_det.ssdn8) *
                         row_csc.cscvalue,
                         2)
              Into l_money
              From supsettledet
             Where ssdbillno = b_hd.sshbillno
               And ssdwmid = i_wmid
               And ssdmarket = i_mkt
               And ssdmfid = i_mfid;
          Else
            l_money := round((o_det.ssdn9 - o_det.ssdn29 - o_det.ssdn23 -
                             o_det.ssdn26) * row_csc.cscvalue,
                             2);
          End If;
          l_begindate := i_startdate;
          l_enddate   := i_enddate;
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexssl Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn44 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexscb Then
          l_money    := round(l_detrow.ssdn37 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getchargeexp(i_contno,
                                           i_supid,
                                           i_wmid,
                                           i_mkt,
                                           i_mfid,
                                           l_startdate,
                                           row_csc.enddate,
                                           row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                           row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                           row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypetmxs Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn40 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypezcxs Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn39 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypevip1 Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn47 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypevip2 Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn48 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypevip3 Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn78 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypevip4 Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn79 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypevip5 Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn80 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyki Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn45 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyko Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn46 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypefqje Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn49 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypesqje Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn50 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk1 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn51 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk2 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn52 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk3 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn53 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk4 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn54 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk5 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn55 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk6 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn56 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk7 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn57 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk8 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn58 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk9 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn59 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexyk10 Then
          l_Money    := Round(l_Detrow.Ssdn60 *
                              Getxykrate(Row_Csc.Ccdeftype) *
                              Row_Csc.Cscvalue,
                              2);
          l_Expmoney := round(getxykchargeexp(i_contno,
                                              i_supid,
                                              i_wmid,
                                              i_mkt,
                                              i_mfid,
                                              l_startdate,
                                              row_csc.enddate,
                                              row_csc.ccdeftype,
                                              row_csc.cscchargecode,
                                              row_csc.cscvalue),
                              2);
          l_Money    := l_Money + nvl(l_Expmoney, 0);
        
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypemzk Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn68 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypexfjf Then
          l_money := round(l_detrow.ssdn69 * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
        Elsif row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypetaxpayerxssr Then
          /*Select fgetprivatepara('SF'),
                 to_number(fgetprivatepara('SE'))
            Into l_a,
                 l_b
            From dual;
          If l_a = 'Y' Then
             GetSupTaxCharge(i_contno, i_supid, i_wmid, i_mkt, i_mfid, l_startdate, row_csc.enddate, l_amount);
             \*（收入 - 收入*送券额/（收入+送券额）） * 小规模税费比率*\
             If l_amount > l_b Then
                l_money := Round(l_amount * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
             End If;
          Elsif l_a = 'N' Then
             GetSupTaxCharge(i_contno, i_supid, i_wmid, i_mkt, i_mfid, l_startdate, row_csc.enddate, l_amount);
             \*（收入 - 收入*送券额/（收入+送券额）） * 小规模税费比率*\
             l_money := Round(l_amount * row_csc.cscvalue, 2);
          End If;*/
          Null;
          -- VIP折扣承担,2013.9
        Elsif Row_Csc.Ccdeftype = ChargeTypeVipZk1 Then
          l_Money := Round(l_Detrow.ssdn61 * Row_Csc.Cscvalue, 2);
        Elsif Row_Csc.Ccdeftype = ChargeTypeVipZk2 Then
          l_Money := Round(l_Detrow.ssdn62 * Row_Csc.Cscvalue, 2);
        Elsif Row_Csc.Ccdeftype = ChargeTypeVipZk3 Then
          l_Money := Round(l_Detrow.ssdn63 * Row_Csc.Cscvalue, 2);
        Elsif Row_Csc.Ccdeftype = ChargeTypeVipZk4 Then
          l_Money := Round(l_Detrow.ssdn64 * Row_Csc.Cscvalue, 2);
        Elsif Row_Csc.Ccdeftype = ChargeTypeVipZk5 Then
          l_Money := Round(l_Detrow.ssdn65 * Row_Csc.Cscvalue, 2);
        End If;
      End If;
    
      --18.8.8 zw新增费用峰值，保底值
      l_money := getmoney(l_money,
                          nvl(Row_Csc.Cscbottomvalues, 0),
                          nvl(Row_Csc.Cscpeakvalues, 0));
      --07.01.30 精度 >>>>
      l_money := fround(l_money, row_csc.ccnum1);
      -- <<<<
      If l_money <> 0 Then
        --负数也显示
        sp_billseq('G01', l_ssc.sscbillno, 'N');
        l_ssc.sscrowno  := 1;
        l_ssc.sscdjbh   := l_ssc.sscbillno;
        l_ssc.ssctype   := '0';
        l_ssc.sscflag   := 'M';
        l_ssc.sscsupid  := i_supid;
        l_ssc.sscwmid   := i_wmid;
        l_ssc.sscmarket := row_csc.cscmarket;
        l_ssc.sscmfid   := row_csc.cscmfid;
        l_ssc.sscdate   := l_begindate;
        l_ssc.sscfsdate := l_enddate;
        l_ssc.sscfsmon  := to_char(l_enddate, 'YYYYMM');
        l_ssc.sscid     := row_csc.cscchargecode;
        l_ssc.sscname   := row_csc.cscchargename;
        l_ssc.sscmoney  := l_money;
        l_ssc.sscjsno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
        l_ssc.ssccontno := i_contno;
        l_ssc.inputor   := b_hd.inputor;
        l_ssc.inputdate := Sysdate;
        -- 记录是否在 结算中扣除
        l_ssc.person1 := row_csc.cscisdeduct;
        /*IF row_csc.cscisdeduct = 'Y' THEN
          l_ssc.sscmemo := '帐扣费用';
        ELSE
          l_ssc.sscmemo := '非帐扣费用';
        END IF;*/
      
        l_ssc.person2       := row_csc.ccprt;
        l_ssc.sscsetpl      := b_hd.sshmkt;
        l_ssc.sscgdmoney    := 0;
        l_ssc.sscmoneyupper := fmoney2chn(l_money);
        l_ssc.sscret        := row_csc.cscisret;
        l_ssc.sscretdate    := row_csc.cscretdate;
        l_ssc.sscretstatus  := 'N';
        l_ssc.Sscnum2       := nvl(row_csc.tax, 0); --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
        l_ssc.Sscnum3       := round(l_ssc.sscmoney / (1 + l_ssc.Sscnum2),
                                     2); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
        Insert Into supsetcharge
          (sscbillno,
           sscrowno,
           sscdjbh,
           ssctype,
           sscflag,
           sscsupid,
           sscwmid,
           sscmarket,
           sscmfid,
           sscdate,
           sscfsdate,
           sscfsmon,
           sscid,
           sscname,
           sscmoney,
           sscjsno,
           ssccontno,
           inputor,
           inputdate,
           auditor,
           auditdate,
           person1,
           person2,
           person3,
           person4,
           person5,
           sscmemo,
           sscsetpl,
           sscgdmoney,
           sscmoneyupper,
           sscret,
           sscretdate,
           sscretstatus,
           Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
           Sscnum3) --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
        Values
          (l_ssc.sscbillno,
           l_ssc.sscrowno,
           l_ssc.sscdjbh,
           l_ssc.ssctype,
           l_ssc.sscflag,
           l_ssc.sscsupid,
           l_ssc.sscwmid,
           l_ssc.sscmarket,
           l_ssc.sscmfid,
           l_ssc.sscdate,
           l_ssc.sscfsdate,
           l_ssc.sscfsmon,
           l_ssc.sscid,
           l_ssc.sscname,
           l_ssc.sscmoney,
           l_ssc.sscjsno,
           l_ssc.ssccontno,
           l_ssc.inputor,
           l_ssc.inputdate,
           l_ssc.auditor,
           l_ssc.auditdate,
           l_ssc.person1,
           l_ssc.person2,
           l_ssc.person3,
           l_ssc.person4,
           l_ssc.person5,
           l_ssc.sscmemo,
           l_ssc.sscsetpl,
           l_ssc.sscgdmoney,
           l_ssc.sscmoneyupper,
           l_ssc.sscret,
           l_ssc.sscretdate,
           l_ssc.sscretstatus,
           l_ssc.Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
           l_ssc.Sscnum3); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
      
        If row_csc.cscisdeduct = 'Y' Then
          --帐扣费用
          o_det.ssdn38 := o_det.ssdn38 + l_ssc.sscmoney;
        Elsif row_csc.cscisdeduct = 'N' Then
          o_det.ssdn30 := o_det.ssdn30 + l_ssc.sscmoney;
        Else
          o_det.ssdn70 := o_det.ssdn70 + l_ssc.sscmoney;
        End If;
      
        --合同最近一次结算单号
        Update contsupcharge
           Set cscjsbillno = b_hd.sshbillno
         Where Rowid = row_csc.ROWID;
        --同步更新到总部
        SettleSupExt.Sp_UpdateCharge(b_hd.sshbillno,
                                     row_csc.csccontno,
                                     row_csc.cscrowno);
      End If;
    
    End Loop;
  
  End contcharge;

  Procedure tempcharge(i_contno   In Varchar2,
                       i_supid    In Varchar2,
                       i_wmid     In Varchar2,
                       i_mkt      In Varchar2,
                       i_mfid     In Varchar2,
                       i_lastdate In Date,
                       i_thisdate In Date,
                       o_det      In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
    lmoney1 Number := 0;
    lmoney2 Number := 0;
    lmoney3 Number := 0;
  Begin
    Update supsetcharge
       Set sscjsno = b_hd.sshbillno, sscsetpl = b_hd.sshmfid, sscflag = 'M'
     Where sscsupid = i_supid
       And sscwmid = i_wmid
       And ssccontno = i_contno
       And ssctype = '1'
       And sscmarket = i_mkt
       And sscmfid = i_mfid
       And sscfsdate < i_thisdate + 1
       And sscflag = 'S';
  
    Select nvl(Sum(decode(person1, 'Y', 1, 0) * nvl(sscmoney, 0)), 0),
           nvl(Sum(decode(person1, 'N', 1, 0) * nvl(sscmoney, 0)), 0),
           nvl(Sum(decode(person1, '0', 1, 0) * nvl(sscmoney, 0)), 0)
      Into lmoney1, lmoney2, lmoney3
      From supsetcharge
     Where sscsupid = i_supid
       And sscwmid = i_wmid
       And ssccontno = i_contno
       And ssctype = '1'
       And sscmarket = i_mkt
       And sscmfid = i_mfid
       And sscfsdate < i_thisdate + 1
       And sscflag = 'M';
  
    o_det.ssdn38 := o_det.ssdn38 + lmoney1;
    o_det.ssdn30 := o_det.ssdn30 + lmoney2;
    o_det.ssdn70 := o_det.ssdn70 + lmoney3;
  End tempcharge;

  --计算税差及税费附加
  Procedure taxcharge(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                      i_supid     In Varchar2,
                      i_wmid      In Char,
                      i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                      i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                      i_startdate In Date,
                      i_enddate   In Date,
                      o_det       In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
    Cursor cur_csc Is
      Select contsupcharge.*,
             contsupcharge.ROWID,
             ccdeftype,
             ccprt,
             ccnum1,
             greatest(csceffdate, i_startdate) startdate,
             least(csclapdate, i_enddate) enddate,
             codecharge.Ccnum5 tax --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
        From contsupcharge, codecharge
       Where csccontno = i_contno
         And cscmarket = i_mkt
         And cscmfid = i_mfid
         And cscflag = 'N'
         And ccdeftype In (chargetypesffj, chargetypescje)
         And csceffdate <= i_enddate
         And csclapdate >= i_startdate
         And cscchargecode = cccode;
  
    --l_startdate DATE;
    l_money Number;
    --l_detrow  supsettledet%ROWTYPE;
    l_ssc       supsetcharge%Rowtype;
    l_begindate Date;
    l_enddate   Date;
    --l_dayrate NUMBER;
  
  Begin
    For row_csc In cur_csc Loop
      l_money     := 0;
      l_begindate := row_csc.startdate;
      l_enddate   := row_csc.enddate;
    
      If row_csc.ccdeftype = chargetypescje Then
        --计算结算金额
        If i_wmid = '1' Then
          Select nvl(Sum(ssdn15), 0) - o_det.ssdn8 - o_det.ssdn38
            Into l_money
            From supsettledet
           Where ssdbillno = b_hd.sshbillno
             And ssdwmid = i_wmid
             And ssdmarket = i_mkt
             And ssdmfid = i_mfid;
        
        Else
          l_money := o_det.ssdn9 - o_det.ssdn29 - o_det.ssdn23 -
                     o_det.ssdn26 - o_det.ssdn38;
        
        End If;
      
        l_money := round(l_money * (row_csc.cscvalue /
                         (1 + row_csc.cscvalue) - 0.04 / 1.04),
                         2); --* 1.11
      Else
        Select decode(1 - row_csc.cscvalue,
                      0,
                      0,
                      round(nvl(Sum(sscmoney), 0) * row_csc.cscvalue /
                            (1 - row_csc.cscvalue),
                            2))
          Into l_money
          From supsetcharge, codecharge
         Where sscjsno = b_hd.sshbillno
           And ccdeftype <> chargetypesffj
           And sscid = cccode
           And cctax = 'Y'
           And sscmarket = row_csc.cscmarket
           And sscmfid = row_csc.cscmfid;
      
      End If;
    
      --07.01.30 精度 >>>>
      l_money := fround(l_money, row_csc.ccnum1);
      -- <<<<
      If l_money <> 0 Then
        --负数也显示
        sp_billseq('G01', l_ssc.sscbillno, 'N');
        l_ssc.sscrowno  := 1;
        l_ssc.sscdjbh   := l_ssc.sscbillno;
        l_ssc.ssctype   := '0';
        l_ssc.sscflag   := 'M';
        l_ssc.sscsupid  := i_supid;
        l_ssc.sscwmid   := i_wmid;
        l_ssc.sscmarket := row_csc.cscmarket;
        l_ssc.sscmfid   := row_csc.cscmfid;
        l_ssc.sscdate   := l_begindate;
        l_ssc.sscfsdate := l_enddate;
        l_ssc.sscfsmon  := to_char(l_enddate, 'YYYYMM');
        l_ssc.sscid     := row_csc.cscchargecode;
        l_ssc.sscname   := row_csc.cscchargename;
        l_ssc.sscmoney  := l_money;
        l_ssc.sscjsno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
        l_ssc.ssccontno := i_contno;
        l_ssc.inputor   := b_hd.inputor;
        l_ssc.inputdate := Sysdate;
        -- 记录是否在 结算中扣除
        l_ssc.person1 := row_csc.cscisdeduct;
        /*IF row_csc.cscisdeduct = 'Y' THEN
          l_ssc.sscmemo := '帐扣费用';
        ELSE
          l_ssc.sscmemo := '非帐扣费用';
        END IF;*/
      
        l_ssc.person2       := row_csc.ccprt;
        l_ssc.sscsetpl      := b_hd.sshmkt;
        l_ssc.sscgdmoney    := 0;
        l_ssc.sscmoneyupper := fmoney2chn(l_money);
        l_ssc.Sscnum2       := nvl(row_csc.tax, 0); --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
        l_ssc.Sscnum3       := round(l_ssc.sscmoney / (1 + l_ssc.Sscnum2),
                                     2); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
        Insert Into supsetcharge
          (sscbillno,
           sscrowno,
           sscdjbh,
           ssctype,
           sscflag,
           sscsupid,
           sscwmid,
           sscmarket,
           sscmfid,
           sscdate,
           sscfsdate,
           sscfsmon,
           sscid,
           sscname,
           sscmoney,
           sscjsno,
           ssccontno,
           inputor,
           inputdate,
           auditor,
           auditdate,
           person1,
           person2,
           person3,
           person4,
           person5,
           sscmemo,
           sscsetpl,
           sscgdmoney,
           sscmoneyupper,
           Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
           Sscnum3) --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
        Values
          (l_ssc.sscbillno,
           l_ssc.sscrowno,
           l_ssc.sscdjbh,
           l_ssc.ssctype,
           l_ssc.sscflag,
           l_ssc.sscsupid,
           l_ssc.sscwmid,
           l_ssc.sscmarket,
           l_ssc.sscmfid,
           l_ssc.sscdate,
           l_ssc.sscfsdate,
           l_ssc.sscfsmon,
           l_ssc.sscid,
           l_ssc.sscname,
           l_ssc.sscmoney,
           l_ssc.sscjsno,
           l_ssc.ssccontno,
           l_ssc.inputor,
           l_ssc.inputdate,
           l_ssc.auditor,
           l_ssc.auditdate,
           l_ssc.person1,
           l_ssc.person2,
           l_ssc.person3,
           l_ssc.person4,
           l_ssc.person5,
           l_ssc.sscmemo,
           l_ssc.sscsetpl,
           l_ssc.sscgdmoney,
           l_ssc.sscmoneyupper,
           l_ssc.Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
           l_ssc.Sscnum3); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
      
        If row_csc.cscisdeduct = 'Y' Then
          --帐扣费用
          o_det.ssdn38 := o_det.ssdn38 + l_ssc.sscmoney;
        Elsif row_csc.cscisdeduct = 'N' Then
          o_det.ssdn30 := o_det.ssdn30 + l_ssc.sscmoney;
        Else
          o_det.ssdn70 := o_det.ssdn70 + l_ssc.sscmoney;
        End If;
      
        --合同最近一次结算单号
        Update contsupcharge
           Set cscjsbillno = b_hd.sshbillno
         Where Rowid = row_csc.ROWID;
        SettleSupExt.Sp_UpdateCharge(b_hd.sshbillno,
                                     row_csc.csccontno,
                                     row_csc.cscrowno);
      End If;
    
    End Loop;
  
  End taxcharge;

  Procedure calccharge(i_contno    In Varchar2,
                       i_supid     In Varchar2,
                       i_wmid      In Char,
                       i_mkt       In Varchar2,
                       i_mfid      In Varchar2,
                       i_startdate In Date,
                       i_enddate   In Date,
                       o_det       In Out supsettledet%Rowtype) Is
  Begin
    --生成促销相关费用
    Genbjfftcharge(i_contno,
                   i_supid,
                   i_wmid,
                   i_mkt,
                   i_mfid,
                   i_startdate,
                   i_enddate,
                   o_det);
    Genparkftcharge(i_contno,
                    i_supid,
                    i_wmid,
                    i_mkt,
                    i_mfid,
                    i_startdate,
                    i_enddate,
                    o_det);
    Genmzftcharge(i_contno,
                  i_supid,
                  i_wmid,
                  i_mkt,
                  i_mfid,
                  i_startdate,
                  i_enddate,
                  o_det);
    --合同费用
    contcharge(i_contno,
               i_supid,
               i_wmid,
               i_mkt,
               i_mfid,
               i_startdate,
               i_enddate,
               o_det);
    --临时费用
    tempcharge(i_contno,
               i_supid,
               i_wmid,
               i_mkt,
               i_mfid,
               i_startdate,
               i_enddate,
               o_det);
    --计算返券费用
    genfqcharge(i_contno,
                i_supid,
                i_wmid,
                i_mkt,
                i_mfid,
                i_startdate,
                i_enddate,
                o_det);
    --计算税差及税费附加费用
    taxcharge(i_contno,
              i_supid,
              i_wmid,
              i_mkt,
              i_mfid,
              i_startdate,
              i_enddate,
              o_det);
  End calccharge;

  -- 经销结算单是否货到付款
  -- 是货到付款才能 按商品算 "应付款比率"和"出入库售价金额比率"费用
  Function ishdfk(i_mfid In Varchar2) Return Char Is
    l_hdfk  Char(1) := 'Y';
    l_cnts  Integer;
    row_ssb settlesupbatch%Rowtype;
  
  Begin
    --帐期设置记录大于1，不是货到付款
    Select Count(1)
      Into l_cnts
      From (Select Distinct ssbday, ssbrate
              From settlesupbatch
             Where ssbjsbillno = b_hd.sshbillno
               And ssbmmfid = i_mfid
               And ssbcontno = b_hd.sshcontno);
  
    If l_cnts > 1 Then
      Return 'N';
    End If;
  
    If l_cnts = 1 Then
      Select Distinct ssbday, ssbrate
        Into row_ssb.ssbday, row_ssb.ssbrate
        From settlesupbatch
       Where ssbjsbillno = b_hd.sshbillno
         And ssbmmfid = i_mfid
         And ssbcontno = b_hd.sshcontno;
    
      --row_ssb.ssbday : 帐期天数
      --row_ssb.ssbrate: 付款比率
      If row_ssb.ssbday <> 0 And row_ssb.ssbrate <> 1 Then
        Return 'N';
      End If;
    
    End If;
  
    Return l_hdfk;
  End;

  Procedure calcdetrow(i_billtype In Char,
                       i_supid    In Varchar2,
                       i_wmid     In Char,
                       i_contno   In Varchar2,
                       i_lastdate In Date,
                       i_thisdate In Date) Is
    lstartdate   Date;
    lenddate     Date;
    l_orderno    Varchar2(20);
    l_isbd       Char(1);
    lbdstartdate Date;
    lbdenddate   Date;
    l_isqs       Char(1);
    lqsstartdate Date;
    lqsenddate   Date;
    l_isqsflag   Char(1);
    i            Number;
    l_qsbdtc     Number;
    l_qsxstc     Number;
    l_qscetc     Number;
    l_qsxskhtc   number;
  Begin
    lstartdate := i_lastdate + 1;
    lenddate   := i_thisdate;
    If i_billtype = billtypewm1 Then
      For r_ssb In (Select *
                      From settlesupbatch
                     Where ssbjhdate + ssbday <= i_thisdate
                       And ssbsupid = i_supid
                       And ssbwmid = i_wmid
                       And ssbstatus = 'N'
                       And ssbisjs = 'Y'
                       And ssbtran In ('1', '2', 'U', 'V')
                       And ssbflag = 'Y'
                       And ssbcontno = i_contno) Loop
        If r_ssb.ssbcontno <> i_contno Then
          raise_application_error(errcode,
                                  '->6.9 批次范围选择错误，一份合同生成一张结算单！');
        End If;
      
        b_detrow.ssdbillno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
        b_detrow.ssdmarket   := r_ssb.ssbmmkt;
        b_detrow.ssdmfid     := r_ssb.ssbmmfid;
        b_detrow.ssdwmid     := r_ssb.ssbwmid;
        b_detrow.ssdcontno   := i_contno;
        b_detrow.ssdybillno  := r_ssb.ssbbillno;
        b_detrow.ssdydjbh    := r_ssb.ssbdjbh;
        b_detrow.ssdlastdate := i_lastdate;
        b_detrow.ssdthisdate := i_thisdate;
        If r_ssb.ssbtran = '1' Then
          b_detrow.ssdvc1 := '入库';
        Elsif r_ssb.ssbtran = '2' Then
          b_detrow.ssdvc1 := '退厂';
        Else
          b_detrow.ssdvc1 := '调整';
        End If;
      
        If r_ssb.ssbcontno = '0' Then
          raise_application_error(errcode,
                                  '->6.8 经销结算批次必须指定合同号！单据编号为:[' ||
                                  r_ssb.ssbbillno || '],事务:[' ||
                                  b_detrow.ssdvc1 || ']。');
        End If;
      
        b_detrow.ssdvc3 := r_ssb.ssbmmkt; --MMKT
        b_detrow.ssdvc4 := r_ssb.ssbmmfid; --MMFID
        b_detrow.ssdvc5 := '1'; --入库
        b_detrow.ssdd1  := r_ssb.ssbjhdate; --发生日期
        b_detrow.ssdd2  := r_ssb.ssbjhdate + r_ssb.ssbday;
        initdetrow(b_detrow);
        If r_ssb.ssbtran = 'U' Then
          b_detrow.ssdn19 := r_ssb.ssbhsje;
          b_detrow.ssdn20 := r_ssb.ssbbhsje;
        Else
          b_detrow.ssdn17 := r_ssb.ssbhsje;
          b_detrow.ssdn18 := r_ssb.ssbbhsje;
        End If;
      
        --更新 预付款supsetyfk.ssyjsdh
        Begin
          Select bihorderno
            Into l_orderno
            From binstrhead
           Where bihbillno = r_ssb.ssbbillno
             And bihflag = binstr.flagapproved;
        
          Update supsetyfk
             Set ssyjsdh = b_hd.sshbillno, ssyjsbz = 'Y'
           Where ssyorderno = l_orderno
             And ssysupid = i_supid
             And ssywmid = i_wmid
             And ssyflag = bsupyfk.flagapproved;
        Exception
          When no_data_found Then
            Null;
        End;
        b_detrow.ssdn21 := nvl(r_ssb.ssbn4, 0); --含税预付款
        b_detrow.ssdn22 := nvl(r_ssb.ssbn5, 0); --不含税预付款
        b_detrow.ssdn15 := r_ssb.ssbhsje; -- - Nvl(r_ssb.ssbn4,0;
        b_detrow.ssdn16 := r_ssb.ssbbhsje; -- - Nvl(r_ssb.ssbn5,0);
        b_detrow.ssdn6  := b_detrow.ssdn15 - b_detrow.ssdn16;
        -- 进项税率
        b_detrow.ssdn35 := nvl(r_ssb.ssbn3, 0);
        --出入库售价金额
        b_detrow.ssdn36 := r_ssb.ssbn2;
        --增加单据明细
        If b_detrow.ssdn16 <> 0 Then
          b_rowno           := b_rowno + 1;
          b_detrow.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
          insertdetail(b_detrow);
          -- 更新记录
          Update settlesupbatch
             Set ssbjsbillno = b_hd.sshbillno, ssbjsdjbh = b_hd.sshdjbh
           Where ssbseq = r_ssb.ssbseq
             And ssbmmkt = r_ssb.ssbmmkt;
        End If;
      
        --计算合计
        adddettot(b_dettot, b_detrow);
      End Loop;
    
      --计算销售供计算费用
      If i_thisdate > b_cont.cmlapdate Then
        lenddate := b_cont.cmlapdate;
      Else
        lenddate := i_thisdate;
      End If;
    
      For vcg In (Select Distinct cmfmarket, cmfmfid
                    From contmanaframe
                   Where cmfcontno = i_contno) Loop
        --初始DETAIL行记录
        b_dettemp.ssdbillno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
        b_dettemp.ssdmarket   := vcg.cmfmarket;
        b_dettemp.ssdmfid     := vcg.cmfmfid;
        b_dettemp.ssdwmid     := i_wmid;
        b_dettemp.ssdcontno   := i_contno;
        b_dettemp.ssdybillno  := Null;
        b_dettemp.ssdydjbh    := Null;
        b_dettemp.ssdlastdate := i_lastdate;
        b_dettemp.ssdthisdate := i_thisdate;
        b_dettemp.ssdvc1      := Null;
        b_dettemp.ssdvc2      := Null;
        b_dettemp.ssdvc3      := Null;
        b_dettemp.ssdvc4      := Null;
        b_dettemp.ssdvc5      := '2'; --销售
        b_dettemp.ssdd1       := Null;
        b_dettemp.ssdd2       := Null;
        initdetrow(b_dettemp);
        --计算基本数据  n1-n20
        saledate(i_contno,
                 i_supid,
                 i_wmid,
                 vcg.cmfmarket,
                 vcg.cmfmfid,
                 lstartdate,
                 lenddate,
                 'N',
                 b_dettemp);
        --计算费用
        calccharge(i_contno,
                   i_supid,
                   i_wmid,
                   vcg.cmfmarket,
                   vcg.cmfmfid,
                   lstartdate,
                   lenddate,
                   b_dettemp);
        adddettot(b_dettemptot, b_dettemp);
        --记录扩展表
        If b_dettemp.ssdn8 <> 0 Then
          Insert Into supsettledet_ex
          Values
            (b_dettemp.ssdbillno,
             b_dettemp.ssdrowno,
             b_dettemp.ssdmarket,
             b_dettemp.ssdmfid,
             b_dettemp.ssdwmid,
             b_dettemp.ssdcontno,
             b_dettemp.ssdybillno,
             b_dettemp.ssdydjbh,
             b_dettemp.ssdlastdate,
             b_dettemp.ssdthisdate,
             b_dettemp.ssdvc1,
             b_dettemp.ssdvc2,
             b_dettemp.ssdvc3,
             b_dettemp.ssdvc4,
             b_dettemp.ssdvc5,
             b_dettemp.ssdd1,
             b_dettemp.ssdd2,
             b_dettemp.ssdn1,
             b_dettemp.ssdn2,
             b_dettemp.ssdn3,
             b_dettemp.ssdn4,
             b_dettemp.ssdn5,
             b_dettemp.ssdn6,
             b_dettemp.ssdn7,
             b_dettemp.ssdn8,
             b_dettemp.ssdn9,
             b_dettemp.ssdn10);
        End If;
      End Loop;
    Else
      For vcg In (Select Distinct cmfmarket, cmfmfid
                    From contmanaframe
                   Where cmfcontno = i_contno) Loop
        --分扣率记录销售汇总
        ins_ssd_bykl(i_contno,
                     i_supid,
                     i_wmid,
                     vcg.cmfmarket,
                     vcg.cmfmfid,
                     lstartdate,
                     lenddate);
      
        --初始DETAIL行记录
        b_detrow.ssdbillno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
        b_detrow.ssdmarket   := vcg.cmfmarket;
        b_detrow.ssdmfid     := vcg.cmfmfid;
        b_detrow.ssdwmid     := i_wmid;
        b_detrow.ssdcontno   := i_contno;
        b_detrow.ssdybillno  := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdydjbh    := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdlastdate := i_lastdate;
        b_detrow.ssdthisdate := i_thisdate;
        b_detrow.ssdvc1      := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdvc2      := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdvc3      := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdvc4      := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdvc5      := '2'; --销售
        b_detrow.ssdd1       := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdd2       := Null;
        initdetrow(b_detrow);
        If b_bdtype = '2' Then
          l_isqsflag    := b_isqs;
          b_unioncontno := Null;
          InitContBd(i_contno, vcg.cmfmarket, vcg.cmfmfid);
          --得到保底期
          b_isqs := '0';
          SaleBdRange(i_contno,
                      vcg.cmfmarket,
                      vcg.cmfmfid,
                      lstartdate,
                      lenddate,
                      l_isbd,
                      lbdstartdate,
                      lbdenddate);
          --多保底点可以在一个帐期进行计算
          If b_bd.COUNT > 0 Then
            For i In 1 .. b_bd.COUNT Loop
              SaleStatBdByRange(i_contno,
                                i_supid,
                                i_wmid,
                                vcg.cmfmarket,
                                vcg.cmfmfid,
                                lstartdate,
                                lenddate,
                                l_isbd,
                                b_bd         (i).startdate,
                                b_bd         (i).enddate,
                                i,
                                'N',
                                l_qsbdtc,
                                l_qsxstc,
                                l_qscetc,
                                l_qsxskhtc);
            End Loop;
          Else
            SaleStatBdByRange(i_contno,
                              i_supid,
                              i_wmid,
                              vcg.cmfmarket,
                              vcg.cmfmfid,
                              lstartdate,
                              lenddate,
                              l_isbd,
                              Null,
                              Null,
                              0,
                              'N',
                              l_qsbdtc,
                              l_qsxstc,
