                              l_qscetc,
                              l_qsxskhtc);
          End If;
          --得到清算期
          b_isqs := '1';
          --是否联合保底
          GetUnionBdCont(i_contno,
                         vcg.cmfmarket,
                         vcg.cmfmfid,
                         lstartdate,
                         lenddate);
          SaleQsRange(i_contno,
                      vcg.cmfmarket,
                      vcg.cmfmfid,
                      lstartdate,
                      lenddate,
                      l_isqs,
                      lqsstartdate,
                      lqsenddate);
          If b_qs.COUNT > 0 Then
            For i In 1 .. b_qs.COUNT Loop
              SaleStatQsByRange(i_contno,
                                i_supid,
                                i_wmid,
                                vcg.cmfmarket,
                                vcg.cmfmfid,
                                lstartdate,
                                lenddate,
                                l_isqs,
                                b_qs         (i).startdate,
                                b_qs         (i).enddate,
                                b_qs         (i).unionflag);
            End Loop;
          End If;
          b_isqs := l_isqsflag;
        Else
          --计算基本数据  n1-n20
          salestat(i_contno,
                   i_supid,
                   i_wmid,
                   vcg.cmfmarket,
                   vcg.cmfmfid,
                   lstartdate,
                   lenddate);
        End If;
        --计算代销领用
        mflydate(i_contno,
                 i_supid,
                 i_wmid,
                 vcg.cmfmarket,
                 vcg.cmfmfid,
                 lstartdate,
                 lenddate);
        --计算费用
        calccharge(i_contno,
                   i_supid,
                   i_wmid,
                   vcg.cmfmarket,
                   vcg.cmfmfid,
                   lstartdate,
                   lenddate,
                   b_detrow);
        --增加单据明细
        If b_detrow.ssdn9 <> 0 Or b_detrow.ssdn17 <> 0 Or
           b_detrow.ssdn19 <> 0 Or b_detrow.ssdn8 <> 0 Or
           b_detrow.ssdn28 <> 0 Or b_detrow.ssdn29 <> 0 Or
           b_detrow.ssdn21 <> 0 Or b_detrow.ssdn23 <> 0 or
           b_detrow.ssdn75 <> 0 Then
          b_rowno           := b_rowno + 1;
          b_detrow.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
          insertdetail(b_detrow);
        End If;
        --genbjfftcharge(i_contno, i_supid, i_wmid, vcg.cmfmarket, vcg.cmfmfid, lstartdate, lenddate);
        --Genparkftcharge(i_contno, i_supid, i_wmid, vcg.cmfmarket, vcg.cmfmfid, lstartdate, lenddate);
        --计算合计
        adddettot(b_dettot, b_detrow);
      
        --salecostday_set
        initssdsrow(b_scds);
        b_scds.scdsmkt  := vcg.cmfmarket;
        b_scds.scdsmfid := vcg.cmfmfid;
        b_scds.scdsxssr := b_detrow.ssdn9;
        --开票费用 + 销售应提 + 保底提成 + 超额提成 + 佣金调整 + 成本代销 内部调拨
        Select b_detrow.ssdn38 + (b_detrow.ssdn29 + b_detrow.ssdn23 +
               b_detrow.ssdn26 + b_detrow.ssdn73) +
               decode(b_hd.sshwmid, '2', b_detrow.ssdn36, 0)
          Into b_scds.scdsml
          From dual;
      
        --
        b_scds.scdsjjje := b_scds.scdsxssr - b_scds.scdsml;
        If b_scds.scdsxssr <> 0 Then
          b_scds.scdskl := round(b_scds.scdsml / b_scds.scdsxssr, 4);
        Else
          b_scds.scdskl := 0;
        
        End If;
      
        insertscds(b_scds);
        --salecostday_set end
      
        Popsalebdce(i_contno,
                    i_supid,
                    i_wmid,
                    vcg.cmfmarket,
                    vcg.cmfmfid,
                    lstartdate,
                    lenddate);
      End Loop;
    
    End If;
    --更新保底税率
    --update supsettledet set ssdn80 = 0.13 where ssdvc6 = '2';
    update supsettledet set ssdn80 = 0.13 where ssdvc6 in ('7','8');
  End calcdetrow;

  Procedure calcdetrowqs(i_billtype In Char,
                         i_supid    In Varchar2,
                         i_wmid     In Char,
                         i_contno   In Varchar2,
                         i_lastdate In Date,
                         i_thisdate In Date) Is
    lstartdate Date;
    lenddate   Date;
    lexists    Number;
  Begin
    lstartdate := i_lastdate + 1;
    lenddate   := i_thisdate;
    If i_wmid = stock.wm_jx Then
      --清算前将压批数据置为可结算
      Update settlesupbatch
         Set ssbflag = 'Y', ssbisjs = 'Y', ssbday = i_thisdate - ssbjhdate
       Where ssbcontno = i_contno
         And ssbsupid = i_supid
         And ssbwmid = i_wmid
         And ssbflag = 'N'; -- AND ssbtype = '2' AND ssbtran ='1';
      For r_ssb In (Select *
                      From settlesupbatch
                     Where ssbjhdate + ssbday <= i_thisdate
                       And ssbsupid = i_supid
                       And ssbwmid = i_wmid
                       And ssbstatus = 'N'
                       And ssbisjs = 'Y'
                       And ssbtran In ('1', '2', 'U', 'V')
                       And ssbflag = 'Y'
                       And ssbcontno = i_contno) Loop
        If r_ssb.ssbcontno <> i_contno Then
          raise_application_error(errcode,
                                  '->6.9 批次范围选择错误，一份合同生成一张清算单！');
        End If;
      
        b_detrow.ssdbillno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
        b_detrow.ssdmarket   := r_ssb.ssbmmkt;
        b_detrow.ssdmfid     := r_ssb.ssbmmfid;
        b_detrow.ssdwmid     := r_ssb.ssbwmid;
        b_detrow.ssdcontno   := i_contno;
        b_detrow.ssdybillno  := r_ssb.ssbbillno;
        b_detrow.ssdydjbh    := r_ssb.ssbdjbh;
        b_detrow.ssdlastdate := i_lastdate;
        b_detrow.ssdthisdate := i_thisdate;
        If r_ssb.ssbtran = '1' Then
          b_detrow.ssdvc1 := '入库';
        Elsif r_ssb.ssbtran = '2' Then
          b_detrow.ssdvc1 := '退厂';
        
        Else
          b_detrow.ssdvc1 := '调整';
        
        End If;
      
        If r_ssb.ssbcontno = '0' Then
          raise_application_error(errcode,
                                  '->6.8 经销结算批次必须指定合同号！单据编号为:[' ||
                                  r_ssb.ssbbillno || '],事务:[' ||
                                  b_detrow.ssdvc1 || ']。');
        End If;
      
        b_detrow.ssdvc3 := r_ssb.ssbmmkt; --MMKT
        b_detrow.ssdvc4 := r_ssb.ssbmmfid; --MMFID
        b_detrow.ssdvc5 := '1'; --入库
        b_detrow.ssdd1  := r_ssb.ssbjhdate; --发生日期
        b_detrow.ssdd2  := r_ssb.ssbjhdate + r_ssb.ssbday;
        initdetrow(b_detrow);
        If r_ssb.ssbtran = 'U' Then
          b_detrow.ssdn19 := r_ssb.ssbhsje;
          b_detrow.ssdn20 := r_ssb.ssbbhsje;
        Else
          b_detrow.ssdn17 := r_ssb.ssbhsje;
          b_detrow.ssdn18 := r_ssb.ssbbhsje;
        
        End If;
      
        b_detrow.ssdn21 := nvl(r_ssb.ssbn4, 0); --含税预付款
        b_detrow.ssdn22 := nvl(r_ssb.ssbn5, 0); --不含税预付款
        b_detrow.ssdn15 := r_ssb.ssbhsje; -- - Nvl(r_ssb.ssbn4,0;
        b_detrow.ssdn16 := r_ssb.ssbbhsje; -- - Nvl(r_ssb.ssbn5,0);
        b_detrow.ssdn6  := b_detrow.ssdn15 - b_detrow.ssdn16;
        -- 进项税率
        b_detrow.ssdn35 := nvl(r_ssb.ssbn3, 0);
        --出入库售价金额
        b_detrow.ssdn36 := r_ssb.ssbn2;
        --增加单据明细
        If b_detrow.ssdn16 <> 0 Then
          b_rowno           := b_rowno + 1;
          b_detrow.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
          insertdetail(b_detrow);
          -- 更新记录
          Update settlesupbatch
             Set ssbjsbillno = b_hd.sshbillno, ssbjsdjbh = b_hd.sshdjbh
           Where ssbseq = r_ssb.ssbseq
             And ssbmmkt = r_ssb.ssbmmkt;
        
        End If;
      
        --计算合计
        adddettot(b_dettot, b_detrow);
      End Loop;
    
    Else
      For vcg In (Select Distinct cqmkt, cqmfid
                    From contqs
                   Where cqcontno = i_contno
                     And cqflag = 'Y'
                     And cqeffdate <= lenddate
                     And cqlapdate >= lstartdate) Loop
        --初始DETAIL行记录
        b_detrow.ssdbillno   := b_hd.sshbillno;
        b_detrow.ssdmarket   := vcg.cqmkt;
        b_detrow.ssdmfid     := vcg.cqmfid;
        b_detrow.ssdwmid     := i_wmid;
        b_detrow.ssdcontno   := i_contno;
        b_detrow.ssdybillno  := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdydjbh    := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdlastdate := i_lastdate;
        b_detrow.ssdthisdate := i_thisdate;
        b_detrow.ssdvc1      := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdvc2      := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdvc3      := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdvc4      := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdvc5      := '2'; --销售
        b_detrow.ssdd1       := Null;
        b_detrow.ssdd2       := Null;
        initdetrow(b_detrow);
        --计算基本数据  n1-n20
        salestat(i_contno,
                 i_supid,
                 i_wmid,
                 vcg.cqmkt,
                 vcg.cqmfid,
                 lstartdate,
                 lenddate);
        hisbddate(i_contno,
                  i_supid,
                  i_wmid,
                  vcg.cqmkt,
                  vcg.cqmfid,
                  lstartdate,
                  lenddate);
        --增加单据明细
        If b_detrow.ssdn9 <> 0 Or b_detrow.ssdn17 <> 0 Or
           b_detrow.ssdn19 <> 0 Or b_detrow.ssdn8 <> 0 Or
           b_detrow.ssdn28 <> 0 Or b_detrow.ssdn29 <> 0 Or
           b_detrow.ssdn21 <> 0 Or b_detrow.ssdn23 <> 0 Then
          b_rowno           := b_rowno + 1;
          b_detrow.ssdrowno := b_rowno;
          insertdetail(b_detrow);
        End If;
      
        --计算合计
        adddettot(b_dettot, b_detrow);
        --salecostday_set
        initssdsrow(b_scds);
        b_scds.scdsmkt := vcg.cqmkt;
      
        b_scds.scdsmfid := vcg.cqmfid;
        b_scds.scdsxssr := b_detrow.ssdn9;
        --开票费用 + 销售应提 + 保底提成 + 超额提成 + 成本代销 内部调拨
        Select b_detrow.ssdn38 + (b_detrow.ssdn29 + b_detrow.ssdn23 +
               b_detrow.ssdn26 + b_detrow.ssdn73) +
               decode(b_hd.sshwmid, '2', b_detrow.ssdn36, 0)
          Into b_scds.scdsml
          From dual;
      
        --
        b_scds.scdsjjje := b_scds.scdsxssr - b_scds.scdsml;
        If b_scds.scdsxssr <> 0 Then
          b_scds.scdskl := round(b_scds.scdsml / b_scds.scdsxssr, 4);
        Else
          b_scds.scdskl := 0;
        
        End If;
      
        insertscds(b_scds);
        --salecostday_set end
      End Loop;
    End If;
  End calcdetrowqs;

  --生成未结数据清单
  Procedure GenUnsettleData(i_sdate In Date,
                            i_edate In Date,
                            i_mkt   In Varchar2,
                            i_supid In Varchar2,
                            i_wmid  In Char) Is
    row_explist supsettleexplist%Rowtype;
    Cursor c_salelist(vsdate Date,
                      vedate Date,
                      vmkt   Varchar2,
                      vsupid Varchar2,
                      vwmid  Char) Is
      Select scdmkt mkt,
             scdmfid mfid,
             scdsupid supid,
             scdwmid wmid,
             Round(Nvl(Sum(xssjje + pfsjje), 0), 2) sjje,
             Round(Nvl(Sum(xssr + pfsr ), 0), 2) xssr,
             Round(Nvl(Sum(xshsjjje + pfhsjjje), 0), 2) hsjjje,
             Round(Nvl(Sum(xshsjjad + pfhsjjad), 0), 2) hsjjadj,
             Round(Nvl(Sum(xssupzk + pfsupzk), 0), 2) supzk
        From salecostday
       Where scdhsrq >= vsdate
         And scdhsrq <= vedate
         And scdmkt = vmkt
         And scdsupid = vsupid
         And scdwmid = vwmid
         And Not Exists (Select 'x'
                From salecostday_supset
               Where scdsdate = scddate
                 And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                 And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                 And scdscatid = scdcatid
                 And scdssupid = scdsupid
                 And scdswmid = scdwmid
                 And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                 And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                 And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                    --AND scdsmd = scdmd
                 And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                  and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                 And scdstmtype = scdtmtype)
       Group By scdmkt, scdmfid, scdsupid, scdwmid;
    row_salelist c_salelist%Rowtype;
    Cursor c_chargelist(vsdate Date,
                        vedate Date,
                        vmkt   Varchar2,
                        vsupid Varchar2,
                        vwmid  Char) Is
      Select sscmarket mkt,
             sscmfid mfid,
             sscsupid supid,
             sscwmid wmid,
             Round(Nvl(Sum(sscmoney), 0), 2) chargeamount
        From supsetcharge
       Where ssctype = '1'
         And sscflag = 'S'
         And sscfsdate < vedate + 1
         And auditdate >= vsdate
         And auditdate < vedate + 1
         And sscmarket = vmkt
         And sscsupid = vsupid
         And sscwmid = vwmid
       Group By sscmarket, sscmfid, sscsupid, sscwmid;
    row_chargelist c_chargelist%Rowtype;
  Begin
    Delete From supsettleexplist
     Where sselsdate >= i_sdate
       And sseledate <= i_edate
       And sselmkt = i_mkt
       And sselsupid = i_supid
       And sselwmid = i_wmid;
    row_explist             := Null;
    row_explist.sselsdate   := i_sdate;
    row_explist.sseledate   := i_edate;
    row_explist.sselsetflag := 'N';
    --1.未结算销售数据
    Open c_salelist(i_sdate, i_edate, i_mkt, i_supid, i_wmid);
    Loop
      Fetch c_salelist
        Into row_salelist;
      Exit When c_salelist%Notfound Or c_salelist%Notfound Is Null;
      row_explist.sselmkt     := row_salelist.mkt;
      row_explist.sselmfid    := row_salelist.mfid;
      row_explist.sselsupid   := row_salelist.supid;
      row_explist.sselwmid    := row_salelist.wmid;
      row_explist.sselxssjje  := row_salelist.sjje;
      row_explist.sselxssr    := row_salelist.xssr;
      row_explist.sselxscb    := row_salelist.hsjjje;
      row_explist.sselxscbadj := row_salelist.hsjjadj;
      row_explist.sselxssupzk := row_salelist.supzk;
      Update supsettleexplist
         Set sselxssjje  = sselxssjje + row_explist.sselxssjje,
             sselxssr    = sselxssr + row_explist.sselxssr,
             sselxscb    = sselxscb + row_explist.sselxscb,
             sselxscbadj = sselxscbadj + row_explist.sselxscbadj,
             sselxssupzk = sselxssupzk + row_explist.sselxssupzk
       Where sselsdate = row_explist.sselsdate
         And sseledate = row_explist.sseledate
         And sselmkt = row_explist.sselmkt
         And sselmfid = row_explist.sselmfid
         And sselsupid = row_explist.sselsupid
         And sselwmid = row_explist.sselwmid;
      If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Then
        Insert Into supsettleexplist
          (sselsdate,
           sseledate,
           sselmkt,
           sselmfid,
           sselsupid,
           sselwmid,
           sselxssjje,
           sselxssr,
           sselxscb,
           sselxscbadj,
           sselxssupzk)
        Values
          (row_explist.sselsdate,
           row_explist.sseledate,
           row_explist.sselmkt,
           row_explist.sselmfid,
           row_explist.sselsupid,
           row_explist.sselwmid,
           row_explist.sselxssjje,
           row_explist.sselxssr,
           row_explist.sselxscb,
           row_explist.sselxscbadj,
           row_explist.sselxssupzk);
        If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Then
          raise_application_error(errcode,
                                  '->1.供应商[' || row_explist.sselsupid ||
                                  ']记录未结算销售数据失败!');
        End If;
      End If;
    End Loop;
    Close c_salelist;
    --2.未结算临时费用
    Open c_chargelist(i_sdate, i_edate, i_mkt, i_supid, i_wmid);
    Loop
      Fetch c_chargelist
        Into row_chargelist;
      Exit When c_chargelist%Notfound Or c_chargelist%Notfound Is Null;
      row_explist.sselmkt    := row_chargelist.mkt;
      row_explist.sselmfid   := row_chargelist.mfid;
      row_explist.sselsupid  := row_chargelist.supid;
      row_explist.sselwmid   := row_chargelist.wmid;
      row_explist.sselcharge := row_chargelist.chargeamount;
      Update supsettleexplist
         Set sselcharge = sselcharge + row_explist.sselcharge
       Where sselsdate = row_explist.sselsdate
         And sseledate = row_explist.sseledate
         And sselmkt = row_explist.sselmkt
         And sselmfid = row_explist.sselmfid
         And sselsupid = row_explist.sselsupid
         And sselwmid = row_explist.sselwmid;
      If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Then
        Insert Into supsettleexplist
          (sselsdate,
           sseledate,
           sselmkt,
           sselmfid,
           sselsupid,
           sselwmid,
           sselcharge)
        Values
          (row_explist.sselsdate,
           row_explist.sseledate,
           row_explist.sselmkt,
           row_explist.sselmfid,
           row_explist.sselsupid,
           row_explist.sselwmid,
           row_explist.sselcharge);
        If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Then
          raise_application_error(errcode,
                                  '->2.供应商[' || row_explist.sselsupid ||
                                  ']记录未结算临时费用数据失败!');
        End If;
      End If;
    End Loop;
    Close c_chargelist;
  End GenUnsettleData;

  --更新未结清单中当前结算数据
  Procedure UptUnsettleData(i_sethead In supsettlehead%Rowtype,
                            i_neg     In Char) Is
    Cursor c_explist(vsupid Varchar2, vwmid Char) Is
      Select *
        From supsettleexplist
       Where sselsetflag = 'N'
         And sselsupid = vsupid
         And sselwmid = vwmid
       Order By sselsdate
         For Update;
    row_explist supsettleexplist%Rowtype;
  Begin
    If i_sethead.sshbillno Is Null Or i_sethead.sshsupid Is Null Or
       i_sethead.sshwmid Is Null Then
      Return;
    End If;
    If i_sethead.sshwmid = '1' Then
      Return;
    End If;
    Open c_explist(i_sethead.sshsupid, i_sethead.sshwmid);
    Loop
      Fetch c_explist
        Into row_explist;
      Exit When c_explist%Notfound Or c_explist%Notfound Is Null;
      Begin
        Select Round(Nvl(Sum(xssjje + pfsjje), 0), 2),
               Round(Nvl(Sum(xssr + pfsr ), 0), 2),
               Round(Nvl(Sum(xshsjjje + pfhsjjje), 0), 2),
               Round(Nvl(Sum(xshsjjad + pfhsjjad), 0), 2),
               Round(Nvl(Sum(xssupzk + pfsupzk), 0), 2)
          Into row_explist.sselsetxssjje,
               row_explist.sselsetxssr,
               row_explist.sselsetxscb,
               row_explist.sselsetxscbadj,
               row_explist.sselsetxssupzk
          From salecostday
         Where scdhsrq >= row_explist.sselsdate
           And scdhsrq <= row_explist.sseledate
           And scdmkt = row_explist.sselmkt
           And scdmfid = row_explist.sselmfid
           And scdsupid = row_explist.sselsupid
           And scdwmid = row_explist.sselwmid
           And Exists
         (Select 'x'
                  From salecostday_supset
                 Where scdsdate = scddate
                   And scdsmkt = scdmkt
                   And scdsmfid = scdmfid
                   And scdscatid = scdcatid
                   And scdssupid = scdsupid
                   And scdswmid = scdwmid
                   And scdstaxtype = scdtaxtype
                   And scdsxstax = scdxstax
                   And scdshsrq = scdhsrq
                      --AND scdsmd = scdmd
                   And scdsbrand = scdbrand
                   And scdstmtype = scdtmtype
                    and scdsjjtax =scdjjtax
                   And scdsjsbillno = i_sethead.sshbillno);
        If i_neg = 'Y' Then
          row_explist.sselsetxssjje  := (-1) * row_explist.sselsetxssjje;
          row_explist.sselsetxssr    := (-1) * row_explist.sselsetxssr;
          row_explist.sselsetxscb    := (-1) * row_explist.sselsetxscb;
          row_explist.sselsetxscbadj := (-1) * row_explist.sselsetxscbadj;
          row_explist.sselsetxssupzk := (-1) * row_explist.sselsetxssupzk;
        End If;
      Exception
        When Others Then
          row_explist.sselsetxssjje  := 0;
          row_explist.sselsetxssr    := 0;
          row_explist.sselsetxscb    := 0;
          row_explist.sselsetxscbadj := 0;
          row_explist.sselsetxssupzk := 0;
      End;
      Begin
        Select Round(Nvl(Sum(sscmoney), 0), 2)
          Into row_explist.sselsetcharge
          From supsetcharge
         Where ssctype = '1'
           And auditdate >= row_explist.sselsdate
           And auditdate < row_explist.sseledate + 1
           And sscmarket = row_explist.sselmkt
           And sscmfid = row_explist.sselmfid
           And sscsupid = row_explist.sselsupid
           And sscwmid = row_explist.sselwmid
           And sscjsno = i_sethead.sshbillno;
        If i_neg = 'Y' Then
          row_explist.sselsetcharge := (-1) * row_explist.sselsetcharge;
        End If;
      Exception
        When Others Then
          row_explist.sselsetcharge := 0;
      End;
      If row_explist.sselsetxssjje <> 0 Or row_explist.sselsetxssr <> 0 Or
         row_explist.sselsetxscb <> 0 Or row_explist.sselsetxscbadj <> 0 Or
         row_explist.sselsetxssupzk <> 0 Or row_explist.sselsetcharge <> 0 Then
        Update supsettleexplist
           Set sselsetxssjje  = sselsetxssjje + row_explist.sselsetxssjje,
               sselsetxssr    = sselsetxssr + row_explist.sselsetxssr,
               sselsetxscb    = sselsetxscb + row_explist.sselsetxscb,
               sselsetxscbadj = sselsetxscbadj + row_explist.sselsetxscbadj,
               sselsetxssupzk = sselsetxssupzk + row_explist.sselsetxssupzk,
               sselsetcharge  = sselsetcharge + row_explist.sselsetcharge,
               sselsettleno   = i_sethead.sshbillno,
               sselsetdate    = Null
         Where Current Of c_explist;
        If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Then
          Null;
        End If;
      End If;
    End Loop;
    Close c_explist;
  End UptUnsettleData;

  Procedure deletesetbill(i_billno In Varchar2) Is
    row_bh supsettlehead%Rowtype;
  Begin
    Begin
      Select * Into row_bh From supsettlehead Where sshbillno = i_billno;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        row_bh := Null;
    End;
  
    Delete From supsettlehead Where sshbillno = i_billno;
  
    If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '结算单[' || i_billno || ']不存在，无法删除！');
    End If;
  
    Delete From supsettledet Where ssdbillno = i_billno;
  
    --扩展表 by liujun 20080411
    Delete From supsettledet_ex Where ssdbillno = i_billno;
  
    Delete From supsetcharge
     Where sscjsno = i_billno
       And ssctype = '0'
       And sscflag <> 'Y';
  
    Update supsetcharge
       Set sscjsno = Null, sscflag = 'S'
     Where sscjsno = i_billno
       And ssctype = '1';
    Update supsetcharge
       Set sscisqs = Null, sscqssettleno = Null
     Where sscqssettleno = i_billno
       And ssctype = '1';
  
    --预付款单
    --一次性核销预付款
    Update supprepay
       Set sppsettleno = Null, sppstatus = /*'P'*/ 'Y' --2015.12.09 =  =P~ 状态'P'造成混乱,直接使用Y
     Where sppsettleno = i_billno
       And Spptype = '1';
    --手工核销预付款
    Update supprepay
       Set sppsettleno = Decode(Nvl(sppvc1, '#'), '#', Null, sppvc1),
           sppstatus   = Decode(Nvl(sppvc2, '#'), '#', 'P', sppvc2)
     Where sppsettleno = i_billno
       And Spptype = '2';
  
    --清除未结算清单
    If row_bh.sshdjlb <> billtypeqsd Then
      UptUnsettleData(row_bh, 'Y');
    End If;
  
    Delete From salecostday_supset
     Where scdsjsflag = 'N'
       And scdsjsbillno = i_billno;
  
    Delete From jxcgoodslistseq Where jglssupjsdh = i_billno;
  
    Update settlesupbatch
       Set ssbstatus = 'N', ssbjsbillno = Null, ssbjsdjbh = Null
     Where ssbjsbillno = i_billno;
    Delete From Settlepaydet Where SPDBILLNO = i_billno;
  
    ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- 2011.01.01
    -- 预付款
    Update SupPrePay Set sppsettleno = Null Where sppsettleno = i_billno;
    Delete From supprepay_usage Where SPPUSETNO = i_billno;
    --应收应付
    supcamana.jsgen(i_billno);
    ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    Delete From SUPSETTLEDETBD Where SSbJsBillNo = i_BillNo;
    --temp
    --supcamana.jsgen(i_billno);
    --删除应收应付明细
    --settleaccpayday.delpaydet(i_billno);
    --COMMIT;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Raise;
      Rollback;
    
  End;

  Procedure SupsetSunYi(i_billno In supsettlehead.sshbillno%Type) Is
    l_ssh  supsettlehead%Rowtype;
    l_jsdh Varchar2(50);
    l_je   Number Default 0;
    l_mfje Number Default 0;
  
    Cursor cur_jgl Is
      Select DBUSRMKT.JXCGOODSLIST.*,
             --DECODE(TA.JGLSSUPJSDH,NULL,'N','Y') flag
             'Y' flag
        From DBUSRMKT.JXCGOODSLIST,
             (Select *
                From DBUSRSET.JXCGOODSLISTSEQ
               Where JGLSSUPJSDH = i_billno) TA
       Where JGLSUPID = l_ssh.sshsupid
         And JGLWMID = l_ssh.sshwmid
         And JGLDATE <= l_ssh.sshthisdate
         And JGLDATE >= add_months(l_ssh.sshthisdate, -6)
         And JGLTRAN In ('7', '8')
         And NVL(JGLVC6, 'N') = 'Y'
         And Exists (Select *
                From CONTMANAFRAME
               Where CMFCONTNO = l_ssh.sshcontno
                 And CMFMFID = JGLMFID
                 And (CMFBRAND = '0' Or CMFBRAND = JGLPPCODE))
         And Not Exists (Select *
                From DBUSRSET.JXCGOODSLISTSEQ
               Where JGLSMARKET = JGLMARKET
                 And JGLSSEQ = JGLSEQ
                 And JGLSSUPJSDH <> i_billno)
         And JGLMARKET = TA.JGLSMARKET(+)
         And JGLSEQ = TA.JGLSSEQ(+)
       Order By JGLMARKET, JGLSEQ;
  
    row_jgl cur_jgl%Rowtype;
  Begin
    Begin
      Select * Into l_ssh From supsettlehead Where sshbillno = i_billno;
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                i_billno || '结算单不存在，不能进行损溢处理!');
    End;
  
    If l_ssh.sshflag = 'Y' Or l_ssh.sshflag = 'E' Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              i_billno || '已审核或结付款，不能进行损溢处理!');
    End If;
  
    If l_ssh.sshdjlb <> '2' And l_ssh.sshdjlb <> '6' Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              i_billno || '非代销结算单，不能进行损溢处理!');
    End If;
  
    Delete From jxcgoodslistseq
     Where jglssupjsdh = i_billno
       And jglssupjsbz = 'N';
    Update supsettledet Set ssdn35 = 0 Where ssdbillno = i_billno;
  
    Open cur_jgl;
    Loop
      Fetch cur_jgl
        Into row_jgl;
      Exit When cur_jgl%Notfound Or cur_jgl%Notfound Is Null;
      If row_jgl.flag = 'Y' Then
        Begin
          Select jglssupjsdh
            Into l_jsdh
            From DBUSRSET.jxcgoodslistseq
           Where jglsseq = row_jgl.jglseq
             And jglsmarket = row_jgl.jglmarket;
        
          If NVL(l_jsdh, '') <> '' And l_jsdh <> i_billno Then
            raise_application_error(errcode,
                                    '有部分盘点单已被结算单[' || l_jsdh ||
                                    ']处理，不能重复处理！');
          End If;
        Exception
          When No_Data_Found Then
            Null;
          When Others Then
            Raise;
        End;
        l_mfje := 0 - row_jgl.jglhsjjje;
        Update supsettledet
           Set ssdn35 = ssdn35 + l_mfje
         Where ssdbillno = i_billno
           And ssdmarket = row_jgl.jglmarket
           And ssdmfid = row_jgl.jglmfid
           And ssdvc5 = '2'
           And rownum = 1;
        If Sql%Rowcount = 1 Then
          Delete From jxcgoodslistseq
           Where jglsseq = row_jgl.jglseq
             And jglsmarket = row_jgl.jglmarket;
        
          Insert Into jxcgoodslistseq
          Values
            (row_jgl.jglseq, row_jgl.jglmarket, 'N', i_billno);
        
          l_je := l_je + l_mfje;
        Else
          raise_application_error(errcode,
                                  '结算单' || i_billno ||
                                  '中没有该柜组的销售数据，不能处理损溢！');
        End If;
      End If;
    End Loop;
  
    Update supsettlehead
       Set sshtotyfje = sshtotyfje - sshn10 + l_je, sshn10 = l_je
     Where sshbillno = i_billno;
  
    recalcsum(i_billno);
  End;

  Procedure recalcsum(i_billno In supsettlehead.sshbillno%Type,
                      i_flag   In Varchar2 Default '%') Is
    l_ssh supsettlehead%Rowtype;
  
  Begin
    Begin
      Select *
        Into l_ssh
        From supsettlehead
       Where sshbillno = i_billno
         For Update;
    
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode, i_billno || '结算单不存在!');
      
    End;
  
    Select nvl(Sum(decode(person1, 'Y', 1, 0) * sscmoney), 0),
           nvl(Sum(decode(person1, 'N', 1, 0) * sscmoney), 0)
      Into l_ssh.sshsetadj, l_ssh.sshtotkk
      From supsetcharge
     Where sscjsno = l_ssh.sshbillno
       And sscflag Like i_flag;
  
    l_ssh.sshsetje  := l_ssh.sshtotyfje - l_ssh.sshsetadj;
    l_ssh.sshsjfkje := l_ssh.sshlastye + l_ssh.sshsetje - l_ssh.sshtotkk -
                       nvl(l_ssh.sshadjustje, 0) - nvl(l_ssh.sshthisye, 0) -
                       nvl(l_ssh.sshyfkje, 0);
    Update supsettlehead
       Set sshsetadj = l_ssh.sshsetadj,
           sshsetje  = l_ssh.sshsetje,
           sshtotkk  = l_ssh.sshtotkk,
           sshsjfkje = l_ssh.sshsjfkje
     Where sshbillno = i_billno;
  
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Rollback;
      Raise;
    
  End recalcsum;

  /*得到所有未参加结算的预付款金额*/
  Procedure SupPrePay(p_contno    In Varchar2,
                      p_jsbillno  In Varchar2,
                      o_prepayamt Out Number) Is
  Begin
    Select Nvl(Sum(sppactpay), 0)
      Into o_prepayamt
      From supprepay
     Where sppcontno = p_contno
       And sppstatus = 'Y'
       And Spptype = '1';
    Update supprepay
       Set sppsettleno = p_jsbillno, sppstatus = BSupPrepay.FlagSettled
     Where sppcontno = p_contno
       And sppstatus = /*'P'*/
           'Y' --调整查询条件--2015.12.09 =  =P~ 状态'P'造成混乱,直接使用Y
       And Spptype = '1';
  
  End;

  Procedure submit(i_supid    In Varchar2,
                   i_wmid     In Char,
                   i_contno   In Varchar2,
                   i_thisdate In Varchar2,
                   i_person   In Varchar2,
                   i_isqs     In Char Default '0',
                   i_lastdate In Date Default Null,
                   i_iscommit In Char Default 'Y',
                   i_isbatch  In Char Default 'N',
                   o_billno   Out Varchar2) Is
    llastdate Date;
    lthisdate Date;
    llastye   Number;
    --lyfk       NUMBER;
    lbillid    Char(3);
    lbilltype  Char(1);
    lexist     Integer;
    loldbillno Varchar2(20);
    lday       Number;
    row_gsd    globsetday%Rowtype;
    lcontno    contmain.cmcontno%Type;
    --l_count    NUMBER;
    lcontlastdate Date;
    ldoname       Varchar2(20);
    llastbillno   Varchar2(20);
    v_enablerule  Char(1);
    l_prepayamt   Number;
    l_mxkpje      number := 0;
  Begin
    insert   into dbusrset.ceshi06 values (i_supid,i_wmid,i_contno,i_thisdate,i_person,i_isqs,i_lastdate,i_iscommit,i_isbatch,o_billno) ;commit;
    v_enablerule := fterp_context.get_isenablerule;
    fterp_searchrule.enablerule(False);
    b_isqs := i_isqs;
    If b_isqs Is Null Or b_isqs <> '1' Then
      b_isqs := '0';
    End If;
  
    If b_isqs = '1' Then
      If i_wmid Not In ('1', '2', '3', '4', '5') Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '只有经销、代销、联营供应商才能清算!');
      End If;
    
      lbillid   := billidqsd;
      lbilltype := billtypeqsd;
      ldoname   := '清算';
    Else
      If i_wmid = '1' Then
        lbillid   := billidwm1;
        lbilltype := billtypewm1;
      Elsif i_wmid = '2' Then
        --IN ('2', '3')
        lbillid   := billidwm2;
        lbilltype := billtypewm2;
      Elsif i_wmid = '3' Then
        lbillid   := billidwm3;
        lbilltype := billtypewm3;
      Else
        lbillid   := billidoth;
        lbilltype := billtypeoth;
      End If;
      ldoname := '结算';
    End If;
  
    Begin
      Select *
        Into b_sb
        From supplierbase
       Where sbid = i_supid
         And sbstatus = 'Y'
         And sbflag In ('0', '1', '2');
    Exception
      When Others Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '->8.' || i_supid || '供应商不存在、非正式、已停止付款!');
    End;
  
    If (i_wmid = '1' And b_sb.sbwmid1 <> 'Y') Or
       (i_wmid = '2' And b_sb.sbwmid2 <> 'Y') Or
       (i_wmid = '3' And b_sb.sbwmid3 <> 'Y') Or
       (i_wmid = '4' And b_sb.sbwmid4 <> 'Y') Or
       (i_wmid = '5' And b_sb.sbwmid5 <> 'Y') Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->9.' || i_supid || '供应商无此经营方式!');
    End If;
  
    lthisdate := to_date(i_thisdate, 'YYYY-MM-DD');
    -- 检查供应商结算日期
    If b_isqs = '0' And b_sb.sbvc8 <> '0' Then
      Begin
        Select * Into row_gsd From globsetday Where gsdid = b_sb.sbvc8;
      
      Exception
        When Others Then
          raise_application_error(errcode, '->10.供应商结算日期设置无效!');
        
      End;
    
      If last_day(lthisdate) = lthisdate Then
        --月末
        lday := 0;
      Else
        lday := to_number(substr(i_thisdate, 9, 2));
      
      End If;
    
      If row_gsd.gsdday1 <> lday And row_gsd.gsdday2 <> lday And
         row_gsd.gsdday3 <> lday And row_gsd.gsdday4 <> lday And
         row_gsd.gsdday5 <> lday Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '->11.本日不是该供应商设置的结算日!');
      End If;
    
    End If;
  
    lcontno := i_contno;
    Begin
      Select * Into b_cont From contmain Where cmcontno = lcontno;
    
    Exception
      When Others Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '->11.合同【' || lcontno || '】不存在!');
      
    End;
  
    If b_cont.cmwmid <> i_wmid Or b_cont.cmsupid <> i_supid Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->12.合同【' || lcontno || '】供应商经营方式不一致!');
    End If;
  
    -- select sbflag into v_flag from supplierbase where sbid =i_supid;
    --if v_flag in ('3','4') then
    If b_sb.sbflag In ('3', '4') Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->20' || i_supid || '供应商暂停付款');
    End If;
  
    If b_cont.cmstatus Not In ('Y', 'Q') Or b_cont.cmeffdate > lthisdate Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->13.合同【' || lcontno || '】不是有效合同!');
    End If;
  
    -- 非经销合同本次结算日前到期的合同的结算日为合同到期日
    If lthisdate > b_cont.cmlapdate And i_wmid <> '1' Then
      lthisdate := b_cont.cmlapdate;
    End If;
  
    If b_isqs = '1' Then
      If b_cont.cmsettletype <> 'Y' Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '->13.合同【' || lcontno || '】不允许清算!');
      End If;
    
      Select Count(*)
        Into lexist
        From supsettlehead
       Where sshsupid = i_supid
         And sshwmid = i_wmid
         And sshcontno = lcontno
         And sshdjlb <> lbilltype
         And
            --sshflag = flagautoed; flagSCMAPP: SCM供应商待确认状态 2007.05.31
             sshflag In (flagautoed, flagscmapp, flagSCMRej);
      If lexist > 0 Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '->14.' || i_supid || '-' || lcontno || '-' ||
                                '该供应商合同还存在未审核的结算单，不能进行清算! ');
      End If;
    End If;
  
    --2014.8.1加入审批流中间状态，有未审批完成的也不能继续。
    Select Count(*)
      Into lexist
      From supsettlehead
     Where sshsupid = i_supid
       And sshwmid = i_wmid
       And sshcontno = lcontno
       And
          --sshthisdate >= lthisdate And
           sshdjlb = lbilltype
       And sshflag In (flagInFlow, FlagFlowRej); --2014.8.1加入审批流中间状态，有未审批完成的也不能继续。
    If lexist > 0 Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->14.' || i_supid || '-' || lcontno || '-' ||
                              i_thisdate || '该供应商合同还存在未审批完成的结算单! ');
    End If;
  
    Select Count(*)
      Into lexist
      From supsettlehead
     Where sshsupid = i_supid
       And sshwmid = i_wmid
       And sshcontno = lcontno
       And sshthisdate >= lthisdate
       And sshdjlb = lbilltype
       And sshflag In (flagapproved, flagsended, flagpayed);
    If lexist > 0 Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->14.' || i_supid || '-' || lcontno || '-' ||
                              i_thisdate || '该供应商合同本日' || ldoname ||
                              '已完成! ');
    Else
      --保留结算信息相同的单据编号
      Begin
        Select sshbillno
          Into loldbillno
          From supsettlehead
         Where sshsupid = i_supid
           And sshwmid = i_wmid
           And sshcontno = lcontno
           And sshthisdate = lthisdate
           And sshdjlb = lbilltype
           And
              --sshflag = flagautoed; flagSCMAPP: SCM供应商待确认状态 2007.05.31
               sshflag In (flagautoed, flagscmapp, flagSCMRej);
      
        deletesetbill(loldbillno);
      Exception
        When Others Then
          loldbillno := '0';
        
      End;
    
      --删除未审核的单据
      For vr In (Select sshbillno
                   From supsettlehead
                  Where sshsupid = i_supid
                    And sshwmid = i_wmid
                    And sshcontno = lcontno
                    And sshdjlb = lbilltype
                    And
                       --sshflag = flagautoed flagSCMAPP: SCM供应商待确认状态 2007.05.31
                        sshflag In (flagautoed, flagscmapp, flagSCMRej)) Loop
        deletesetbill(vr.sshbillno);
      End Loop;
    
    End If;
  
    ---上次结算日期
    Select decode(b_isqs, '1', b_cont.cmlastqsdate, b_cont.cmlastsetdate)
      Into lcontlastdate
      From dual;
  
    Begin
      Select Max(sshthisdate)
        Into llastdate
        From supsettlehead
       Where sshsupid = i_supid
         And sshwmid = i_wmid
         And sshcontno = lcontno
         And sshdjlb = lbilltype
         And sshflag In (flagapproved, flagpayed);
    
      Select nvl(sshthisye, 0), nvl(sshthisdate, lcontlastdate), sshbillno
        Into llastye, llastdate, llastbillno
        From supsettlehead
       Where sshsupid = i_supid
         And sshwmid = i_wmid
         And sshcontno = lcontno
         And sshthisdate = llastdate
         And sshdjlb = lbilltype
         And sshflag In (flagapproved, flagpayed);
    
      b_firstset := 'N';
    Exception
      When Others Then
        llastye := 0;
        --llastdate := lcontlastdate;
        --第一次结算，上次日期取合同生效日期
        If lcontlastdate Is Null Then
          llastdate := trunc(b_cont.cmeffdate) - 1;
        Else
          llastdate := lcontlastdate;
        End If;
        b_firstset := 'Y';
      
    End;
  
    If i_wmid = wmid1 And b_firstset <> 'Y' Then
      llastdate := lcontlastdate;
    End If;
  
    ---liulei 购物中心使用 090709
    If i_lastdate Is Not Null Then
      llastdate := i_lastdate;
    End If;
  
    ---初始单据头
    If loldbillno = '0' Then
      sp_billseq(lbillid, b_hd.sshbillno, 'N'); --结算单号
    Else
      b_hd.sshbillno := loldbillno; --如果是从新生成，则不改变单据编号
    
    End If;
  
    b_hd.sshdjbh     := b_hd.sshbillno;
    b_hd.sshdjlb     := lbilltype; --单据类别
    b_hd.sshflag     := flagautoed; --标志
    b_hd.sshsupid    := i_supid; --供应商
    b_hd.sshwmid     := i_wmid; --经营方式
    b_hd.sshmkt      := currentmkt; --结算位置
    b_hd.sshmfid     := Null;
    b_hd.sshcontno   := lcontno; --合同编号
    b_hd.sshbank     := b_cont.cmchar1; --b_sb.sbbank; --开户银行   modified by ty 2010/7/15
    b_hd.sshaccntno  := b_cont.cmchar2; --b_sb.sbaccntno; --银行帐号 modified by ty 2010/7/15
    b_hd.sshtaxno    := b_sb.sbtaxno; --纳税号
    b_hd.sshn29      := b_sb.sbtaxrate; --供应商税率，2018.05.17，leo
    b_hd.sshdate     := Sysdate; --制单日期
    b_hd.sshlastdate := llastdate; --上次结算日期
    b_hd.sshthisdate := lthisdate; --本次结算日期
    b_hd.sshlastye   := llastye; --上次计算余额
    b_hd.sshthisye   := 0; --本次计算余额
    b_hd.sshogdje    := 0; --应提成金额
    b_hd.sshmgdje    := 0; --保底提成额
    b_hd.sshaqdje    := 0; --超额提成额
    b_hd.sshtotdje   := 0; --实际提成额合计
    b_hd.sshtotyfje  := 0; --应付金额合计
    b_hd.sshtotkk    := 0; --扣款合计
    b_hd.sshyfkje    := 0; --预付款金额
    b_hd.sshadjustje := 0; --调整金额
    b_hd.sshsjfkje   := 0; --实际付款
    b_hd.sshn1       := 0; --销售收入
    b_hd.sshn2       := 0; --销售成本
    b_hd.sshn3       := 0; --供应商折扣
    b_hd.sshn4       := 0; --销售成本调整
    b_hd.sshn5       := 0; --本期进货
    b_hd.sshn6       := 0; --本期进货调整
    b_hd.sshn7       := 0; --联营销售金额(不含保底、超额)
    b_hd.sshn8       := 0; --联营销售应提(不含保底、超额)
    b_hd.sshn9       := 0; --内部领用
    b_hd.sshn10      := 0; --损溢金额
    b_hd.sshn11      := 0; --清算应结金额
    b_hd.sshn12      := 0; --清算已结金额
    b_hd.sshn13      := 0; --供应商不含税折扣，20130702
    If lbillid = billidoth And b_cont.cmweek6 = '2' Then
      b_hd.sshvc1 := '2'; --自收银
    Else
      b_hd.sshvc1 := '1'; --统一收银
    
    End If;
  
    b_hd.sshvc2     := Null;
    b_hd.sshvc3     := b_sb.sbaddr;
    b_hd.sshvc4     := b_cont.cmtype;
    b_hd.sshvc5     := b_sb.sbcname;
    b_hd.sshd1      := Null;
    b_hd.sshd2      := Null;
    b_hd.sshsupsign := Null;
    b_hd.inputor    := i_person;
    b_hd.inputdate  := Sysdate;
    b_hd.auditor    := Null;
    b_hd.auditdate  := Null;
    b_hd.buyer      := b_sb.sbyjcgy;
    b_hd.person1    := Null;
    b_hd.person2    := Null;
    b_hd.person3    := Null;
    b_hd.person4    := Null;
    b_hd.person5    := Null;
    b_hd.sshsetadj  := 0; --结算调整（开票前费用）
    b_hd.sshsetje   := 0; --结算金额
    /*b_hd.sshplanpaydate := trunc(SYSDATE) + nvl(fgetprivatepara('PL'), 0); --预计付款日期*/
    if nvl(b_sb.sbn10, 0) = 0 or b_sb.sbn10 = 0 then
      b_hd.sshplanpaydate := last_day(add_months(b_hd.sshthisdate, 1));
    elsif to_number(to_char(last_day(add_months(b_hd.sshthisdate, 1)), 'dd')) <
          b_sb.sbn10 then
      b_hd.sshplanpaydate := last_day(add_months(b_hd.sshthisdate, 1));
    else
      b_hd.sshplanpaydate := to_date(to_char(add_months(b_hd.sshthisdate, 1),
                                             'yyyy-mm') || '-' ||
                                     to_char(b_sb.sbn10),
                                     'yyyy-mm-dd');
    end if;
  
    --b_hd.sshplanpaydate := trunc(Sysdate) + nvl(b_cont.cmzqts3, 0); --预计付款日期
    b_hd.sshlastbillno := llastbillno;
    --初始DETAIL合计
    initdetrow(b_dettot);
    initdetrow(b_dettemptot);
    Delete From salecostday_supset
     Where scdsjsflag = 'N'
       And scdsjsbillno = b_hd.sshbillno;
  
    -- 修改settlesupbatch结算标志
    If i_wmid = stock.wm_jx Then
      Update settlesupbatch
         Set ssbjsbillno = Null, ssbjsdjbh = Null
       Where ssbjsbillno = b_hd.sshbillno;
    
    End If;
  
    --初始化明细行号
    b_rowno := 0; --结算单明细
    If b_isqs = '1' Then
      calcdetrowqs(lbilltype,
                   i_supid,
                   i_wmid,
                   lcontno,
                   llastdate,
                   lthisdate);
      If b_rowno = 0 Then
        If i_wmid = '1' Then
          raise_application_error(errcode,
                                  '生成清算单失败：不存在未清算数据! 【合同编号：' || 'lcontno' || '】');
        Else
          raise_application_error(errcode,
                                  '生成清算单失败：合同不存在清算条款! 【合同编号：' || 'lcontno' || '】');
        End If;
      End If;
    Else
      calcdetrow(lbilltype, i_supid, i_wmid, lcontno, llastdate, lthisdate);
      SupPrePay(lcontno, b_hd.sshbillno, l_prepayamt);
    End If;
  
    --增加单据主单
    If b_hd.sshwmid = '1' Then
      b_hd.sshn3 := b_dettemptot.ssdn8;
      b_hd.sshn5 := b_dettot.ssdn17;
      b_hd.sshn6 := b_dettot.ssdn19;
      --b_hd.sshyfkje   := b_dettot.ssdn21; 改为记录核销的预付款
      b_hd.sshn21 := b_dettot.ssdn21;
    
      b_hd.sshtotyfje := b_dettot.ssdn15 - b_hd.sshn3;
      b_hd.sshsetadj  := b_dettemptot.ssdn38;
      b_hd.sshtotkk   := b_dettemptot.ssdn30;
      --gejx,20101025
      --本期入库
      /*Select nvl(Sum(jglhsjjje), 0)
        Into b_hd.sshn13
        From jxcgoodslist,
             contmain
       Where jgldate >= cmeffdate And
             jgldate <= cmlapdate And
             jglsupid = b_hd.sshsupid And
             jglwmid = b_hd.sshwmid And
             cmcontno = b_hd.sshcontno And
             jgltran = '1';
      
      --本期退货
      Select -1 * nvl(Sum(jglhsjjje), 0)
        Into b_hd.sshn14
        From jxcgoodslist,
             contmain
       Where jgldate >= cmeffdate And
             jgldate <= cmlapdate And
             jglsupid = b_hd.sshsupid And
             jglwmid = b_hd.sshwmid And
             cmcontno = b_hd.sshcontno And
             jgltran = '2';
      --本期调整
      Select nvl(Sum(jglhsjjje), 0)
        Into b_hd.sshn15
        From jxcgoodslist,
             contmain
       Where jgldate >= cmeffdate And
             jgldate <= cmlapdate And
             jglsupid = b_hd.sshsupid And
             jglwmid = b_hd.sshwmid And
             cmcontno = b_hd.sshcontno And
             jgltran = 'U';
      --上期未结余款：前期合同中未结的金额+该合同前期未结的金额
      
      Select nvl(Sum(ssbhsje), 0)
        Into b_hd.sshn16 --前期合同中未结的金额
        From settlesupbatch
       Where ssbcontno <> ssbvc1 And
             ssbstatus <> 'Y' And
             ssbsupid = b_hd.sshsupid And
             ssbwmid = b_hd.sshwmid;
      
      
      Select nvl(Sum(ssbhsje), 0) + b_hd.sshn16
        Into b_hd.sshn16 --该合同前期未结的金额
        From settlesupbatch
       Where ssbcontno = b_hd.sshcontno And
             ssbstatus <> 'Y' And
             ssbjhdate <= llastdate And
             ssbsupid = b_hd.sshsupid And
             ssbwmid = b_hd.sshwmid;
      --本年累计入库：本自然年累计入库金额
      Select nvl(Sum(jhhsjjjede - jhhsjjjecr + jhhsjjjead), 0)
        Into b_hd.sshn20
        From jxcsupplierday
       Where jsddate >= trunc(Sysdate, 'yyyy') And
             jsddate <= lthisdate And
             jsdsupid = b_hd.sshsupid And
             jsdwmid = b_hd.sshwmid;
      --本自然年本合同的累计付款
      Select nvl(Sum(pbsf), 0)
        Into b_hd.sshn17
        From paybatch,
             suppayhead
       Where pbmcontno = b_hd.sshcontno And
             sphbillno = pbpaybillno And
             sphpaydate >= trunc(Sysdate, 'yyyy') And
             sphpaydate <= lthisdate;
      --本自然年本合同的累计销售金额
      Select nvl(Sum(xshsjjjede - xshsjjjecr + xshsjjjead), 0)
        Into b_hd.sshn18
        From jxcsupplierday
       Where jsddate >= trunc(Sysdate, 'yyyy') And
             jsddate <= lthisdate And
             jsdsupid = b_hd.sshsupid And
             jsdwmid = b_hd.sshwmid;
      --本结算单截至日的库存金额
      If lthisdate = FGETERPDATE Then
         Select nvl(Sum(gstkchsjjje), 0)
           Into b_hd.sshn19
           From goodsstock
          Where gstsupid = b_hd.sshsupid And
                (gstmarket = b_hd.sshmkt Or b_hd.sshmkt = '0') And
                gstwmid = b_hd.sshwmid;
      Else
         Select nvl(Sum(gstkchsjjje), 0)
           Into b_hd.sshn19
           From goodsstock_bak
          Where gstdate = lthisdate And
                gstsupid = b_hd.sshsupid And
                gstwmid = b_hd.sshwmid And
                (gstmarket = b_hd.sshmkt Or b_hd.sshmkt = '0');
      End If;*/
    Else
      b_hd.sshn1 := b_dettot.ssdn9;
      b_hd.sshn2 := b_dettot.ssdn1;
      b_hd.sshn3 := b_dettot.ssdn8;
      b_hd.sshn4 := b_dettot.ssdn4;
    
      b_hd.sshn7    := b_dettot.ssdn28; --销售收入(不含保底、超额)
      b_hd.sshn8    := b_dettot.ssdn29; --销售提成
      b_hd.sshogdje := b_dettot.ssdn10; --应提成金额
      b_hd.sshmgdje := b_dettot.ssdn23; --保底提成额
      b_hd.sshaqdje := b_dettot.ssdn26; --超额提成额+特卖超额
      /*实际提成=销售提成+保底提成+超额提成*/
      /*      if b_dettot.ssdvc6='7' then*/
      b_hd.sshtotdje := b_dettot.ssdn29 + b_hd.sshmgdje + b_hd.sshaqdje +
                        b_dettot.ssdn73;
      /*      else
        b_hd.sshtotdje := b_dettot.ssdn29 + b_hd.sshmgdje + b_hd.sshaqdje; --实际提成额合计
      end if;*/
      If b_isqs = '1' Then
        --清算应付金额不含销售收入
        b_hd.sshtotyfje := -b_hd.sshtotdje; --应付金额
      Else
        b_hd.sshtotyfje := b_dettot.ssdn9 - b_hd.sshtotdje; --应付金额
        If b_hd.sshdjlb In (billtypewm2, billtypewm3) Then
          --代销ssdn9为内部领用
          b_hd.sshn9      := b_dettot.ssdn36;
          b_hd.sshtotyfje := b_hd.sshtotyfje + b_hd.sshn9;
        End If;
      
      End If;
    
      b_hd.sshsetadj := b_dettot.ssdn38;
      b_hd.sshtotkk  := b_dettot.ssdn30;
      b_hd.Sshn23    := b_dettot.ssdn70;
    End If;
  
    b_Hd.Sshyfkje := Nvl(l_Prepayamt, 0);
    b_hd.sshn22   := Nvl(l_Prepayamt, 0); --未核销的预付款
    b_hd.sshsetje := b_hd.sshtotyfje - b_hd.sshsetadj;
  
    b_hd.sshsjfkje := b_hd.sshlastye + b_hd.sshsetje - b_hd.sshtotkk -
                      b_hd.sshyfkje - nvl(b_hd.sshn21, 0);
    If b_NullBill = 'Y' Or abs(b_hd.sshtotyfje) > 0.001 Or
       abs(b_hd.sshsetadj) > 0.001 Or abs(b_hd.sshtotkk) > 0.001 Then
      inserthead;
      /*cmdsend.sp_cmdsend_target('CONTHQ',
      currentmkt,
      '0',
      '''' || lcontno || '''',
      NULL);*/
    Else
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->18.供应商本期无发生不能生成' || ldoname || '单!');
    End If;
  
    --统计销售数量
    SaleQtyStatis(b_hd.sshbillno);
  
    --代销进行损溢处理
    --清算单不需要做进行损溢处理
    If i_wmid In (Stock.WM_zbdx, Stock.WM_kldx) and
       b_hd.sshdjlb <> billtypeqsd Then
      SupsetSunYi(b_hd.sshbillno);
    End If;
  
    /*--结算生成完成，记录应收应付
    settleaccpay.jsgenaccpay(b_hd.sshbillno);*/
    --Gensettlepaydet(b_hd.sshbillno);
    --不在生成时生成付款明细,mux,20101123
    supcamana.jsgen(b_hd.sshbillno);
  
    --更新未结算清单
    If i_isbatch = 'N' And b_hd.sshdjlb <> billtypeqsd Then
      UptUnsettleData(b_hd, 'N');
    End If;
  
    If i_iscommit = 'Y' Then
      if b_hd.sshwmid = wmid4 or b_hd.sshwmid = wmid5 then
        select sum(decode(ssdvc6, '0', ssdn61 - nvl(ssdn77, 0), 0) -
                   nvl(ssdn63, 0))
          into l_mxkpje
          from supsettledet
         where ssdbillno = b_hd.sshbillno;
        update supsettlehead
           set sshsetje = nvl(l_mxkpje, 0) - nvl(sshsetadj, 0)
         where sshbillno = b_hd.sshbillno;
        /*elsif b_hd.sshwmid = wmid2 or b_hd.sshwmid = wmid3 then
        select sum(nvl(ssdn63, 0))
          into l_mxkpje
          from supsettledet
         where ssdbillno = b_hd.sshbillno;
        update supsettlehead
           set sshn8     = nvl(l_mxkpje, 0),
               sshtotdje = nvl(l_mxkpje, 0) + nvl(sshmgdje, 0) +
                           nvl(sshaqdje, 0)
         where sshbillno = b_hd.sshbillno;
         Update Supsettlehead
           Set Sshsetje  = Nvl(l_Mxkpje, 0) - Nvl(Sshsetadj, 0)
         Where Sshbillno = b_Hd.Sshbillno;*/
      end if;
      Commit;
    End If;
  
    If v_enablerule = 'Y' Then
      fterp_searchrule.enablerule;
    End If;
  
    o_billno := b_hd.sshbillno;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      If v_enablerule = 'Y' Then
        fterp_searchrule.enablerule;
      End If;
      Rollback;
      Raise;
  End submit;

  Procedure approve(p_billno In Char,
                    p_person In Char,
                    p_billid In Char,
                    p_djlb   In Char) Is
    vsupisscm supplierbase.sbvc10%Type; --是否scm发布订单 xu
    vphoneno  supplierbase.sblxfs%Type; --手机号码
    st        scm_settle%Rowtype;
    l_jsmkt   Varchar2(20);
    l_billno  Varchar2(20);
  Begin
    Begin
      Select *
        Into b_hd
        From supsettlehead
       Where sshbillno = p_billno
         For Update;
    
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode, p_billno || '->CHK01 单据不存在!');
      
    End;
  
    If b_hd.sshdjlb <> p_djlb Or
       b_hd.sshdjlb Not In
       (billtypewm1, billtypewm2, billtypewm3, billtypeoth, billtypeqsd) Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK02 单据类别不一致!');
    End If;
  
    /*IF currentmkt <> b_hd.sshmkt OR currentmkttype <> stock.mf_mkt THEN
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK03 结算单只能在门店审核!');
    END IF;*/
  
    --改成检查是否结算位置的合同,mux
    Begin
      Select cmjsmkt
        Into l_jsmkt
        From contmain
       Where cmcontno = b_hd.sshcontno;
    
    Exception
      When Others Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                p_billno || '->CHK03 检查合同信息失败!');
      
    End;
  
    If l_jsmkt <> currentmkt Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK03.1 结算单只能在合同对应结算位置[' ||
                              l_jsmkt || ']审核!');
    End If;
  
    If b_hd.sshflag Not In (flagediting, flagautoed, flagSCMAck) Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK105 单据已经审核或单据状态不一致!');
    End If;
    Begin
      Select sscbillno
        Into l_billno
        From supsetcharge
       Where nvl(sscjsno, '0') = p_billno
         And person1 = '0'
         And sscflag <> 'G';
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK106 现金类费用' || l_billno ||
                              '未缴费!');
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Null;
    End;
    --对于进入SCM系统的供应商
    --暂时只修改结算单标志为 SCM供应商待确认状态（B），并不做其它处理；
    --SCM供应商网上确认结算单后 sp_scmorder过程会将此单审核
    Select nvl(sbvc10, 'N'), nvl(sblxfs, '86')
      Into vsupisscm, vphoneno
      From supplierbase
     Where sbid = b_hd.sshsupid;
  
    If vsupisscm = 'Y' Then
      Begin
        Select * Into st From scm_settle Where stbillno = p_billno;
      
      Exception
        When no_data_found Then
          Update supsettlehead
             Set sshflag = 'B',
                 --SCM供应商待确认状态
                 auditor   = p_person,
                 auditdate = sysdate
           Where sshbillno = p_billno;
        
          If Sql%Rowcount < 0 Or Sql%Rowcount Is Null Then
            raise_application_error(errcode,
                                    p_billno || '->48 修改单据标志失败！');
          End If;
        
          --
          If vphoneno <> '86' Then
            vphoneno := '86' || Replace(vphoneno, ',', ',86');
          End If;
        
          -- fGetsmid
          Insert Into scm_send_msg
            (sm_id, sm_phone_num, sm_content, sm_create_time)
            Select 'ERP' || decode(b_hd.sshdjlb,
                                   '1',
                                   '5628',
                                   '2',
                                   '5629',
                                   '3',
                                   '5631',
                                   '4',
                                   '5620') ||
                   to_char(seq_scm_sms.NEXTVAL, '000000000000000'),
                   vphoneno,
                   '尊敬的客户, 订单[' || p_billno || ']已发出，请查收。',
                   Sysdate
              From dual;
        
          Return; --scm供应商
      
      End;
    
    End If;
  
    -- <<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<
  
    If b_hd.sshdjlb = billtypeqsd Then
      Update contmain
         Set cmlastqsdate = b_hd.sshthisdate
       Where cmcontno = b_hd.sshcontno;
      --同步更新总部合同
      SettleSupExt.Sp_UpdateSettleDate('Y',
                                       b_hd.sshcontno,
                                       b_hd.sshthisdate);
    Else
      Update contmain
         Set cmlastsetdate = b_hd.sshthisdate
       Where cmcontno = b_hd.sshcontno;
      --同步更新总部合同
      SettleSupExt.Sp_UpdateSettleDate('N',
                                       b_hd.sshcontno,
                                       b_hd.sshthisdate);
    End If;
  
    If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Or Sql%Rowcount Is Null Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->20.结算单的合同[' || b_hd.sshcontno || ']不存在!');
    End If;
  
    -- 修改settlesupbatch结算标志
    If b_hd.sshwmid = stock.wm_jx Then
      Update settlesupbatch
         Set ssbstatus = 'Y', ssbjsdate = b_hd.sshthisdate
       Where ssbjsbillno = p_billno;
    
    End If;
  
    If b_hd.sshdjlb <> billtypeqsd Then
      Update salecostday_supset
         Set scdsjsflag = 'Y'
       Where scdsjsbillno = p_billno;
    
      --修改预付款结算标志
      Update supsetyfk Set ssyjsbz = 'Y' Where ssyjsdh = p_billno;
    
      -- 修改一次性结算合同费用的标志
      Update contsupcharge
         Set cscflag = 'Y'
       Where nvl(cscjsbillno, '0') = p_billno
         And cscismcjs = setmodeyc;
      --同步更新总部合同
      SettleSupExt.Sp_UpdateChargeFlag(p_BillNo, 'Y');
    
      --修改费用记录
      Update supsetcharge
         Set sscflag   = flagapproved,
             auditor   = decode(ssctype, '0', p_person, auditor),
             auditdate = decode(ssctype, '0', Sysdate, auditdate)
      --auditor = p_person,
      --auditdate = trunc(SYSDATE)
       Where nvl(sscjsno, '0') = p_billno;
    
      --预付款结算审核
      Update supprepay
         Set sppstatus = BSupPrepay.FlagFinished
       Where sppsettleno = p_billno
         And spptype = BSupPrepay.Mode_Oncetime;
    
      If b_hd.sshwmid <> stock.wm_jx Then
        Delete From SUPSETTLEDETBD Where SSbJsBillNo = b_hd.sshbillno;
        --更新合同保底中的已保底标志，将已生成保底数据的保底期更新为已处理保底
        Insert Into SUPSETTLEDETBD
          Select b_hd.sshbillno,
                 cbcontno,
                 cbseqno,
                 cbeffdate,
                 cblapdate,
                 cbisrunbd,
                 cbisrunqs,
                 'BD'
            From contbd
           Where cbcontno = b_hd.sshcontno
             And cbisbd = 'Q';
        Update contbd
           Set cbisbd = 'Y'
         Where cbcontno = b_hd.sshcontno
           And cbisbd = 'Q';
        --同步更新到总部
        SettleSupExt.Sp_SetY_Bd(b_hd.sshcontno);
        --更新合同保底中的已清算标志，将已生成清算数据的保底期更新为已处理清算
        Insert Into SUPSETTLEDETBD
          Select b_hd.sshbillno,
                 cbcontno,
                 cbseqno,
                 cbeffdate,
                 cblapdate,
                 cbisrunbd,
                 cbisrunqs,
                 'QS'
            From contbd
           Where cbcontno = b_hd.sshcontno
             And cbisqs = 'Q';
        Update contbd
           Set cbisqs = 'Y'
         Where cbcontno = b_hd.sshcontno
           And cbisqs = 'Q';
        --同步更新到总部
        SettleSupExt.Sp_SetY_Qs(b_hd.sshcontno);
        Update supprepay
           Set sppstatus = BSupPrepay.FlagSettled
         Where sppsettleno = p_billno
           And spptype = '1';
      End If;
    
      --更新未结数据清单
      Update supsettleexplist
         Set sselsetdate = trunc(Sysdate),
             sselsetflag = Decode(Nvl(sselsetxssr, 0) - Nvl(sselxssr, 0),
                                  0,
                                  Decode(Nvl(sselsetcharge, 0) -
                                         Nvl(sselcharge, 0),
                                         0,
                                         'Y',
                                         'N'),
                                  'N')
       Where sselsettleno = p_billno;
    End If;
  
    Update supsettlehead
       Set sshflag = flagapproved, auditor = p_person, auditdate = Sysdate
     Where sshbillno = p_billno;
  
    If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Or Sql%Rowcount Is Null Then
      raise_application_error(errcode, '->21.修改供应商结算单标志不成功!');
    End If;
    bsupprepay.Settle_Hx(p_billno);
    Gensettlepaydet(p_billno);
    --[[[[审核时检查并调整手工核销的预付款状态 2015.12.09 =  =P~
    For V_Supprepay_Usage In (Select Distinct Sppubillno
                                From Supprepay_Usage
                               Where Sppusetno = P_Billno) Loop
      Begin
        Update Supprepay
           Set Sppstatus = 'S'
         Where Sppbillno = V_Supprepay_Usage.Sppubillno
           And Sppye = 0
           And Sppstatus = 'Y'
           And Spptype = '2';
      Exception
        When No_Data_Found Then
          Null;
        When Others Then
          Raise;
      End;
    End Loop;
    --]]]]------------------------------------------------------
    /*--审核应付应收帐1
    settleaccpay.approve(p_billno,'4');
    --记录已付
    settleaccpay.genaccpayed(p_billno);
    --审核应付应收帐2
    settleaccpay.approve(p_billno,'1');*/
  
    --改为实时更新
    /*If CurrentMktType = Stock.MF_MKT Then
       Cmdsend.sp_cmdsend_target('CONTHQ',Currentmkt, '0', '''' || b_hd.sshcontno || '''', NULL);
    End If;*/
  
    Commit;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Raise;
    
  End approve;

  Procedure payment(p_billno In Char,
                    p_person In Char,
                    p_billid In Char,
                    p_djlb   In Char) Is
  Begin
    Begin
      Select *
        Into b_hd
        From supsettlehead
       Where sshbillno = p_billno
         For Update;
    
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode, p_billno || '->CHK01 单据不存在!');
      
    End;
  
    If b_hd.sshdjlb <> p_djlb Or
       b_hd.sshdjlb Not In
       (billtypewm1, billtypewm2, billtypewm3, billtypeoth, billtypeqsd) Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK02 单据类别不一致!');
    End If;
  
    If currentmkt <> b_hd.sshmkt Or currentmkttype <> stock.mf_mkt Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK03 结算单只能在门店审核!');
    End If;
  
    If b_hd.sshflag <> flagapproved Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK105 单据已经付款或未审核!');
    End If;
  
    Update supsettlehead
       Set sshflag = flagpayed,
           -- 新建字段保存付款审核人及付款审核日期 07.04.20
           --auditor   = p_person,
           --auditdate = trunc(SYSDATE)
           payer   = p_person,
           paydate = trunc(Sysdate)
     Where sshbillno = p_billno;
  
    If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Or Sql%Rowcount Is Null Then
      raise_application_error(errcode, '->21.修改供应商结算单标志不成功!');
    End If;
  
    Commit;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Raise;
    
  End payment;

  Procedure sendsetpl(p_setpl    In Char,
                      p_thisdate In Varchar2,
                      p_person   In Char,
                      p_billid   In Char,
                      p_djlb     In Char) Is
    lexist Number;
  
  Begin
    Select Count(*)
      Into lexist
      From supsettlehead
     Where sshdjlb = p_billid
       And sshmkt = p_setpl
       And sshthisdate = to_date(p_thisdate, 'YYYY-MM-DD')
       And sshflag = flagautoed;
  
    If lexist < 1 Then
      raise_application_error(errcode, '->CHK01 单据不存在!');
    End If;
  
    If currentmkt = '0' Then
      cmdsend.sp_cmdsend_target(cmdsendtomkt,
                                currentmkt,
                                p_setpl,
                                '''' || p_setpl || ''',''' || p_thisdate || '''',
                                Null);
    Else
      raise_application_error(errcode, '->CHK03 本位置不能发送该结算单!');
    
    End If;
  
    --修改费用记录
    Update supsetcharge
       Set sscflag = flagsended, auditor = p_person, auditdate = sysdate
     Where Exists (Select sshbillno
              From supsettlehead
             Where sshbillno = sscjsno
               And sshdjlb = p_billid
               And sshmkt = p_setpl
               And sshthisdate = to_date(p_thisdate, 'YYYY-MM-DD')
               And sshflag = flagautoed);
  
    Update supsettlehead
       Set sshflag = flagsended, auditor = p_person, auditdate = sysdate
     Where sshdjlb = p_billid
       And sshmkt = p_setpl
       And sshthisdate = to_date(p_thisdate, 'YYYY-MM-DD')
       And sshflag = flagautoed;
  
    If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Or Sql%Rowcount Is Null Then
      raise_application_error(errcode, '->22.修改供应商结算单标志不成功!');
    End If;
  
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Raise;
    
  End;

  Procedure cancel(p_billno In Char,
                   p_person In Char,
                   p_billid In Char,
                   p_djlb   In Char) Is
    --lflag CHAR(1);
    Cursor cur_charge Is
      Select *
        From supsetcharge
       Where ssctype = '1'
         And sscjsno = p_billno;
  
    row_charge cur_charge%Rowtype;
  Begin
    Begin
      Select *
        Into b_hd
        From supsettlehead
       Where sshbillno = p_billno
         For Update;
    
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode, p_billno || '->CHK01 单据不存在!');
      
    End;
  
    If b_hd.sshdjlb <> p_djlb Or
       b_hd.sshdjlb Not In
       (billtypewm1, billtypewm2, billtypewm3, billtypeoth) Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK02 单据类别不一致!');
    End If;
  
    If b_hd.sshflag <> flagsended Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK05 单据已经审核或单据状态不一致!');
    End If;
  
    --修改费用记录
    Update supsetcharge
       Set sscflag = flagcanceled, auditor = p_person, auditdate = sysdate
     Where sscjsno = p_billno;
  
    Open cur_charge;
    Loop
      Fetch cur_charge
        Into row_charge;
      Exit When cur_charge%Notfound Or cur_charge%Notfound Is Null;
      row_charge.sscrowno := row_charge.sscrowno + 1;
      row_charge.sscmemo  := substr(nvl(row_charge.sscmemo, '') || '取消' ||
                                    p_billno || '保存临时费用',
                                    1,
                                    39);
      row_charge.sscjsno  := Null;
      row_charge.sscflag  := 'S';
      Insert Into supsetcharge
        (sscbillno,
         sscrowno,
         sscdjbh,
         ssctype,
         sscflag,
         sscsupid,
         sscwmid,
         sscmarket,
         sscmfid,
         sscdate,
         sscfsdate,
         sscfsmon,
         sscid,
         sscname,
         sscmoney,
         sscjsno,
         ssccontno,
         inputor,
         inputdate,
         auditor,
         auditdate,
         person1,
         person2,
         person3,
         person4,
         person5,
         sscmemo,
         sscsetpl,
         sscgdmoney,
         Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
         Sscnum3) --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
      Values
        (row_charge.sscbillno,
         row_charge.sscrowno,
         row_charge.sscdjbh,
         row_charge.ssctype,
         row_charge.sscflag,
         row_charge.sscsupid,
         row_charge.sscwmid,
         row_charge.sscmarket,
         row_charge.sscmfid,
         row_charge.sscdate,
         row_charge.sscfsdate,
         row_charge.sscfsmon,
         row_charge.sscid,
         row_charge.sscname,
         row_charge.sscmoney,
         row_charge.sscjsno,
         row_charge.ssccontno,
         row_charge.inputor,
         row_charge.inputdate,
         row_charge.auditor,
         row_charge.auditdate,
         row_charge.person1,
         row_charge.person2,
         row_charge.person3,
         row_charge.person4,
         row_charge.person5,
         row_charge.sscmemo,
         row_charge.sscsetpl,
         row_charge.sscgdmoney,
         row_charge.Sscnum2, --税率 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
         row_charge.Sscnum3); --不含税金额 =  =P~ 2017.01.24
    
    End Loop;
  
    Update supsettlehead
       Set sshflag = flagcanceled, auditor = p_person, auditdate = sysdate
     Where sshbillno = p_billno;
  
    If Sql%Rowcount = 0 Or Sql%Rowcount Is Null Then
      raise_application_error(errcode, '->23.修改供应商结算单标志不成功!');
    End If;
  
    /*IF currentmkt <> b_hd.sshmkt THEN
      IF currentmkt = '0' THEN
        cmdsend.sp_cmdsend_target(cmdcancelmkt,
                                  currentmkt,
                                  b_hd.sshmkt,
                                  --              ''''||p_billno||'''',
                                  '''' || p_billno || ''',''' || p_person ||
                                  ''',''' || p_billid || ''',''' || p_djlb || '''',
                                  --               p_billno IN CHAR,p_person IN CHAR,p_billid IN CHAR,p_djlb IN CHAR
                                  NULL);
      END IF;
      --      ELSE
      --         IF CurrentMkt <> '0' THEN
      --            cmdsend.SP_CMDSEND_TARGET
      --                  (CmdCancelHq,CurrentMkt,'0',
      --                   ''''||p_billno||''','''||p_person||''','''||p_billid||''','''||p_djlb||'''',
      --                   NULL);
      --         END IF;
    END IF;*/
  
    Commit;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Raise;
    
  End cancel;

  --反审 内部使用
  Procedure noapprove(p_billno In Char,
                      p_person In Char,
                      p_billid In Char,
                      p_djlb   In Char) Is
    l_contdate Date;
    l_ye       Number;
    l_retmoney Number;
    l_money    Number;
    l_cnt      number;
    l_row      number;
  Begin
    Begin
      Select *
        Into b_hd
        From supsettlehead
       Where sshbillno = p_billno
         For Update;
    
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode, p_billno || '->CHK01 单据不存在!');
      
    End;
  
    If b_hd.sshdjlb <> p_djlb Or
       b_hd.sshdjlb Not In
       (billtypewm1, billtypewm2, billtypewm3, billtypeoth, billtypeqsd) Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK02 单据类别不一致!');
    End If;
  
    If currentmkt <> b_hd.sshmkt /*OR currentmkttype <> stock.mf_mkt */
     Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK03 结算单只能在门店反审!');
    End If;
  
    If b_hd.sshflag <> flagapproved Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->CHK105 单据不是审核状态!');
    End If;
  
    If b_hd.sshpayflag = 'Y' Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '-->chk106 单据已付款！');
    End If;
    --2014.3.31
    Select Count(1)
      Into l_ye
      From Settlepaydet
     Where SPDBILLNO = p_BillNo
       And SpdSf <> 0;
    If l_ye > 0 Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '-->chk106 单据已付款（2）！');
    else
      --判断是否生成过供应商付款单
      delete from settlepaydet where spdbillno = p_billno;
      delete from paybatchtemp where pbjsno = p_billno;
    End If;
  
    /*if b_hd.sshisjz = 'Y' then
       raise_application_error(errcode,
                               p_billno ||
                               '-->chk107 单据已结帐！');
    end if;*/
  
    Select cmlastsetdate
      Into l_contdate
      From contmain
     Where cmcontno = b_hd.sshcontno;
  
    If b_hd.sshthisdate <> l_contdate Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno ||
                              '-->chk108 该单据不是该合同的最后一份结算单，不能反审！');
    End If;
  
    Update contmain
       Set cmlastsetdate = b_hd.sshlastdate
     Where cmcontno = b_hd.sshcontno;
    --同步更新总部合同
    SettleSupExt.Sp_UpdateSettleDate('N', b_hd.sshcontno, b_hd.sshlastdate);
  
    --修改合同保底状态
    select count(*)
      into l_cnt
      from contbd
     where cbcontno = b_hd.sshcontno
       And cbisbd = 'Y'
       And cbflag = 'Y'
       And cbmkt = b_hd.sshmkt
       And cbmfid = b_hd.sshmfid
       And cbeffdate <= b_hd.sshthisdate;
    for vr_bd in (select *
                    from contbd
                   where cbcontno = b_hd.sshcontno
                     And cbisbd = 'Y'
                     And cbflag = 'Y'
                     And cbmkt = b_hd.sshmkt
                     And cbmfid = b_hd.sshmfid
                     And cbeffdate <= b_hd.sshthisdate) loop
      --同步更新到总部
      DBUSRSYS.sp_debug('Sp_SetN_Bd-start',vr_bd.cbcontno||'-'||vr_bd.cbseqno);
      SettleSupExt.Sp_SetN_Bd(vr_bd.cbcontno, vr_bd.cbseqno);
      SettleSupExt.Sp_SetN_Qs(vr_bd.cbcontno, vr_bd.cbseqno);
    end loop;
  
    Begin
      Update salecostday_supset
         Set scdsjsflag = 'N'
       Where scdsjsbillno = p_billno;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Null;
      
    End;
  
    --修改预付款结算标志
    Begin
      Update supsetyfk Set ssyjsbz = 'N' Where ssyjsdh = p_billno;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Null;
    End;
  
    --供应商预付款
    --含一次性核销和手工核销
    Begin
      Update supprepay
         Set sppstatus = BSupPrepay.FlagSettled
       Where Nvl(sppsettleno, '0') = p_billno
      /*AND spptype = BSupPrepay.Mode_Oncetime*/
      ;
    
      --取消核销, 2014.3.31
      For Vr In (Select * From SupPrePay_Usage Where SppuSetNo = p_billno) Loop
        Update SupPrePay
           Set Sppye = Sppye + Vr.Sppuhxmoney
         Where SppBillNo = Vr.Sppubillno Return Sppye Into l_ye;
        Update SupPrePay_Usage
           Set sppuflag = 'N', sppuhxye = Null, sppuvchr1 = Null
         Where sppubillno = vr.sppubillno
           And sppusetno = vr.sppusetno;
        --[[[[反审时检查并调整手工核销的预付款状态 2015.12.09 =  =P~
        Begin
          Update Supprepay
             Set Sppstatus = 'Y'
           Where Sppbillno = Vr.Sppubillno
             And Sppye > 0
             And Sppstatus = 'S'
             And Spptype = '2';
        Exception
          When Others Then
            Null;
        End;
        --]]]]------------------------------------------------------
      End Loop;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Null;
      
    End;
  
    -- 修改一次性结算合同费用的标志
    Begin
      Update contsupcharge
         Set cscflag = 'N'
       Where nvl(cscjsbillno, '0') = p_billno
         And cscismcjs = 0;
      --同步更新总部合同
      SettleSupExt.Sp_UpdateChargeFlag(p_BillNo, 'N');
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Null;
      
    End;
  
    --修改费用记录
    Begin
      /*Update supsetcharge
        Set sscflag   = 'M',
            auditor   = decode(ssctype, '0', Null, auditor),
            auditdate = decode(ssctype, '0', Null, auditdate)
      Where nvl(sscjsno, '0') = p_billno;
      */
    
      --2014.4.3修改
      For Vr In (Select *
                   From supsetcharge
                  Where nvl(sscjsno, '0') = p_billno) Loop
        Update supsetcharge
           Set sscflag   = 'M',
               auditor   = decode(ssctype, '0', Null, auditor),
               auditdate = decode(ssctype, '0', Null, auditdate)
         Where SSCBILLNO = Vr.Sscbillno
           And SSCROWNO = Vr.Sscrowno;
      
        If Vr.Sscflag = 'G' And Vr.sscyretbillno Is Not Null Then
          Update supsetcharge
             Set sscretmoney  = nvl(sscretmoney, 0) - Vr.sscmoney,
                 sscretstatus = 'N'
           Where sscbillno = Vr.sscyretbillno
          Returning sscretmoney, sscmoney Into l_retmoney, l_money;
        
          If l_money = l_retmoney Then
            Update supsetcharge
               Set sscretstatus = 'Y'
             Where sscbillno = Vr.sscyretbillno;
          Else
            Update supsetcharge
               Set sscretstatus = 'N'
             Where sscbillno = Vr.sscyretbillno;
          End If;
        End If;
      End Loop;
      recalcsum(p_billno);
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Null;
      
    End;
  
    --更新未结数据清单
    Update supsettleexplist
       Set sselsetdate = Null, sselsetflag = 'N'
     Where sselsettleno = p_billno;
  
    --
    Update supsettlehead
       Set sshflag = 'M', auditor = Null, auditdate = Null
     Where sshbillno = p_billno;
  
    Update settlesupbatch
       Set ssbstatus = 'M' /*,
                                                                 ssbjsbillno = Null,
                                                                 ssbjsdjbh   = Null*/
     Where ssbjsbillno = p_billno;
  
    --付款信息
    Delete From Settlepaydet Where Spdbillno = p_Billno;
  
    --重置保底和清算标志
    For Vr in (Select * From SupSettleDetBd Where SsbJsBillNo = p_BillNo) Loop
      If Vr.Ssbtype = 'BD' Then
        Update ContBd
           Set CbIsBd = 'Q'
         Where CBCONTNO = Vr.Ssbcontno
           And CBSEQNO = Vr.Ssbseqno;
        DBUSRSYS.sp_debug('Sp_SetQ_Bd-start',Vr.Ssbcontno||'-'||Vr.Ssbseqno);   
        SettleSupExt.Sp_SetQ_Bd(Vr.Ssbcontno, Vr.Ssbseqno);
      Else
        Update ContBd
           Set CbIsQs = 'Q'
         Where CBCONTNO = Vr.Ssbcontno
           And CBSEQNO = Vr.Ssbseqno;
        SettleSupExt.Sp_SetQ_Qs(Vr.Ssbcontno, Vr.Ssbseqno);
      End If;
    End Loop;
  
    Commit;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Raise;
    
  End noapprove;

  Procedure auditsupcharge(p_billno   In Char,
                           p_num      In Number,
                           p_person   In Char,
                           p_iscommit In Char Default 'Y') Is
    row_ssc supsetcharge%Rowtype;
    r_cont  contmain%Rowtype;
    --r_exp   set_mall_exp%ROWTYPE;
  
  Begin
    Begin
      Select *
        Into row_ssc
        From supsetcharge
       Where sscbillno = p_billno
         And sscrowno = p_num
         For Update;
    
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '->24.费用单【' || p_billno || '】不存在!');
      When Others Then
        raise_application_error(errcode, '审核费用单失败!');
      
    End;
  
    If row_ssc.sscflag <> 'N' Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->25.费用单【' || p_billno || '】之前已被审核，不能重复审核!');
    End If;
  
    --供应商、合同、柜组在费用发生日期上是否有效合同
    Begin
      Select Distinct contmain.*
        Into r_cont
        From contmain, contmanaframe
       Where cmcontno = cmfcontno
         And cmstatus In ('Y', 'Q')
         And cmjsmkt = CurrentMkt
         And cmeffdate <= trunc(row_ssc.sscfsdate)
         And cmlapdate >= trunc(row_ssc.sscfsdate)
         And cmsupid = row_ssc.sscsupid
         And cmcontno = row_ssc.ssccontno
         And cmfmfid = row_ssc.sscmfid;
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                p_billno || '->26 合同【' || row_ssc.ssccontno ||
                                '】柜组【' || row_ssc.sscmfid || '】在费用发生日期【' ||
                                to_char(row_ssc.sscfsdate, 'YYYY-MM-DD') ||
                                '】上无有效合同！');
    End;
  
    /*SELECT * INTO r_cont FROM contmain WHERE cmcontno = row_ssc.ssccontno;
