    IF r_cont.cmstatus not IN ('Y', 'Q') AND row_ssc.person1='Y' THEN
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->26.合同不是有效的合同!');
    
    END IF;*/
    --liulei 090721 购物中心
    /*IF r_cont.cmsptype IN ('S', 'G', 'Z') THEN
      exes.p_mall_expinit(r_exp);
      r_exp.seqno    := p_billno; --VARCHAR2(20) N     结算主单号
      r_exp.billno   := p_billno; --VARCHAR2(20)  N     结算子单号
      r_exp.billtype := dbusrmall.mallset.sub_lsfy; -- VARCHAR2(3) N     单据类型
      r_exp.rowno    := '1'; --NUMBER  N     行号
      r_exp.mfid     := r_cont.cmmfid; --VARCHAR2(15) N     柜组
      r_exp.supid    := r_cont.cmsupid; --VARCHAR2(8)  N     供应商
      r_exp.wmid     := r_cont.cmwmid; --CHAR(1)  N     经营方式
      r_exp.contno   := r_cont.cmcontno; --VARCHAR2(20) N     合同编码
      r_exp.contgrp  := dbusrmall.mallset_base.f_get_contgrp(r_cont.cmcontno); --VARCHAR2(10)  N     合同组
      r_exp.begrq    := add_months(last_day(row_ssc.sscfsdate), -1) + 1; --DATE Y     结算期间1
      r_exp.endrq    := last_day(row_ssc.sscfsdate); --DATE  Y     结算期间2
      r_exp.xmcode   := row_ssc.sscid; --VARCHAR2(10) N     项目编码
      r_exp.xmname   := row_ssc.sscname; --VARCHAR2(40) Y     项目名称
      r_exp.fsrq     := row_ssc.sscfsdate; --DATE N     发生日期
      r_exp.fsje     := row_ssc.sscmoney; --NUMBER  N 0   发生金额
      r_exp.shr      := p_person; --VARCHAR2(8)  Y     审核员
      r_exp.shrq     := fgeterpdate; --DATE Y     审核日期
      r_exp.flag     := 'Y'; --CHAR(1)  N     单据状态(N新单Y已审核C已取消G已执行)
      r_exp.memo     := '临时费用单号[' || p_billno || ']'; --VARCHAR2(60)  Y     备注
      exes.p_mall_expins(r_exp);
    END IF;*/
  
    --liulei
    Update supsetcharge
       Set sscflag = 'S', auditor = p_person, auditdate = Sysdate --fgeterpdate
     Where sscbillno = p_billno
       And sscrowno = p_num;
  
    --这里不能 commit，否则批量录入费用单可能会出错
    --Commit;
  Exception
    When Others Then
     -- Rollback;
      Raise;
    
  End auditsupcharge;

  --结算单'现金付款'  费用单'收款'
  Procedure gathersupcharge(p_billno In Char,
                            p_num    In Number,
                            p_person In Char) Is
    row_ssc            supsetcharge%Rowtype;
    l_money            Number;
    l_retmoney         Number;
    row_p              nc_temp_cashpay%Rowtype;
    Lseq               Number;   
    lsupsub            varchar2(20);
    lmfsub             varchar2(20);
    lzt                varchar2(20);  
    lsupaccntno        varchar2(50);
    lsupbank           varchar2(50);
    mktbank            varchar2(50);
    mktaccnt           varchar2(50);
  Begin
    Begin
      Select *
        Into row_ssc
        From supsetcharge
       Where sscbillno = p_billno
         And sscrowno = p_num
         For Update;
    
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '费用单【' || p_billno || '(' || to_char(p_num) ||
                                ')】不存在!');
      When Others Then
        raise_application_error(errcode, '费用单收款失败!');
      
    End;
  
    If row_ssc.sscflag = 'G' Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '费用单【' || p_billno || '(' || to_char(p_num) ||
                              ')】已收款，不能重复收款!');
    End If;
  
    If row_ssc.sscflag <> 'S' And row_ssc.sscflag <> 'Y' Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '费用单【' || p_billno || '(' || to_char(p_num) ||
                              ')】不能收款，只有审核过的费用或结算单才能收款!');
    End If;
  
    If row_ssc.person1 = 'Y' Then
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '费用单【' || p_billno || '(' || to_char(p_num) ||
                              ')】是帐扣费用，不能现金收款!');
    End If;
  
    Update supsetcharge
       Set sscflag = 'G', auditor = p_person, auditdate = fgeterpdate
     Where sscbillno = p_billno
       And sscrowno = p_num;
  
    --结算审核过的费用收费后重算实付金额
    If row_ssc.sscflag = 'Y' And row_ssc.sscjsno Is Not Null Then
      recalcsum(row_ssc.sscjsno, row_ssc.sscflag);
      --生成已收
      --settleaccpayday.approve(row_ssc.sscjsno,p_billno,'2');
    Else
      --直接付款，生成应收和已收
      --settleaccpayday.sp_payforfzkfy(p_billno);
      --settleaccpayday.genaccpayed('1',p_billno);
      --settleaccpayday.approve('1',p_billno,'2');
      Null;
    
    End If;
  
    If row_ssc.sscrettype = '2' Then
      Update supsetcharge
         Set sscretmoney   = nvl(sscretmoney, 0) - row_ssc.sscmoney,
             sscrecretdate = trunc(Sysdate),
             sscretstatus  = row_ssc.sscretstatus
       Where sscbillno = row_ssc.sscyretbillno
      Returning sscretmoney, sscmoney Into l_retmoney, l_money;
    
      If l_retmoney > l_money Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '费用单【' || p_billno || '(' || to_char(p_num) ||
                                ')】是本次返还金额不能大于剩余返还金额!');
      End If;
    
      If l_money = l_retmoney Then
        Update supsetcharge
           Set sscretstatus = 'Y'
         Where sscbillno = row_ssc.sscyretbillno;
      
      End If;
    
    End If;
    --Gensettlepaydet(p_billno);
    -- 直接收款么有结算单号,2013.11.5
    If row_ssc.sscjsno Is Not Null Then
      Gensettlepaydet(row_ssc.sscjsno);
    End If;
    -- Supcamana.Charge(p_Billno,'PAY',p_Num);
    
    select seq_nc_temp_cashpay.nextval into lseq from dual;
    row_p.id                   := lseq;
    begin
      select ztdm into lzt from cwzzzt where ztdymarket = row_ssc.sscmarket and rownum = 1;
    exception when others then
      Raise_Application_Error(Errcode, '->08.门店找不到对应帐套信息!');
    end;  
    row_p.corp                 := lzt;
    row_p.tradetype            := '0';
    row_p.settlecode           := '01';
    row_p.billdate             := to_char(sysdate, 'yyyy-mm-dd');
    row_p.headid               := lseq;
    row_p.bodyid               := 1;
    select nvl(sbsubject,sbid),sbbank,sbaccntno into lsupsub,lsupbank,lsupaccntno from supplierbase where sbid = row_ssc.sscsupid;
    row_p.cvcode               := lsupsub;
    /*select count(distinct pbmfid) into lcount from paybatch where pbpaybillno = p_billno;
    if lcount > 1 then
      Raise_Application_Error(Errcode, '->08.付款单不允许包含多个柜组数据!');
    end if;*/
    select pivalue into mktbank from privateinfo where pimkt = row_ssc.sscmarket and piid = '03';
    select pivalue into mktaccnt from privateinfo where pimkt = row_ssc.sscmarket and piid = '04';    
    select nvl(mfsubject,mfcode) into lmfsub from manaframe where mfcode = row_ssc.sscmfid;
    row_p.deptcode             := lmfsub;
    row_p.paybkaccount         := mktaccnt;
    row_p.paybkname            := mktbank;
    row_p.recebkaccount        := lsupaccntno;
    row_p.recebkname           := lsupbank;
    row_p.crc                  := '人民币';
    row_p.rate                 := 1;
    row_p.digest               := '收款';
    row_p.payoriginalmny       := row_ssc.Sscmoney;
    row_p.paylocalmny          := row_ssc.Sscmoney;
    row_p.billflag             := '0';
    row_p.sourcebillcode       := row_ssc.Sscbillno;
    row_p.iflag                := 'N';
    row_p.note                 := '';
    row_p.ts                   := to_char(sysdate, 'yyyy-mm-dd hh24:mi:ss');
    row_p.billcode             := null;
    row_p.prepaydate           := null;
    row_p.cashflowcode         := null;
    if lsupaccntno is null or lsupaccntno = '' then
      Raise_Application_Error(Errcode, '->09.供应商银行账号为空，请维护后进行收款!');
    end if;         
    insert into nc_temp_cashpay values row_p;        
    Commit;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      Rollback;
      Raise;
    
  End gathersupcharge;
  
  Procedure ins_midcashpay(P_Billno In Varchar2,p_num in number) Is
    row_ssc            supsetcharge%Rowtype;
    Lcount             Number;
    row_p              nc_temp_cashpay%Rowtype;
    Lseq               Number;   
    lsupsub            varchar2(20);
    lmfsub             varchar2(20);
    lzt                varchar2(20);  
    lsupaccntno        varchar2(50);
    lsupbank           varchar2(50);
    mktbank            varchar2(50);
    mktaccnt           varchar2(50);
  Begin
    Begin
      Select *
        Into row_ssc
        From supsetcharge
       Where sscbillno = p_billno
         And sscrowno = p_num;
    Exception
      When no_data_found Then
        raise_application_error(errcode,
                                '费用单【' || p_billno || '(' || to_char(p_num) ||
                                ')】不存在!');
     
    End;

    If row_ssc.sscflag <> 'G' Then
      Raise_Application_Error(Errcode,
                              P_Billno || '->04.单据不是已收款状态!');
    End If;
    
    select seq_nc_temp_cashpay.nextval into lseq from dual;
    row_p.id                   := lseq;
    begin
      select ztdm into lzt from cwzzzt where ztdymarket = row_ssc.sscmarket and rownum = 1;
    exception when others then
      Raise_Application_Error(Errcode, '->08.门店找不到对应帐套信息!');
    end;  
    row_p.corp                 := lzt;
    row_p.tradetype            := '0';
    row_p.settlecode           := '01';
    row_p.billdate             := to_char(sysdate, 'yyyy-mm-dd');
    row_p.headid               := lseq;
    row_p.bodyid               := 1;
    select nvl(sbsubject,sbid),sbbank,sbaccntno into lsupsub,lsupbank,lsupaccntno from supplierbase where sbid = row_ssc.sscsupid;
    row_p.cvcode               := lsupsub;
    /*select count(distinct pbmfid) into lcount from paybatch where pbpaybillno = p_billno;
    if lcount > 1 then
      Raise_Application_Error(Errcode, '->08.付款单不允许包含多个柜组数据!');
    end if;*/
    select pivalue into mktbank from privateinfo where pimkt = row_ssc.sscmarket and piid = '03';
    select pivalue into mktaccnt from privateinfo where pimkt = row_ssc.sscmarket and piid = '04';    
    select nvl(mfsubject,mfcode) into lmfsub from manaframe where mfcode = row_ssc.sscmfid;
    row_p.deptcode             := lmfsub;
    row_p.paybkaccount         := mktaccnt;
    row_p.paybkname            := mktbank;
    row_p.recebkaccount        := lsupaccntno;
    row_p.recebkname           := lsupbank;
    row_p.crc                  := '人民币';
    row_p.rate                 := 1;
    row_p.digest               := '收款';
    row_p.payoriginalmny       := row_ssc.Sscmoney;
    row_p.paylocalmny          := row_ssc.Sscmoney;
    row_p.billflag             := '0';
    row_p.sourcebillcode       := row_ssc.Sscbillno;
    row_p.iflag                := 'N';
    row_p.note                 := '';
    row_p.ts                   := to_char(sysdate, 'yyyy-mm-dd hh24:mi:ss');
    row_p.billcode             := null;
    row_p.prepaydate           := null;
    row_p.cashflowcode         := null;
    if lsupaccntno is null or lsupaccntno = '' then
      Raise_Application_Error(Errcode, '->09.供应商银行账号为空，请维护后进行收款!');
    end if;         
    insert into nc_temp_cashpay values row_p;         
       
  End;  
  

  --自动生成结算单
  Procedure Auto_GenerageSettle(i_mkt In Varchar2, i_date In Date) Is
    lpara      Varchar2(60);
    lisauto    Char(1);
    lgendate   Varchar2(10);
    lisgendate Char(1);
    lday       Number;
    Cursor c_genlist(vmkt Varchar2, vdate Number, vsettledate Date) Is
      Select CMCONTNO,
             CMSTATUS,
             CMTYPE,
             CMSUPID,
             CMWMID,
             CMTITLE,
             CMOBJECT,
             CMPPNAME,
             CMCATNAME,
             CMCATNUM,
             CMEFFDATE,
             CMLAPDATE,
             cmlastsetdate,
             CMMONEY,
             SBVC8
        From CONTMAIN, SUPPLIERBASE
       Where CMWMID <> '1'
         And CMSUPID = SBID
         And CMSTATUS In ('Y', 'Q')
         And CMJSMKT = vmkt
         And SBSTATUS = 'Y'
         And SBFLAG In ('0', '1', '2')
         And (cmlastsetdate Is Null Or
             (cmlastsetdate Is Not Null And cmlastsetdate < cmlapdate))
         And --未结算完结的合同
             cmeffdate <= vsettledate
         And --开始执行的合同才结算
             cmlapdate >= to_date('2011-04-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD')
         And --之前的历史合同不批量生成（已经处理完毕,避免处理迁移数据）
             (SBVC8 In (Select GSDID
                          From globsetday
                         Where gsdday1 = vdate
                            Or gsdday2 = vdate
                            Or gsdday3 = vdate
                            Or gsdday4 = vdate
                            Or gsdday5 = vdate) Or SBVC8 = '0')
       Order By cmwmid, cmcontno;
    row_genlist c_genlist%Rowtype;
    ljsbillno   Varchar2(20);
    Cursor c_sup(vmkt Varchar2, vsettledate Date) Is
      Select Distinct cmsupid, cmwmid, cmfmarket
        From contmain, contmanaframe
       Where cmcontno = cmfcontno
         And cmwmid <> '1'
         And cmjsmkt = vmkt
         And ((cmstatus = 'Y') Or (cmstatus In ('Q', 'N', 'S') And
             cmlapdate >= add_months(vsettledate, -6)))
       Order By cmsupid, cmwmid;
    row_sup      c_sup%Rowtype;
    lsettlesdate Date;
    lsettleedate Date;
  Begin
    currentdate    := fgeterpdate;
    currentmkt     := i_mkt;
    currentmkttype := fgetsystype(currentmkt);
    b_bdtype       := fgetprivatepara('MB');
    Begin
      lpara    := fgetprivatepara('MF');
      lisauto  := substr(lpara, 1, instr(lpara, ',') - 1);
      lgendate := substr(lpara, instr(lpara, ',') + 1);
      If to_number(substr(to_char(i_date, 'YYYYMMDD'), 7)) =
         to_number(lgendate) Then
        lisgendate := 'Y';
      Else
        lisgendate := 'N';
      End If;
    Exception
      When Others Then
        Return;
    End;
  
    If lisauto = 'Y' And lisgendate = 'Y' Then
      lsettlesdate := to_date(to_char(trunc(i_date, 'mm') - 1, 'YYYYMM') ||
                              lgendate,
                              'YYYYMMDD');
      lsettleedate := i_date - 1;
    
      If i_date - 1 = last_day(i_date - 1) Then
        lday := 0;
      Else
        lday := to_number(to_char(i_date - 1, 'DD'));
      End If;
      Open c_genlist(i_mkt, lday, i_date - 1);
      Loop
        Fetch c_genlist
          Into row_genlist;
        Exit When c_genlist%Notfound Or c_genlist%Notfound Is Null;
        Begin
          submit(row_genlist.cmsupid,
                 row_genlist.cmwmid,
                 row_genlist.cmcontno,
                 to_char(i_date - 1, 'YYYY-MM-DD'),
                 'System',
                 '0',
                 Null,
                 'Y',
                 'Y',
                 ljsbillno);
        Exception
          When Others Then
            sp_opererrors('自动生成结算单',
                          Sqlcode,
                          row_genlist.cmcontno || '-' || Sqlerrm);
        End;
      End Loop;
      Close c_genlist;
      --生成未结数据清单
      Open c_sup(i_mkt, i_date - 1);
      Loop
        Fetch c_sup
          Into row_sup;
        Exit When c_sup%Notfound Or c_sup%Notfound Is Null;
        Begin
          GenUnsettleData(lsettlesdate,
                          lsettleedate,
                          row_sup.cmfmarket, --发生门店
                          row_sup.cmsupid,
                          row_sup.cmwmid);
        Exception
          When Others Then
            sp_opererrors('生成未结算数据清单',
                          Sqlcode,
                          ljsbillno || '-' || Sqlerrm);
        End;
      End Loop;
      Close c_sup;
    End If;
    Commit;
  End;

  Procedure cmd_supsetcopytohq(p_billno   In Char,
                               p_person   In Char,
                               p_billid   In Char,
                               p_djlb     In Char,
                               p_adjustje Number,
                               p_sjfkje   Number,
                               p_thisye   Number) Is
  Begin
    Update supsettlehead
       Set sshadjustje = p_adjustje,
           sshsjfkje   = p_sjfkje,
           sshthisye   = p_thisye
     Where sshbillno = p_billno;
  
    If Sql%Rowcount = 1 Then
      approve(p_billno, p_person, p_billid, p_djlb);
    Else
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              p_billno || '->26.单据不存在或单据错误!');
    
    End If;
  
  End cmd_supsetcopytohq;

  Procedure cmd_supchargetohq(p_billno In Char,
                              p_num    In Number,
                              p_person In Char) Is
  Begin
    Update supsetcharge
       Set sscflag   = flagsended,
           auditor   = p_person,
           auditdate = fgeterpdate
     Where sscbillno = p_billno
       And sscrowno = p_num;
  
    /*IF currentmkttype <> stock.mf_hq THEN
      cmdsend.sp_cmdsend_target(cmdchargetohq,
                                currentmkt,
                                '0',
                                '''' || p_billno || ''',' || p_num,
                                NULL);
    END IF;*/
  
  End cmd_supchargetohq;

  Procedure cmd_supsetcptomkt(vuser    In Varchar2,
                              vdblink  In Varchar2,
                              p_billno In Char) --总部发送结算单到门店
   Is
    dest_cursor Integer;
    rowp        Integer;
    tab_charge  Varchar2(100); --结算费用
    tab_head    Varchar2(100); --结算单
    tab_detail  Varchar2(100); --结算明细
    l_stmt      dbms_sql.varchar2s;
    /*结算数据传送涉及表 supsettlehead(表头) supsettledet(明细) supsetcharge(费用)
    采用先删除后插入的方式实现*/
  
  Begin
    --Delete SUPSETCHARGE 删除费用
    tab_charge := vuser || 'supsetcharge' || vdblink;
    Begin
      l_stmt.DELETE;
      l_stmt(1) := 'BEGIN';
      l_stmt(2) := '  Delete From supsetcharge';
      l_stmt(3) := '    Where (sscbillno,sscrowno) In';
      l_stmt(4) := '             (Select sscbillno,sscrowno';
      l_stmt(5) := '                From ' || tab_charge;
      l_stmt(6) := '               Where sscjsno=''' || p_billno || ''');';
      l_stmt(7) := 'END;';
      dest_cursor := dbms_sql.open_cursor;
      dbms_sql.parse(dest_cursor,
                     l_stmt,
                     l_stmt.FIRST,
                     l_stmt.LAST,
                     True,
                     dbms_sql.v7);
      rowp := dbms_sql.EXECUTE(dest_cursor);
      If dbms_sql.is_open(dest_cursor) Then
        dbms_sql.close_cursor(dest_cursor);
      End If;
    
    End;
  
    --Delete SUPSETTLEHEAD  删除结算单(头)  明细由触发器删除
    tab_head := vuser || 'supsettlehead' || vdblink;
    Begin
      l_stmt.DELETE;
      l_stmt(1) := 'BEGIN';
      l_stmt(2) := '  Delete From supsettlehead';
      l_stmt(3) := '   Where sshbillno=''' || p_billno || ''';';
      l_stmt(4) := 'END;';
      dest_cursor := dbms_sql.open_cursor;
      dbms_sql.parse(dest_cursor,
                     l_stmt,
                     l_stmt.FIRST,
                     l_stmt.LAST,
                     True,
                     dbms_sql.v7);
      rowp := dbms_sql.EXECUTE(dest_cursor);
      If dbms_sql.is_open(dest_cursor) Then
        dbms_sql.close_cursor(dest_cursor);
      End If;
    
    End;
  
    --Insert SUPSETTLEHEAD
    Begin
      l_stmt.DELETE;
      l_stmt(1) := 'BEGIN';
      l_stmt(2) := '  Insert Into supsettlehead';
      l_stmt(3) := '  Select * From ' || tab_head || ' Where sshbillno=''' ||
                   p_billno || ''';';
      l_stmt(4) := 'END;';
      dest_cursor := dbms_sql.open_cursor;
      dbms_sql.parse(dest_cursor,
                     l_stmt,
                     l_stmt.FIRST,
                     l_stmt.LAST,
                     True,
                     dbms_sql.v7);
      rowp := dbms_sql.EXECUTE(dest_cursor);
      If dbms_sql.is_open(dest_cursor) Then
        dbms_sql.close_cursor(dest_cursor);
      End If;
    
    End;
  
    --Insert SUPSETTLEDETAIL
    tab_detail := vuser || 'supsettledet' || vdblink;
    Begin
      l_stmt.DELETE;
      l_stmt(1) := 'BEGIN';
      l_stmt(2) := 'Insert Into supsettledet';
      l_stmt(3) := 'Select * From ' || tab_detail || ' Where ssdbillno=''' ||
                   p_billno || ''';';
      l_stmt(4) := 'END;';
      dest_cursor := dbms_sql.open_cursor;
      dbms_sql.parse(dest_cursor,
                     l_stmt,
                     l_stmt.FIRST,
                     l_stmt.LAST,
                     True,
                     dbms_sql.v7);
      rowp := dbms_sql.EXECUTE(dest_cursor);
      If dbms_sql.is_open(dest_cursor) Then
        dbms_sql.close_cursor(dest_cursor);
      End If;
    
    End;
  
    --Insert SUPSETCHARGE
    Begin
      l_stmt.DELETE;
      l_stmt(1) := 'BEGIN';
      l_stmt(2) := 'Insert Into supsetcharge';
      l_stmt(3) := 'Select * From ' || tab_charge || ' Where sscjsno=''' ||
                   p_billno || ''';';
      l_stmt(4) := 'END;';
      dest_cursor := dbms_sql.open_cursor;
      dbms_sql.parse(dest_cursor,
                     l_stmt,
                     l_stmt.FIRST,
                     l_stmt.LAST,
                     True,
                     dbms_sql.v7);
      rowp := dbms_sql.EXECUTE(dest_cursor);
      If dbms_sql.is_open(dest_cursor) Then
        dbms_sql.close_cursor(dest_cursor);
      End If;
    
    End;
  
    Commit;
  Exception
    When Others Then
      If dbms_sql.is_open(dest_cursor) Then
        dbms_sql.close_cursor(dest_cursor);
      End If;
    
      Rollback;
      raise_application_error(errcode,
                              '->30.执行settlesup.cmd_supsetcptomkt错误，结算单未发送--' ||
                              p_billno);
    
  End cmd_supsetcptomkt;

Begin
  currentdate      := fgeterpdate;
  currentmkt       := fgetsysplace;
  currentmkttype   := fgetsystype(currentmkt);
  b_bdtype         := fgetprivatepara('MB');
  ChargeDeductMode := fGetPrivatePara('MG');
  AdjQsChargeId    := fgetprivatepara('MK');
End settlesup;
